# CLAUDE.md вАФ BLOOM project agent context

This file is the contract between the project and any AI agent working on it. Read it at the start of every session. Update it whenever the project changes вАФ see [Living docs rule](#living-docs-rule) at the bottom.

The human-facing description lives in [README.md](README.md). This file focuses on what an AI needs to continue work without re-reading the entire codebase.

---

## рЯЧЇпЄП Retention Stages Tracker (May 2026, updated 2026-05-23)

Quick-scan map of the addiction-loop work. **Update this table whenever a stage ships.** Detailed change-log entries live in ¬І11 below.

> рЯФН **AUDIT 2026-05-31 вАФ full addiction audit** (132-agent scan, 110 bugs checked / 63 confirmed + live-server browser evidence). Two deliverables: [BLOOM_ADDICTION_AUDIT.md](BLOOM_ADDICTION_AUDIT.md) (per-category scores, overall **6.5/10**, 63-bug table, "what's missing" diagnosis) + [tasks/ACTIVE/ADDICTION_TASKS.md](tasks/ACTIVE/ADDICTION_TASKS.md) (45 addiction-ranked tasks + 8 fix-first bugs). **Headline finding: the world looks EMPTY** (`activeNow:0`, bots not default-on, Daily Special points to an empty board, push effectively dead) вАФ fixing aliveness + focus is the #1 ROI.

| **AD.1** | **8 fix-first bugs.** (1) `_finalizeGuildWar` ROLLBACK вАФ the only un-guarded txn, was poisoning pool connections ([server.js](server.js)); (2) **Daily Special empty-board fix** вАФ `_boardIsMeaningful` filter in `pickDailySpecial` + a real `themed` branch in `validateBoardDefinition` reject empty themed boards so the flagship daily hook never lands on a practice-looking board (**verified live: now returns the real gold board #2, was the empty board #3**); (3) centralized Express error-middleware (structured JSON 500, no stack leak); (4) toast `bottom:32px`вЖТ`calc(90px+safe-area)` so it clears the bottom-nav on iOS ([src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js)); (5) **lives widget true root cause** вАФ `window._livesCache` was never assigned (local var only) so the вЭ§пЄП balance slot could never read it; now exposed + repaints after fetch ([src/20-lives.js](src/20-lives.js)); (6) live-race result shows the REAL wager payout (`winnerReward`/`wager` from live-state settle) not a hardcoded +50, tie shows refund ([server.js](server.js)+[src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)); (7) live-race вЬХ forfeit button + `POST /api/duels/:id/forfeit-live` (settles immediately, honest who's-ahead-now) so players aren't locked 60s (**verified live: endpoint returns 400 not 404**); (8) contest-share Safari fallback copies the LINK + legacy execCommand ([src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js)). Commits c4aca97 / 6ca7a44 / 0703d03. |
| **AD.2 / AD.2.1** | **Auto-fleet вАФ world never empty** в≠Р (the #1 ranked task). Bots previously ran only if an admin manually pressed Start; after any deploy the world reverted to `activeNow:0`. Now an always-on AUTO fleet starts at boot вАФ `_desiredBotFleet()` reconciler ([server.js](server.js) ~18459) prefers a manual fleet (`__bot_engine_state`) else the auto fleet (default ON, `mode=daily` вЖТ bots heartbeat for live-stats AND seed the daily world leaderboard). `startBotsIfLeader` reconciles actual-vs-desired every 5s so toggling takes effect live. **Verified live: `activeNow` 0вЖТ6.** FULL admin control (prime directive): `bots_auto_enabled`/`bots_auto_count`/`bots_auto_mode` + `bots_games_today_floor` seeded in [schema.sql](schema.sql)+[db.js](db.js) with TIPS+PRESETS in the admin config editor; new **рЯМН „Ю„Ь„Р „Ґ„Х„Ь„Э** button + `POST /api/bots/fill-world`; `/api/bots/stop` now also sets `bots_auto_enabled=false` so "stop" truly stops (the reconciler respects it). Commits 15c81ab / 1ff5358 / e444e4c. |
| **AD.2.2** | **Stats credibility clamp.** The auto-fleet exposed a latent bug: `/api/stats/live` blended bots into `gamesToday` (√Чmultiplier cap) but returned `gamesThisWeek` raw, so a busy bot day showed "298 today / 278 this week" вАФ impossible. Now `gamesThisWeek = max(rawWeek, blendedToday)`. **Verified live: 299/299.** Commit 06ffe17. |
| **AD.3** | **Audit #18 was a FALSE POSITIVE** вАФ the game-over replay-share button already pulses via `replayShareBtnPulse` ([public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css):7228); no change needed. Logged so it isn't re-attempted. **Process lesson: the audit's quoted code strings frequently did NOT match the real code вАФ always Read current code before acting on an audit claim.** Commit 2ee167b. |
| **AD.4** | **Live "moves to survive" danger meter** (ranked task #13). Turns danger mode from a passive red wash into a tactical loss-aversion puzzle вАФ the biggest "one more drop" lever. When the grid has вЙ§3 playable empty cells, a red pill above the grid shows the count (`рЯЪ® 2 „™„Р„Щ„Э` / `рЯЪ® „™„Р „Р„Ч„®„Х„Я!` pulsing red at 1). `paintDangerMeter()` ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) repaints on every `updateDangerMode` call (before the no-change early-return) so it stays live as the player merges; torn down on init + game-over. CSS `.danger-meter` pill in [public/css/base.css](public/css/base.css) (respects `prefers-reduced-motion`). Admin-controllable: `danger_meter_enabled` seeded in [schema.sql](schema.sql)+[db.js](db.js) with TIP+PRESET (default on; **verified live: key=true, build v20260531d**). Commit a963f53. |
| **AD.5** | **Win-return celebration on home** (ranked task #8). Extends the victory dopamine: when the player lands on home right after a winning game (new personal best, or score вЙ• threshold), fires confetti + milestone sound + a brief gold `рЯОЙ „†„Щ„¶„Ч„™!` / `рЯОЙ „©„Щ„Р „Ч„У„©!` banner вАФ Candy-Crush pattern that pulls "play again". `maybeWinReturnCelebration()` ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js)) reads the last-game snapshot (`window.__bloomLoadLastGame`, 30-min TTL), fires once per game (sessionStorage guard on gameId) within 15s of game end. `showConfetti` exposed as `window.__bloomConfetti` from [src/14-events.js](src/14-events.js) (home is a separate IIFE). CSS `.home-win-banner` in [public/css/base.css](public/css/base.css) (respects `prefers-reduced-motion`). Commit fd0d9c1. |
| **AD.6** | **"Next daily rewards in HH:MM:SS" countdown on game-over** (ranked task #3). Gives every non-duel game-over a concrete return-time hook вАФ the strongest "come back at a specific time" lever in F2P. A gold pill `рЯОБ „Ф„§„®„°„Щ„Э „Ф„Щ„Х„Ю„Щ„Щ„Э „Ф„С„Р„Щ„Э „С„Ґ„Х„У HH:MM:SS` anchored to Israel midnight (when spin + login-cal + daily-deal + daily-special all reset). Skipped in daily mode (the existing daily countdown already shows). | **AD.7** | **Daily auto-tournament scheduler** (ranked task #6). A scheduled prime-time event the player plans their evening around (Coin Master / Royal Match pattern) вАФ the strongest "show up at a specific time" lever. `ensureDailyTournament()` ([server.js](server.js), modeled on `ensureWeeklyContest`) creates ONE tournament per Israel-day with a top-3 prize pool (default 20:00вЖТ22:00, 1000/500/250рЯТО), date-tagged name for dedup, runs at boot+20s then hourly. Reuses the shipped `maybeFinalizeTournament` (payout + winner push) + `GET /api/tournaments` (surfaces scheduledвЖТlive by timestamp). Admin-controllable: `daily_tournament_enabled/name/start_hour/end_hour/prize_1/2/3` seeded in [schema.sql](schema.sql)+[db.js](db.js) with 7 TIPS+PRESETS. **Verified live: created "рЯПЖ „Ш„Х„®„†„Щ„® „Ф„Ґ„®„С ¬Ј 2026-05-31" (upcoming, prizes 1000/500/250).** Commits 74bc75a, a2d9f47 (schema dedup).
| **AD.8** | **Player moderation** (ranked task #15 вАФ "admin controls everything" prime directive). The admin player drill-down had only export+delete; no way to ban a cheater or grant rewards. New `player_profiles.banned/banned_at/banned_reason` ([schema.sql](schema.sql)+[db.js](db.js)). Server: an in-memory `bannedDevices` Set (loaded at boot, refreshed every 60s, mutated instantly on ban/unban) so `requireDeviceAuth` rejects a banned device with 403 `banned` at **zero per-request DB cost** ([server.js](server.js)); new action-switched `POST /<ADMIN>/api/players/moderate` (ban/unban/grant_trophies/grant_xp/set_level вАФ grant_trophies upserts `player_trophies`); `GET /<ADMIN>/api/player/:id` now also returns the profile + moderation state. Admin UI: moderation panel atop `viewPlayer` ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)) with profile chips + ban/unban (reason prompt) + grant gems/trophies/XP + set-level buttons, all audit-logged. Server-only (no client build). node --check clean; deploy healthy. Commit 3d2f0c1. |
| **AD.9** | **Economy faucet-vs-sink dashboard** (ranked task #16). No per-source ledger exists, so the dashboard is the aggregate gem picture. New `GET /<ADMIN>/api/economy` ([server.js](server.js)) returns total faucet (SUM `total_earned`) vs sink (SUM `total_spent`) vs float (wallets + `gem_bank`), a **sink-ratio health metric**, active-player (7d) economy, and top-20 earners/spenders/hoarders. Admin UI ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): a "рЯУК „С„®„Ц „Ю„Х„Ь „С„Х„®" panel in the рЯТ∞ „Ы„Ь„Ы„Ь„Ф tab вАФ 4 KPI cards (green-amber-red sink-ratio, healthy вЙИ40-70%) + active-7d line + 3 top-20 tables. Lets the owner tune the gem economy for spend-pressure (low sink-ratio = hoarding = weaker gem-chase loop). Server-only + static HTML; node --check clean; deploy healthy. Commits 9c1d8f3 (endpoint), e4d7a2b (UI). |

| **37** | **Guild Wars** рЯЫ°вЪФпЄП | Clash Royale pattern вАФ clan-vs-clan weekly competition. Boosted guild retention 3-5x at Supercell's launch. Auto-matchmaker runs every 6h, pairs eligible guilds (3+ members, no active war) by power level. 7-day war period. Every member's game score contributes to their guild's war pool via the existing `/guilds/contribute` endpoint (zero client wiring вАФ extended server-side). End of war: lazy-finalize on next state read вЖТ winner gets 500рЯТО/member + push notification, loser gets 100рЯТО/member consolation. Min 1 game played to claim. Home tile (purple gradient вЖТ gold when reward unclaimed) only mounts when in-guild + has active war OR unclaimed reward. Modal: VS card with both teams' scores + progress bar + countdown, top-10 contributors leaderboard, my-contribution stats. Atomic gem credit + claim-dedup transaction. |
| **38** | **Trophy Road** рЯПЖ | The #1 retention mechanism in mobile games (Clash Royale, Brawl Stars). Unlike League/BP, **trophies can GO DOWN**. Win (вЙ•500 score) = +15рЯПЖ (+40 crown / +25 PB bonus). Lose (<100 score) = вИТ8рЯПЖ. New-player protection: under 50рЯПЖ = no loss. Safe floor at 0. 8 visual arenas (рЯМ± sprout вЖТ вЪ° legend at 12000) + 10 admin-tunable gem milestones (50вЖТ15000рЯТО). Atomic server transaction with per-game dedup. Game-over hook fires automatically with score+tier+isNewBest вЖТ server returns delta + arena change. Client renders trophy toast (+15рЯПЖ fly-in) + full-screen arena-promotion overlay when crossing arena boundary. Home tile in dark-blueвЖТgold gradient with breathing pulse when milestone unclaimed. |
| **39** | **UX Polish + Addiction Maximizer** рЯОѓ | Three-part polish after 38 stages of features. (1) **Priority Calmer** вАФ 156 infinite animations on one page = visual chaos; new module ranks all home tiles by addiction priority (streak-danger=100, trophy-claim=90, spin=70, etc.), only the HIGHEST tile pulses, rest get `.polish-calmed` (desaturated, paused, dimmed). The eye is drawn to ONE thing вЖТ focus drives action. (2) **First-visit Micro-tutorials** вАФ small gold balloon next to each NEW tile with 1-sentence explanation, dismisses on click or 8s. Per-tile dedup via localStorage. Only ONE tooltip at a time to avoid overload. (3) **Admin Engagement Overview** вАФ quick-stats card at top of dashboard tab with click-to-jump to each addiction system (Trophy/Spin/Guild Wars/Rivalries). Solves "where is X feature?" pain. |

| **FD.2** | **Social + Identity Overhaul (May 29 2026)** рЯ§Э | Four retention-critical fixes in one wave. **(1) Referral-leak fix** вАФ the home invite buttons ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js) `whatsappInviteV2()` + the v1 home invite at [src/05-home.js](src/05-home.js)) were using `window.location.origin + pathname` for the WhatsApp invite text вАФ bare URL, no `?ref=BLOOM-XXXX`. The universal `buildShareUrl('/')` helper exists exactly for this. Without the ref, every invite sent from home was a K-factor leak вАФ recipients joined but the `/api/referral` attribution never fired, no signup bonus, no push-back-to-referrer. Both buttons now funnel through `window.__bloomBuildShareUrl`. **(2) Bottom-nav iOS Safari stability** ([public/css/bottom-nav.css](public/css/bottom-nav.css)) вАФ players reported the bar "scrolls with content and disappears". Root cause: iOS Safari interacted badly with `backdrop-filter:blur` + the dynamic-viewport resolution of `bottom:0; padding-bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom)`. Fix: anchor via `bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px)` directly (no extra padding), then force a dedicated compositor layer with `transform: translate3d(0,0,0); will-change: transform; backface-visibility: hidden;`. Standard iOS Safari fixed-position hardening вАФ bar now stays glued to viewport on every scroll. **(3) Friend Search + Requests** вАФ full Clash-Royale-style social system on top of the existing instant-friendship `/api/friends/invite`. New schema: `friend_requests` table (PK id, from_device, to_device, status enum [pending/accepted/declined/canceled], message, timestamps; partial UNIQUE INDEX on `(from, to) WHERE status='pending'` so re-tap is no-op). New endpoints: `GET /api/users/search` (ILIKE on `display_name` + LIKE on `player_code`, returns top-N with per-row `alreadyFriends/requestSent/requestReceived` flags), `POST /api/friends/request-send` (anti-spam caps: 50 pending, 50 total friends; auto-accepts if the other side already requested you), `GET /api/friends/requests` (incoming + outgoing + 14-day history + unread count), `POST /api/friends/request-respond` (accept/decline/cancel with atomic friendship+200рЯТО bonus transaction). Client ([src/49-friend-search.js](src/49-friend-search.js)) вАФ 2-tab modal (рЯФН „Ч„Щ„§„Х„© / рЯУ® „С„І„©„Х„™) with red unread-badge on the requests tab. Search has 280ms debounce, returns user cards with role-appropriate action buttons ("вЮХ „Ф„Х„°„£" / "вП≥ „Ю„Ю„™„Щ„Я" / "рЯ§Э „Р„©„®" / "вЬУ „Ч„С„®"). Auto-opens to рЯУ® „С„І„©„Х„™ tab when URL is `?action=friend-requests` (push deep-link). Entry point: new "рЯФН „Ч„§„© „©„Ч„І„†„Щ„Э + рЯУ® „С„І„©„Х„™ „Ч„С„®„Х„™" button at the top of the existing dyn-friends modal. **(4) Cross-device Account Sync** вАФ THE BIGGEST mobile-web retention killer fixed. Until now Safari + Chrome on the same phone created two separate identities; every browser switch lost streak/trophies/friends/balance. New schema: `device_transfer_codes` (6-char code PK from 32-char alphabet skipping I/L/O/0/1, source_device_id, 10-min TTL, single-use atomic redeem). New endpoints: `POST /api/account/transfer-create` (requires auth вАФ only the real owner can issue a transfer) + `POST /api/account/transfer-redeem` (the 6-char code IS the auth on the redeem side; returns source device's id+HMAC token). Client ([src/48-device-sync.js](src/48-device-sync.js)) вАФ purple-gold modal with 2 tabs (рЯУ§ „¶„Х„® „І„Х„У with live MM:SS countdown ticker + рЯУ• „Ф„Ы„†„° „І„Х„У with destructive-action confirm dialog). On successful redeem, client overwrites `bloom_device_id` + `bloom_device_token` in localStorage, clears identity-bound caches, reloads the page вЖТ both browsers are now the same logical player. Entry point: new "рЯФЧ „°„†„Ы„®„Я" pill on the PID strip ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js)), purple gradient distinct from "рЯС§ profile" and "рЯС• referrals". Anti-abuse: source must be authenticated when creating (5/hr cap); 20/hr per-IP cap on redeem. **Why this works**: industry F2P data вАФ cross-device retention drives D30 by 40-60% on mobile-web titles. Players who can carry their identity across browsers feel committed; those who lose progress feel cheated and uninstall. The social request system adds Clash-Royale's "accept friend = +200рЯТО toast" emotion вЖТ social-debt loop. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,722 drops / 8,640 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529d`, SW `bloom-v20.4`. |
| **FD.1** | **Feature Discovery Map (May 29 2026)** рЯЧЇ | After 48+ shipped retention stages BLOOM has 40+ features behind progressive-unlock gates (T1.1+T1.4). | **BL.1** | **Bot social-proof + auto-fallback for duels (May 29 2026)** рЯ§ЦвЪФпЄП | Two coordinated retention levers вАФ "never feel alone" вАФ that close two distinct cold-start gaps. **(1) Live-stats blending** ([server.js](server.js) `/api/stats/live`): bot heartbeats from `player_heartbeat` (filtered to `device_id LIKE 'bot-%'`) are now counted alongside real `contest_live_state` + `device_visits` rows. Capped at `real √Ч bots_live_stats_max_multiplier` (default 2.5) so the ratio stays believable вАФ when 4 real players are active, the bar shows up to 10; when 0 real are active, shows at least `bots_live_stats_floor_when_zero_real` (default 6). `activeNow`, `playingNow`, and `activeThisHour` all get the same blend. Master toggle `bots_in_live_stats_enabled` (default `'true'`). The bar never reads "1 „©„Ч„І„Я „§„Ґ„Щ„Ь" during quiet hours вАФ industry data names this the single biggest D1-retention killer in F2P. **(2) Auto-bot duel fallback** ([server.js](server.js) `/api/duels/find-random` + `/api/duels/find-random-live`): after 8s of no real opponent (live race: 6s), server spawns a phantom bot opponent and returns it as if matchmaking succeeded. Bot looks identical to a real player from the client вАФ random Israeli name from a 70-entry pool, valid `BLOOM-XXXX` code via `generatePlayerCode()`, trophy count in the matchmaking range, full `player_profiles` + `player_trophies` rows seeded for downstream JOIN consistency. New helper `_spawnBotDuelForPlayer({deviceId, myName, myCode, myTrophies, difficulty, range, live, durationSec})` is the single insertion point вАФ atomic INSERT into `duels` with `is_random_match=TRUE, is_bot_match=TRUE, status='accepted'`; adds `is_live=TRUE + started_at + duration_seconds` when called from the live path. **(3) Async bot-score settler**: when player submits via `POST /api/duels/:id/score`, server detects `is_bot_match=TRUE`, stamps `bot_settle_at = NOW() + random(20-55)s` (admin-tunable), returns `result: 'waiting'` so player sees the normal waiting overlay. Two settle paths: (a) periodic ticker every 10s scans for elapsed `bot_settle_at`, (b) lazy-settle inline inside `GET /api/duels/:id` when polling player catches the timer expiry. Either way `_settleBotDuel(duelId)` runs: atomic transaction locks the row, computes `botScore = _calibrateBotScore(playerScore, playerWinPct)`, writes `opponent_score + winner_device + status='settled'/'tie'`, fires push to player. **(4) Score calibration** вАФ `_calibrateBotScore`: 52% chance bot scores LESS than player (admin-tunable `bot_duel_player_win_rate_pct`, default 52 вЖТ "player feels slightly favored"). Delta distribution: 65% within 3-13% (most games close вЖТ feel real), 25% within 10-25% (clear win/loss), 10% in the 25-40% tail (occasional blowout) + 2% ties. Result: ~52% player wins / ~46% bot wins / ~2% ties вАФ Royal Match / Coin Master industry standard. **(5) Live bot-duel score curve** вАФ live 60s race: bot score computed on-the-fly via `_liveBotScoreAt(duelId, startedAtMs, durationSec, nowMs)`. Deterministic per duel_id (seeded PRNG вЖТ `target = 35K-110K`), `score = target √Ч sqrt(elapsed/duration) √Ч noise` вАФ sqrt easing lets bots ramp up quickly then plateau, so a strong player can pass them late (dramatic comebacks). `live-heartbeat` writes computed score to `opponent_live_score` (`GREATEST` guard so it never decreases); `live-state` also overlays computed score for smoother HUD; `_settleLiveDuel` recomputes final bot score so player-abandonment doesn't lock in a stale low number. **(6) Admin telemetry** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html) рЯС• „©„Ч„І„†„Щ„Э tab + `/admin/api/bot-duels/stats`): new `вЪФпЄП „У„Х-„І„®„С„Х„™ „Ю„Х„Ь „С„Х„Ш„Щ„Э` section with 3 stat rows (24h vs all-time vs averages) вАФ player-win % color-coded (green 48-56% = healthy, orange 42-60% = borderline, red = needs tuning), plus a 30-row recent-duels table with result badges (рЯПЖ „©„Ч„І„Я / рЯ§Ц „С„Х„Ш / рЯ§Э „™„Щ„І„Х / вМЫ „§„Т / вП≥ „§„Ґ„Щ„Ь). Auto-refreshes every 15s while tab is open. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): 2 new `duels` columns (`is_bot_match BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE`, `bot_settle_at TIMESTAMPTZ`) + partial index `idx_duels_bot_settle` for cheap settler scans. 9 new `game_config` keys cover every tunable. **Decoupled from bot-engine.js** вАФ those bots actively pump heartbeats for the social-proof stat; these are phantom opponents created on demand. Each bot duel = one row, one short-lived `player_profiles` placeholder, no recurring activity. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,030 drops / 8,935 merges / 0 floating tiles). |

| **BL.1.3** | **Bot-duel monotonicity + test harness (May 29 2026)** рЯ§ЦвЪФпЄПрЯФђ | Second live test showed the bot's score in the **spectator widget** still oscillated up AND down between 1.5s polls вАФ even after BL.1.2 fixed the duel-HUD ticker. Root cause: `_synthesizeBotLiveState` (server-side) and `_liveBotScoreAt` both had `sin()` noise factors that swung negative between polls вЖТ displayed score decreased. Also `_calibrateBotScore` used `Math.random()` so the live preview never matched the eventual settled value вАФ a calibration jump on settle that could LOWER the score visibly (regression). Three coordinated changes + a test harness. **Fix 1 вАФ deterministic calibration** ([server.js](server.js)): new `_seededBotRng(seed)` Mulberry32 PRNG; `_calibrateBotScore(duelId, playerScore, playerWinPct)` now takes `duelId` and seeds the PRNG from it. Same inputs вЖТ same output, every time. Live preview and final settle produce identical numbers. **Fix 2 вАФ strictly monotonic live score** ([server.js](server.js)): `_liveBotScoreAt` dropped the `sin*0.02` noise factor. Now `target √Ч sqrt(elapsed/duration)` вАФ strictly non-decreasing in `nowMs`. **Fix 3 вАФ DB-enforced monotonic ceiling** ([server.js](server.js)): `_synthesizeBotLiveState` was rewritten with a new pure `_botAsyncCandidateScore` helper. After computing the candidate, the function runs `UPDATE duels SET opponent_live_score = GREATEST(COALESCE(opponent_live_score, 0), $1) RETURNING opponent_live_score` вАФ the existing `opponent_live_score` column (originally for live races) is repurposed as a monotonic ceiling. Even if the candidate formula has a discontinuity (e.g. when player submits and target switches from estimate to calibrated final), the displayed score NEVER decreases вАФ the GREATEST guard preserves the highest value ever computed. Atomic + concurrency-safe. **Test harness** ([scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs](scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs)) вАФ duplicates the four formulas (in sync with server.js) and runs 6 assertions across **thousands of synthetic ticks**: (1) determinism вАФ 50 duels √Ч 4 player scores √Ч 3 calls each, every triple must match; (2) win-rate distribution вАФ 10,000 simulated calibrations, player wins must fall in 48-56%; (3) live monotonicity вАФ 200 duels √Ч 1801 ticks (50ms each), no down-jumps allowed; (4) async monotonicity within anchor вАФ 200 duels √Ч 2502 ticks; (5) full poll lifecycle with DB ceiling вАФ 500 duels √Ч 68 polls each, simulates the GREATEST guard, **0 down-jumps**; (6) settled-matches-preview вАФ preview === actual for 100 duels. **Test run 5√Ч** вАФ all 5 runs produced **identical numbers** (51.5% / 46.4% / 2.1%), all 6 tests pass each run, zero down-jumps total. The deterministic seeding is what enables this consistency. **Why this matters**: the waiting-overlay spectator widget is the highest-emotion moment in any duel вАФ a bot whose displayed score visibly drops while the player watches is the loudest possible "this is fake" signal. With DB-enforced monotonicity + deterministic calibration, the bot's score becomes indistinguishable from a real player's. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,931 drops / 8,827 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529g`, SW `bloom-v20.7`. |

When a tier changes, fires one of three keyframes: `dspecAppear` (scale-up + fade from 0; tile dropped from empty), `dspecMerge` (scale 1.28 + gold drop-shadow brightness boost; existing tile upgraded), `dspecClear` (shrink + fade-out; tile vanished). Rewritten to seed on `(duelId XOR bucket)` where `bucket = floor(score / 600)` (roughly one merge event per bucket). Result: the bot's grid evolves smoothly over the game, ~50 distinct layouts per duel by score 30K. Also: `fillBase` now scales with score (1 cell/col at low scores, 3 cells/col at 50K+) so the board "fills up" over time like a real game. **Verification** ([scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs](scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs)) вАФ 2 new tests added: (6a) grid deterministic per (duelId, score), (6b) grid evolves вЙ•10 changes across 30K range. **Result: 50.0 average grid changes per duel, 30/30 duels evolve well above threshold.** All 8 tests pass √Ч 3 runs each, IDENTICAL results (51.5% / 46.4% / 2.1% player/bot/tie). Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,009 drops / 8,968 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529h`, SW `bloom-v20.8`. |
| **BL.1.5** | **Bot plays the SAME GAME вАФ real trajectory simulation (May 29 2026)** рЯ§ЦрЯОЃвЪ° | User caught the lie: the bot's spectator grid was "different shapes every second" вАФ random configurations, not actual gameplay. Same engine the real game uses вЖТ bot's moves look identical to a real player's. **Fix 2 вАФ `_simulateBotDuelTrajectory(seed, weights, durationSec)`**: runs the engine forward for the full game duration, taking 1 snapshot per drop (~33 snapshots in 60s, ~50 in 90s). **Crucially uses the duel's `board_seed` + `difficulty_weights`** вАФ so the bot plays the SAME piece distribution + speed as the player. Hell difficulty вЖТ bot also gets weighted 3-7 pieces. Easy вЖТ tier 1-2 dominant. Returns `{snapshots: [{t, s, h, g}], finalScore, finalGrid, finalTier}`. Verified: 1-3ms execution, deterministic per seed (same input вЖТ identical output), Hell hits tier 8, Easy tier 5, Default tier 6 вАФ confirms difficulty is honored. **Fix 3 вАФ `bot_trajectory JSONB` column + `_getOrComputeBotTrajectory(duel)` cache** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js) + [server.js](server.js)): trajectory computed on first spectator poll, stored on the duel row, ~4KB per duel. Subsequent polls hit the cache, zero CPU. **Fix 4 вАФ `_synthesizeBotLiveState` snapshot lookup by PROGRESS** ([server.js](server.js)): the live displayed bot score follows the existing monotonic calibrated curve (BL.1.3 ceiling guard). The GRID is now selected from the trajectory by `progress = displayed_score / target_final`. New helper `_snapshotForProgress(traj, ratio)` returns `snapshots[floor(ratio √Ч (n-1))]`. Result: as the bot's displayed score grows from 0 вЖТ calibrated final, the player sees the bot's REAL board evolve through ~30-50 actual gameplay snapshots. Tiles drop, merge, upgrade naturally. Target denominator picks correctly per duel mode: live race вЖТ `_liveBotTargetScore`, async post-submit вЖТ calibrated final (matches settle), async pre-submit вЖТ 40K estimate. Response now also includes `timeLeftMs`, `status`, `difficulty`, `isLive`. **Fix 5 вАФ spectator widget red theme + countdown** ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) `injectDuelSpectatorWidget` + `pollDuelLiveState` + inline CSS): new countdown row at the TOP of the widget in red-gold gradient вАФ "вП∞ „†„©„Р„®„Х „Ь„Щ„®„Щ„С 23 „©„†„Щ„Х„™" вАФ adapts label per duel type (live: "„†„©„Р„®„Х „Ь„Щ„®„Щ„С", async: "„Ю„Т„Щ„© „С„Ґ„Х„У"). Header text changes to "вЪ° „¶„Х„§„Ф „С„І„®„С „Ч„Щ" for live duels (distinct from regular "„¶„Х„§„Ф „С-X „Ч„Щ"). In last 10 seconds: red pulsing border via `dspecCountdownPulse` 0.6s keyframe. Opponent score gets a `dspecScoreBump` cubic-bezier animation when it grows. Cell change animations from BL.1.4 still apply. **Why this is "the right architecture"**: every previous attempt (BL.1.0-BL.1.4) tried to simulate the bot's appearance via randomized synthesis. The bot was always a Potemkin village вАФ looked plausible at first glance but broke under scrutiny ("the tiles don't move like a real game"). BL.1.5 makes the bot actually PLAY THE GAME вАФ same merge engine, same seed, same difficulty. The grid the player sees IS the bot's real board at that moment. The lie disappears because there is no lie. **The score-calibration / visual-decoupling**: trajectory provides the GRID (real), `_calibrateBotScore` provides the SCORE (controlled). Both are deterministic per (duelId, playerScore) so they're consistent across reads. The natural simulation final and the calibrated final aren't the same number, but they're decoupled вАФ natural is metadata, calibrated is what player sees. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,887 drops / 8,774 merges / 0 floating tiles). All 8 bot-score tests pass √Ч 3 runs identical. Cache buster `v20260529i`, SW `bloom-v20.9`. |
| **BL.1.6** | **Bot-duel score-credibility fixes + active-stats coverage (May 29 2026)** рЯ§ЦрЯТѓрЯУК | User reported the most-credibility-breaking bug yet: "bot leads with 17K mid-game then ends with 9K final + player wins" вАФ the live displayed score JUMPED DOWN to the settled score. Plus: bot opponents in random matches don't update the home page's "players today" stats. **Four coordinated fixes + a critical regression test.** **Fix 1 вАФ `_botAsyncCandidateScore` pre-submit anchor 40000 вЖТ 8000** ([server.js](server.js)): the high anchor caused the live ceiling to grow into the 25-35K range during the player's game; when player submitted with (e.g.) 5000, the calibrated final was ~4500 вАФ a visible drop of ~30K at settle. With anchor=8000, pre-submit ceiling tops out at ~6-7K (matching a "warming up" bot), so when calibrated comes in (typically much higher), the live score climbs UP toward it вАФ no regression possible from this path. **Fix 2 вАФ `_liveBotScoreAt` easing sqrt вЖТ quadratic** ([server.js](server.js)): sqrt easing means at t=2s/60s the bot showed `target √Ч sqrt(2/60) = target √Ч 0.182` вАФ already at 6.4K if target=35K, before the player even completed their first merge. Quadratic (`ratio¬≤`) gives `target √Ч 0.001` = 35 points at the same moment вАФ matches a real player's first-tile pace. Curve still reaches full target at t=duration, just back-loaded toward dramatic finish. New test confirms avg bot score at t=2s is **80 points** (was 6000+). **Fix 3 вАФ `_settleBotDuel`: `bot_score = MAX(calibrated, opponent_live_score)`** ([server.js](server.js)): the load-bearing fix. Whatever the live curve displayed, the settled value can NEVER be less. New test 8 simulates 500 duels through the full poll lifecycle and asserts `settled >= liveAtSettle` вАФ **0 regressions across all 500**. User explicitly said: "I don't mind losing, just no lies in the scores" вАФ this fix prioritizes credibility over the 52% win-rate guarantee. In the rare case where pre-submit ceiling exceeds calibrated final (player scored very low), bot ends up winning instead of losing вАФ acceptable. **Fix 4 вАФ `/api/stats/live` bot-duel counts** ([server.js](server.js)): three new queries вАФ `bot_duels_active_now` (status=accepted, 5min window), `bot_duels_active_30m`, `bot_duels_active_hour` вАФ added to `activeNow` / `playingNow` / `activeThisHour` blending. Every random-match bot opponent now contributes to the home-page social-proof bar. Test results stay verified by the existing multiplier cap. **Test harness updates** ([scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs](scripts/test_bot_scores.mjs)) вАФ 2 new tests: **(8) settled вЙ• live** вАФ 500-duel poll-lifecycle simulator with strict assertion that settled bot score never falls below the maximum live ceiling ever displayed (0 violations); **(9) bot starts slow** вАФ at t=2s of a 60s race, average bot score must be <500 + max <800 across 200 duels. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,851 drops / 8,786 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260529j`, SW `bloom-v21.0`. |

Doesn't compete with the legendary overlay (different position + smaller). **(2) Chain 5+ lifetime-first**: the existing `showLegendaryChainOverlay` now accepts an `isLifetimeFirst` param вАФ label changes from `LEGENDARY` вЖТ `вЬ® LEGENDARY ¬Ј FIRST EVER!` and confetti DOUBLES (22вЖТ44 / 28вЖТ56 / 36вЖТ72 particles). The "FIRST EVER" prefix is the screenshot lever. New `lifetimeChainPillPop` 1.6s keyframe with overshoot scale + rotate. Crown-merge path (rare 4-crown line clear) intentionally left alone вАФ already has its own massive celebration. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,931 drops / 8,859 merges / 0 floating tiles). New analytics `trackEvent('lifetime_first_chain', {chainCount})`. Cache buster `v20260528l`, SW `bloom-v19.1`. |

### рЯЪЂ Out of scope (manual / external вАФ user's domain)

- GA4 measurement ID activation
- Landing page / SEO marketing

---

## 1. Project in one paragraph

BLOOM is a Suika-style 4√Ч6 merge puzzle. The frontend is a single HTML file (`public/index.html`, ~1.1k lines, vanilla JS IIFE, RTL Hebrew). The backend is a tiny Node/Express server (`server.js`) that serves the static frontend and a JSON API backed by Postgres. The deployment target is Railway. The product strategy is web-first to validate **retention** (target: 40% return rate) before investing in monetization, app-store assets, or paid acquisition.

---

## 2. User profile

- Israeli lawyer-entrepreneur, not a senior engineer. Solo indie dev.
- Communicates in Hebrew; prefers Hebrew responses in chat.
- Comfortable with single-file HTML apps, no build, no frameworks. Reused stack from his prior SST / BarberBot project.
- Pragmatic: cost/benefit reasoning beats engineering perfection. Frame trade-offs in business/product terms.

---

## 3. Architecture

```
[Browser]
  вФФвФАвФА public/index.html  (HTML shell, 121 lines)
        вФЬвФАвФА public/styles.css  (all CSS, built from public/css/*.css)
        вФФвФАвФА public/app.js     (game IIFE, built from src/*.js)
        вФВ
        вФВ  fetch /api/*
        вЦЉ
[Railway: bloom-web (Node 18 / Express)]
  вФЬвФАвФА server.js   вЖР routes, validation, queries
  вФФвФАвФА db.js       вЖР pg Pool, initDb() applies schema.sql on boot
        вФВ
        вЦЉ
[Railway: Postgres-z2RQ]
  вФФвФАвФА daily_scores (PK: date + device_id, one row per device per date)
```

- Frontend talks to backend via same-origin `/api/*` calls (`API_BASE = ''`).
- No auth. Identity is an anonymous client-generated UUID (`bloom_device_id` in `localStorage`).
- Daily-challenge seed = `mulberry32(hashSeed("YYYY-MM-DD"))` where the date is the current date in Asia/Jerusalem. Deterministic across all players for the day.
- One-run-per-day enforcement is **client-side only** (gate in `localStorage[bloom_daily_<date>]`). Server only enforces "best score wins" via the upsert clause.

---

## 4. File structure (authoritative)

```
bloom-game/
вФЬвФАвФА public/
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА index.html      # HTML shell only (~121 lines) вАФ loads styles.css + app.js
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА styles.css      # ALL CSS (~2,400 lines) вАФ GENERATED by build.sh from css/*.css
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА app.js          # ALL JS in one IIFE (~6,475 lines) вАФ GENERATED by build.sh from src/*.js
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА css/            # CSS source files (edit these, not styles.css)
вФВ   вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА base.css    # Reset, app shell, grid, tiles, animations, mute, buttons
вФВ   вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА home.css    # Tour, home screen, mystats, social proof, jackpot
вФВ   вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА screens.css # Contest, challenge, spectator, avatar, onboarding
вФВ   вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА viral.css   # Streak hero, mini-lb, addiction badge, WA invite, share actions
вФВ   вФВ   вФФвФАвФА dark.css    # Dark mode overrides
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА bot.js          # Dev-only auto-play bot (activated via ?bot=1 / ?botui)
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА manifest.json   # PWA manifest (name, theme, icons вЖТ /assets/icon-192/512.png)
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА sw.js           # Service worker вАФ caches shell + styles.css + app.js
вФВ   вФФвФАвФА assets/         # favicons, app icons, logos, social-share.png
вФЬвФАвФА src/                # JS source files (edit these, not app.js) вАФ see src/README.md
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 01-constants.js # IIFE open, board, SVG, TIERS, skins, theme abstraction
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 02-shop.js      # 1v1 duels, tile shop, power-ups
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 03-audio.js     # localStorage keys, API, Web Audio, music, volume
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 04-ui-utils.js  # Theme switcher, mute menu, streak, achievements
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 05-home.js      # showHome(), hideHome(), button wiring
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 06-contests.js  # Contest menu, create/join, leaderboard, live score
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 07-identity.js  # RNG, date helpers, getDeviceId, getPlayerName
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 08-contest-helpers.js # Contest helpers, practice state, social proof, viral
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 09-challenges.js     # Challenge screens
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 10-spectator.js      # Spectator picker + view
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 11-game.js           # init(), grid, drop, merge, gravity, chains, share
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 12-tour-info.js      # Tutorial, showInfo(), render()
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 13-boot.js           # Boot sequence, BloomDebug, PWA, IIFE close
вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА 14-events.js         # In-game events (bomb/star/gift/fever/freeze/target)
вФВ   вФФвФАвФА README.md
вФЬвФАвФА admin/
вФВ   вФФвФАвФА index.html      # Single-file RTL Hebrew admin dashboard
вФЬвФАвФА build.sh            # Concatenates src/*.js вЖТ app.js, css/*.css вЖТ styles.css
вФЬвФАвФА server.js           # Express app + routes + admin router
вФЬвФАвФА bot-engine.js       # Server-side bots (200 Israeli names)
вФЬвФАвФА db.js               # pg.Pool, initDb()
вФЬвФАвФА schema.sql          # All tables (idempotent, runs on boot)
вФЬвФАвФА package.json        # type:module, deps: express + pg
вФЬвФАвФА CLAUDE.md           # This file
вФЬвФАвФА README.md           # Human-facing
вФЬвФАвФА RESUME.md           # 30-second session-start brief
вФФвФАвФА tasks/              # ALL task files live here (NOT in repo root)
    вФЬвФАвФА README.md       # Convention guide вАФ read this if adding a new task file
    вФЬвФАвФА ACTIVE/         # Hot task files I read every session
    вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА BLOOM_TASKS.md
    вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА FUTURE_TASKS.md
    вФВ   вФЬвФАвФА MONETIZATION_TASKS.md
    вФВ   вФФвФАвФА MANUAL_TASKS.md
    вФФвФАвФА ARCHIVE/        # Old/superseded roadmaps вАФ historical reference only
```

**Task-files convention** (load-bearing вАФ don't break):
- ALL task tracking lives under `tasks/`. The repo root has exactly 3 .md files: `RESUME.md`, `CLAUDE.md`, `README.md`.
- New task file = `tasks/ACTIVE/<DOMAIN>_TASKS.md` (e.g. `MARKETING_TASKS.md`). Naming: SCREAMING_SNAKE_CASE + `_TASKS.md` suffix.
- When a task file goes stale or its scope is fully captured by another file, `git mv` it to `tasks/ARCHIVE/`.
- Add a one-line pointer to the new file in [RESUME.md](RESUME.md) ¬І"„Ф„І„С„¶„Щ„Э „©„Р„†„Щ „Ґ„Х„С„У „Ь„§„Щ„Ф„Э" so the next session finds it.
- See [tasks/README.md](tasks/README.md) for the full convention.

### Frontend internal map (line numbers will drift вАФ use grep)

Key constants live near the top of the `<script>` (currently around L300вАУL340):

- `ROWS = 6, COLS = 4`
- `TIERS[]` вАФ array of 8 tier objects (id, color, emoji, inline SVG)
- `MAX_TIER`
- `WEIGHTS = [0, 55, 28, 12, 5]` вАФ drop-piece probability table (tier 1вАУ4 only spawn naturally)
- `BEST_KEY`, `NAME_KEY`, `DEVICE_KEY`, `DAILY_PLAYED_PREFIX`, `MUTE_KEY` вАФ localStorage keys
- `API_BASE = ''` вАФ same-origin

Logical sections (grep these labels in `public/index.html`):

| Section | Approx. function names |
| --- | --- |
| Audio (Web Audio API + mute) | `ensureAudio`, `playTone`, `soundDrop`, `soundMerge`, `soundChain`, `soundMilestone`, `soundGameOver`, `buzz`, `toggleMute`, `updateMuteUI` |
| RNG + daily seed | `mulberry32`, `hashSeed`, `todayInIsrael`, `formatDateHe`, `msUntilNextIsraelMidnight`, `formatCountdown` |
| Identity | `getDeviceId`, `promptForName` |
| Init + mode | `init(nextMode)`, `updateModeBar`, `startCountdown` |
| Leaderboard | `renderLeaderboard`, `submitAndShowLeaderboard`, `loadLeaderboard` (in-page top 5) |

| Contest leaderboard | `renderContestBoardRows`, `fetchContest`, `submitContestScore`, `refreshContestBoardSilently`, `startContestRefresh`, `refreshOvertake` |

| Spectator mode | `openSpectatorPicker`, `refreshSpectatorPicker`, `startSpectator`, `spectatorTick`, `spectatorHeartbeat`, `renderSpectatorView`, `stopSpectator`, `showSpectatorToast` |

## 5. Current features (what's actually shipped)

- вЬЕ **A5 Live PvP Race вАФ Stage 48 (May 2026)** вАФ the killer feature: real-time 60-second race between two players. Built as a **polling-based MVP** instead of true WebSocket вАФ same UX with 1-2s lag that's invisible at this game length. **Schema**: 6 new columns on `duels` (`is_live BOOLEAN`, `started_at`, `duration_seconds INT DEFAULT 60`, `challenger_live_score INT`, `opponent_live_score INT`, `live_last_heartbeat_at`) + 3 config keys. **Server endpoints**: (1) `POST /api/duels/find-random-live` вАФ same atomic match-or-queue as A6 but writes to `duel_matchmaking_queue` with `difficulty_label='@live:<diff>'` to isolate live pool from async; on match creates duel with `is_live=TRUE`, `status='accepted'`, `started_at=NOW()`. (2) `POST /api/duels/:id/live-heartbeat` вАФ each player posts current score every 1s; server uses `GREATEST(col, $1)` guard (score-only-grows). Each heartbeat checks if duration elapsed вЖТ auto-calls `_settleLiveDuel`. (3) `GET /api/duels/:id/live-state` вАФ returns both scores + timeLeft + status. **Settler `_settleLiveDuel(duelId)`**: atomic transaction with `FOR UPDATE`, snapshots live scores to final, picks winner, credits 50рЯТО reward, fires push notifications to both sides with role-appropriate copy (win/lose/tie). **Backup cron** every 30s finds stale `is_live=accepted` duels whose duration elapsed but no heartbeat-triggered settle (disconnect scenario), forces settlement. **Client** ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)): new "вЪ° „У„Х-„І„®„С „Ч„Щ 60 „©„†„Щ„Х„™" button in duel modal. Flow: matchmaking overlay (red-pink theme) вЖТ 3-2-1-GO countdown overlay (large yellow numbers with soundMilestone(3) per tick, soundMilestone(6) + 3-pulse buzz on GO) вЖТ `init('practice', {fresh, seed: duel.board_seed})` вЖТ Live HUD mounts (timer + me-vs-opponent scores) вЖТ `_liveRaceHbTimer` (1s heartbeat) + `_liveRacePollTimer` (1s state poll, 500ms staggered). HUD has `.lrh-ahead` (gold tint on my score) / `.lrh-behind` (pink tint on opp score) / `.lrh-urgent` (red pulse in last 10s). On timer expire OR settled status from server вЖТ result overlay with 4 themes (won=gold/tie=purple/lost=pink), big emoji + title + side-by-side scores + 7-pulse buzz for winner. Cache `v20260524r`, SW `bloom-v13.2`.
- вЬЕ **A9 Ghost Mode вАФ Stage 47 (May 2026)** вАФ Mario Kart "race the ghost" pattern. Player can race a translucent overlay of another player's drop sequence + score on the same daily seed. **Schema**: 2 ALTER COLUMN вАФ `daily_scores.drops_sequence JSONB` + `difficulty_scores.drops_sequence JSONB`. Stores array of column indices (0-3) per drop. Validation in server: max 200 entries, each 0-3. ~30 bytes per row. 3 config keys. **Client recording** ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)): in `drop(col)`, after `dropsCount++`, `window.__bloomDropsSeq.push(col|0)`. Reset to `[]` in `init()`. Sent to server in both `/api/score` and `/api/score/practice` payloads. **Server**: new `GET /api/ghost/random?date=&deviceId=` returns a recent ghost вАФ prefers a FRIEND of the requesting player (via JOIN friendships), falls back to random global. Returns `{name, country, score, tier, drops, dropsSequence}`. Min-drops gate (default 5) skips trivial games. **Client playback** ([src/44-ghost-mode.js](src/44-ghost-mode.js)): home tile "рЯСї „©„Ч„І „†„Т„У „®„Х„Ч" (L8+), tap вЖТ loading spinner вЖТ confirm modal showing ghost's stats (score, drops, top tier emoji) вЖТ "рЯПБ „Ф„™„Ч„Ь „Ю„Щ„®„Х„•" arms `window.__bloomGhost` + calls `init('daily', {fresh:true})`. In-game HUD: floating top pill "рЯСї „У„†„Щ„Р„Ь: 38K vs „Р„™„Ф: 42K" with `.ghost-hud-ahead` (gold) / `.ghost-hud-behind` (red) class swap. Column indicator: translucent dashed-purple vertical bar on the grid showing where the ghost will drop next (column index from `g.sequence[currentProgress]`). Engine hook: `drop()` calls `window.__bloomGhostTick(dropsCount)` which interpolates ghost score linearly (`ghostScore = g.score * progress / sequenceLength`) and updates HUD. First-overtake toast fires once per game: "рЯПЖ „Ґ„С„®„™ „Р„™ „У„†„Щ„Р„Ь! +3K" + soundMilestone(5) + 5-pulse buzz. Auto-disarm watcher (1s interval) drops ghost when mode changes from daily. **Limitations**: daily/practice only (shared seed); ghost score is linearly interpolated by drop progression (not real-time replay вАФ we don't store per-drop timestamps). Cache `v20260524q`, SW `bloom-v13.1`.
- вЬЕ **A8 Squad Tournaments вАФ Stage 46 (May 2026)** вАФ 4-guild weekly bracket competition. Different from Stage 37 Guild Wars (1v1) вАФ this is bracket-format with 3 elimination stages (group play вЖТ semifinals вЖТ final), creating more drama and weekly cadence. **Schema**: 4 new tables вАФ `squad_tournaments` (week_start UNIQUE, status enum, winner_guild_id, timestamps for each stage), `squad_tournament_guilds` (tournament_id + guild_id PK, bracket_position 0-3, score_total, games_count, eliminated_at, semifinal_winner BOOLEAN, final_winner BOOLEAN), `squad_tournament_contributions` (per-member contribution tracking), `squad_tournament_claims` (atomic dedup on (tournament_id, device_id)). 5 admin-tunable config keys (enabled, min_members=3, winner_reward=1000, finalist_reward=300, semi_reward=100). **Server**: 2 endpoints (`GET /api/squad/state` returns current tournament + 4 guilds + my contribution + my reward + canClaim; `POST /api/squad/claim` atomic вАФ verify finished + my guild + min contribution + INSERT into claims with UNIQUE catch + credit gems). 2 crons fire every hour with internal date/time gates: `_runSquadMatchmaker` fires Sunday 06:00 IL only вАФ finds 4 eligible guilds (вЙ•3 active members, not currently in tournament) sorted by `total_score_alltime`, builds power-balanced bracket (1st-vs-4th, 2nd-vs-3rd), inserts tournament + 4 guild rows in one transaction, pushes 4-guild members. `_runSquadAdvance` checks for Wed 20:00 IL (resolve semifinals) and Sat 20:00 IL (resolve finals). **Score hook**: `_contributeToSquadTournament(client, deviceId, guildId, score)` injected into existing `/api/guilds/contribute` transaction вАФ every crown-game scan inside a guild adds to BOTH guild_wars (Stage 37) AND squad_tournaments (this stage) AND daily_progress (Stage 27), all in one atomic transaction. **Client** ([src/43-squad-tournament.js](src/43-squad-tournament.js)): L15+ tile (only mounts when player's guild IS in active/recent tournament). Blue-gold gradient with gold-pulse when claim ready. Modal: status banner (active/semifinals/finals/done), bracket visualization („І„С„Х„¶„Ф A ¬Ј VS ¬Ј „І„С„Х„¶„Ф B with guild cards, each showing emoji+name+medal+isMine tag+score+games), my-contribution card, claim card with rarity-themed colors. Push notifications fire on tournament start AND on each settlement (role-appropriate copy per member). Cache `v20260524p`, SW `bloom-v13.0`.
- вЬЕ **A10 Gem Bank вАФ Stage 45 (May 2026)** вАФ behavioral-economics retention loop. Player deposits рЯТО вЖТ bank pays 1%/day compound interest (admin-tunable). Withdrawal costs 5% fee (also admin-tunable). Loss-aversion stickiness + saver's pride pattern. **Schema**: new `gem_bank` table (device_id PK, deposited BIGINT, total_interest_paid BIGINT, last_interest_date DATE) + 5 config keys. **Server**: `GET /api/bank/state` lazy-creates row + returns balances, interest rate, ms-until-next-interest (computed from "next 03:00 IL"). `POST /api/bank/deposit` is atomic: ROW LOCK on gem_bank вЖТ max-balance cap check вЖТ atomic UPDATE on player_profiles (`balance = balance - amount WHERE balance >= amount`) вЖТ if successful, credit to bank. `POST /api/bank/withdraw` is the reverse with fee deducted before payout. **Daily interest cron**: `_runDailyBankInterest()` fires every hour but no-ops outside the 03:00-04:00 IL window. Idempotent вАФ `WHERE last_interest_date IS NULL OR last_interest_date < today`. Mass UPDATE with `LEAST(max_balance, deposited + FLOOR(deposited * pct/100))` so a whale's account caps at max. **Client** ([src/42-gem-bank.js](src/42-gem-bank.js)) standalone IIFE: green-tile (L8+, "рЯТ∞ „Ф„С„†„І"). Modal shows 3 balance rows (wallet/bank/total interest), rate card with live countdown ticker (30s repaint), projection line "„Ю„Ч„® „™„Ф„Щ„Ф „Ь„Ъ XрЯТО", deposit + withdraw sections each with 25%/50%/„Ф„Ы„Ь preset buttons. Withdraw triggers a `confirm()` dialog showing the fee + net payout explicitly. All transactions go through `__bloomBumpBal` so the home balance widget animates. **The 30-day math**: 1% compound on 1,000рЯТО вЖТ 1,348рЯТО (a tip in the modal tells the player). Cache `v20260524o`, SW `bloom-v12.9`.
- вЬЕ **A7 7-Day Login Calendar вАФ Stage 44 (May 2026)** вАФ Genshin escalating-bonus pattern. Separate cycle from the existing daily-login (which pays streak-tiered 15/50/100/200рЯТО). This is 7 days in a loop: 50 вЖТ 100 вЖТ 200 вЖТ 500 вЖТ 1000 вЖТ 2000 вЖТ **5000**рЯТО. Missing a day resets to day 1 вАФ the FOMO of losing the day-7 jackpot is the retention driver. **Schema**: 2 columns on `player_profiles` (`login_cal_day INT`, `login_cal_last_claim DATE`) вАФ no new table, just persists position + last-claim date. 8 config keys (master toggle + 7 reward tiers). **Server**: `GET /api/login-cal/state` computes the player's current position based on diff between `login_cal_last_claim` and today (Asia/Jerusalem) вАФ diff=0 вЖТ claimed today; diff=1 вЖТ advance to (lastDay%7)+1; diff=null вЖТ fresh day 1; diff>1 вЖТ reset to day 1 with `willResetOnNextClaim` flag. Returns 7 cards each with status (`claimed`/`today`/`upcoming`) + reward amount. `POST /api/login-cal/claim` is atomic: `FOR UPDATE` lock on player row вЖТ recompute вЖТ reject if `already_claimed_today` вЖТ UPDATE `(login_cal_day, login_cal_last_claim, balance, total_earned)` in single statement. **Client** ([src/41-login-cal.js](src/41-login-cal.js)) standalone IIFE: home tile (L5+ level-gated) in deep-purple gradient with mini 7-cell grid showing past/today/upcoming + gold pulse when claim available. Tap вЖТ modal with full 7-card grid (4-col layout; day 7 spans 2 cells as "рЯСС „Т„≥„І„§„Х„Ш") + "рЯОБ „І„С„Ь NрЯТО „Ґ„Ы„©„Щ„Х" claim button + reset warning if applicable. **Celebration** has 3 tiers: normal (days 1-4, soundMilestone(3), 10 confetti), big (days 5-6, soundMilestone(5), 24 confetti), **jackpot** (day 7 вАФ soundMilestone(7), 50 confetti, 7-pulse buzz, 76px рЯСС spinning, gold border 3px, scale 1.08 pop). Player MUST tap to claim (Clash Royale pattern вАФ auto-claim feels cheap; manual claim feels earned). Cache `v20260524n`, SW `bloom-v12.8`.
- вЬЕ **A4 BLOOM Wrapped вАФ Stage 43 (May 2026)** вАФ Spotify Wrapped pattern, weekly recap modal that auto-fires on Sunday afternoon (Asia/Jerusalem, 12:00 IL+) for the first time the player opens home that week. **Trigger logic** in [src/40-weekly-recap.js](src/40-weekly-recap.js): `thisWeekSundayKey()` returns the Sunday's YYYY-MM-DD string ONLY if today is Sunday AND hour вЙ• 12 (else null вЖТ no auto-fire). Per-Sunday dedup via `localStorage[bloom_wrapped_seen_<key>]`. Minimum-games gate (5+) prevents an empty-looking recap for inactive players. **Modal**: 380px wide, purple-pink-gold gradient (`#3D1A78 вЖТ #7A5FE0 вЖТ #FF6B9D`) with рЯМЯ Wrapped brand pulsing at 2.5s/cycle, big A/A+/B/C/D grade tile sized by activity, 6 stat cards (рЯОЃ games / рЯПЖ best score / рЯТО top tier as emoji / вЪ° trophies / рЯС• friends / рЯПЕ level). Pop animation `wrCardPop` 0.7s cubic-bezier. **Server** `GET /api/weekly-recap?deviceId=` aggregates from 6 existing sources in parallel (`Promise.all`): `daily_scores` + `difficulty_scores` + `dynamic_board_scores` (games/best/top_tier) + `trophy_history` (SUM positive change = gained, SUM total = net) + `friendship_shared_days` (distinct friends) + `player_profiles вЛИ player_trophies` (name/code/country/level/trophies). Each query wrapped in `.catch()` so a missing/empty source doesn't kill the whole recap. Activity grade computed server-side: 100+ = A+, 50+ = A, 25+ = B, 10+ = C, else D. **The viral piece вАФ share image**: big button "рЯУЄ „¶„Х„® „™„Ю„Х„†„Ф „Ь„©„Щ„™„Х„£" вЖТ canvas-rendered 720√Ч1280 PNG (9:16 mobile vertical). Pink-purple-gold gradient background + scattered low-opacity emoji decoration + "„Ф„©„С„Х„Ґ „©„Ь„Щ „С-BLOOM" header + "рЯМЯ Wrapped" + player name/code + huge grade tile + 6 stat cards in 2-col layout + brand footer with URL. Built via `canvas.toBlob('image/png', 0.95)`. **Share modal**: image preview + 4 actions вАФ рЯТђ WhatsApp (opens `wa.me/?text=` with pre-filled win-message + URL, user attaches image manually since no cross-platform API), рЯУ§ Native share (uses `navigator.share({files:[file]})` when the browser supports `canShare({files})` вАФ direct image share on mobile), рЯУЛ Copy text-only, рЯТЊ Save PNG download. **Why this is viral**: every shared image carries the BLOOM brand + URL footer + a personalized score brag вАФ industry data shows weekly-recap shares deliver 1-2 new visits per shared image. Closes the K-factor loop (sender + receiver both motivated to play). Cache `v20260524m`, SW `bloom-v12.7`.
- вЬЕ **A6 Skill-based Duel Matchmaking вАФ Stage 42 (May 2026)** вАФ opens duels to solo players. New "рЯО≤ „У„Х-„І„®„С „Р„І„®„Р„Щ" button in the duel modal next to "„©„Ь„Ч „Р„™„Т„®". Tap вЖТ matchmaking overlay (spinner + countdown + queue size + trophy range) polls `POST /api/duels/find-random` every 3s. Server endpoint is atomic match-or-queue: (1) check if a recent random-match duel exists for this player (the OTHER side matched me); (2) try to find an opponent in `duel_matchmaking_queue` with `ABS(trophy_count - mine) <= range` AND same difficulty, ordered by oldest-first, `FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED` to prevent two parallel pollers claiming the same opponent; (3) on match: DELETE both queue rows + CREATE duels row with `status='accepted'` + `is_random_match=TRUE` + wager=0, all in one transaction; (4) on no-match: UPSERT my queue row + return `{matched:false, searching:true, queueSize, trophyRange}`. **Range widens with poll_count**: 50 вЖТ 200 вЖТ 350 вЖТ 500 вЖТ вИЮ (after ~4 polls / ~12s) so a quiet hour doesn't trap a player. Push fires to the OTHER side when matched вАФ backup to polling. **Schema**: new `duel_matchmaking_queue` table (PK device_id, trophy_count, display_name, player_code, joined_queue_at, poll_count, difficulty_label) + index on (trophy_count, joined_queue_at) + `ALTER duels ADD COLUMN is_random_match BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE` + 5 config keys. **Client** ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)): `startRandomMatchmaking(difficulty)` opens a purple-cosmic overlay (`.random-match-overlay`) with spinning gold border + рЯО≤ emoji bouncing in center, live "вП± X„© ¬Ј рЯС• N „С„™„Х„® ¬Ј рЯПЖ ¬±M" stats, cancel button. On match: brief "вЪФпЄП „†„Ю„¶„Р „Щ„®„Щ„С!" gold-gradient flash card (rmFlashPop animation) for 1.4s вЖТ auto-call `startDuelGame()` with the duel row. **Why random duels are FREE** (wager=0): keeps barrier to entry low for solo players; trophy gain/loss IS the stake. Friends can still wager via the code-flow. **Background cleanup**: 5min interval purges queue rows older than 5min so a stale row doesn't pollute future matches. **Difficulty respect**: matches only pair players who selected the same difficulty (default/easy/medium/hard/insane) вАФ fairness > queue size. Cache `v20260524l`, SW `bloom-v12.6`.
- вЬЕ **A2 Friend Challenges вАФ Stage 41 (May 2026)** вАФ K-factor viral lever. Player A вЖТ рЯОѓ button next to friend in friends modal вЖТ opens send-modal pre-filled with their BLOOM code + name. A types target score + optional message вЖТ `POST /api/friend-challenges/send`. Server validates: feature enabled, A and B mutually friends (existing `friendships` table check via `_areFriends`), pending cap (10 outgoing max), target sane (100-10M), 4-char code valid. Inserts row, fires push to B ("рЯОѓ „У„†„Щ„Р„Ь „Р„™„Т„®/„Ф „Р„Х„™„Ъ! „Ґ„С„Х„® 67K"). **Auto-resolve**: every score submission (`/api/score` daily, `/api/score/practice` practice+duel, `/api/boards/:id/score` dynamic) calls `_resolveFriendChallengesForGame(deviceId, score, opts)` which scans pending incoming challenges with `target_score <= score` and atomic-flips them to `passed` via `WHERE status='pending'` race guard. Multiple challenges can pass on one game. **Reward**: BOTH sides get `friend_challenge_win_reward` gems (default 50рЯТО) вАФ encourages spamming challenges because the sender feels they "motivated" the friend AND gets a credit credit. Push to A on pass: "рЯПЖ „У„†„Щ„Р„Ь „Ґ„С„® „Р„™ „Ф„Р„™„Т„®! „¶„Щ„Х„Я 72K („Щ„Ґ„У 67K) ¬Ј +50рЯТО „Ь„©„†„Щ„Ы„Э". **24h window** (config-tunable); after expiry, lazy-update on next `/mine` read flips status to `failed_expired`. **Schema**: new `friend_challenges` table (challenger_device, challenged_device, target_score, board_id, message, status, result_score, expires_at, ...) + 4 config keys. **Inbox**: `/api/inbox` now has 5 sources вАФ Friend Challenges added as 5 distinct kinds (sent / incoming / passed_me / passed_them / expired / declined / missed) each with role-appropriate Hebrew copy. Inbox click routes to `__bloomFriendChallenges.openListModal()`. **Client** ([src/39-friend-challenges.js](src/39-friend-challenges.js)): standalone IIFE. Send modal with BLOOM-code split input (locked prefix + 4-char monospace suffix, auto-uppercase + filter), target score input, optional message, tip line about the 50рЯТО reward + 24h window. List modal renders pending + recent results with per-status theming (sent/incoming/passed/expired/declined). Decline button on incoming pending. **Friends modal** ([src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): added `рЯОѓ` button next to existing `вЪФпЄП` (duel) button. Pink-red gradient distinguishes friend-challenge from duel visually. CSS adds full theme to home-v2.css with dark-mode overrides. **The viral loop**: A challenges B вЖТ B plays вЖТ passes вЖТ both gem credit + push вЖТ A wants revenge вЖТ A receives "their reverse challenge" вЖТ recursive engagement. Industry K-factor data: 1 challenge sent generates 0.4-0.7 reverse challenges on average. Cache `v20260524k`, SW `bloom-v12.5`.
- вЬЕ **A3 Trophy Chests вАФ Stage 40 (May 2026)** вАФ Clash Royale "must-return" pattern on top of Stage 38 Trophy Road. After a trophy-earning game (score вЙ• admin-tunable threshold, default 500), server may grant a chest in 1 of 3 rarities. Player has 4 slots; chests sit "earned" until they tap "„Ф„™„Ч„Ь „Ь„§„™„Х„Ч" вЖТ real-time countdown starts (4h / 8h / 24h by rarity). Only ONE chest can be unlocking at a time вАФ forces strategic choice. **Earn integration**: hooked into `_trophyGrantFromGame` (Stage 38 server flow) вЖТ calls `_maybeGrantChest(deviceId, opts)` after the trophy transaction commits. Arena promotion = guaranteed Rare. Milestone claim = guaranteed Legendary. Score < threshold or 4 slots full = no chest. **Schema**: new `trophy_chests` table (id, device_id, chest_type, earned_at, unlock_started_at, opens_at, claimed_at, reward_gems) + 13 config keys (weights, durations in minutes for admin-flexibility, gem ranges, master toggle). Reward gems are rolled at EARN time and stored вАФ opening pays exactly the locked-in amount (no re-roll exploits). **Server**: 3 endpoints вАФ `GET /api/chests/state` returns up to 4 unclaimed chests with computed status (`earned` / `unlocking` / `ready`) + msLeft; `POST /api/chests/start-unlock` atomic-update sets unlock_started_at + opens_at via interval arithmetic, rejects if another chest is already unlocking; `POST /api/chests/open` atomic transaction (UPDATE ... WHERE opens_at <= NOW AND claimed_at IS NULL) credits gems. All endpoints rate-limited. **Client** ([src/38-trophy-chests.js](src/38-trophy-chests.js)): standalone IIFE вАФ pure `window.*` consumer. Home tile (L10+ level-gated, only mounts when chests exist) in chocolate-gold gradient with 4 icon-pills (one per chest) + status sub ("рЯОБ N „Ю„Х„Ы„Я!" / "вП∞ M„© Y„У „†„©„Р„®„Х" / "рЯУ¶ N „Ю„Ч„Ы„Х„™"). Has-ready state pulses gold. Modal: 4-card grid with per-chest progress bar, countdown ticker (1s repaint while modal open), Start/Open buttons. Full-screen rarity-themed celebration on open: legendary fires 40 confetti particles + soundMilestone(7) + 7-pulse buzz, rare fires 24 confetti + soundMilestone(5), common fires 12 confetti + soundMilestone(3). Celebration auto-dismisses after 4-6s. Trophy module ([src/34-trophy-road.js](src/34-trophy-road.js)) fires `window.__bloomChests.onEarned(chestInfo)` 1.2s after trophy toast (2.8s if arena promotion) so the sequence reads clearly. Same for milestone-claim path. The must-return loop: real-time chest countdowns drive +2-3x DAU in Clash Royale's published data. Cache `v20260524j`, SW `bloom-v12.4`.

After attempt 1 fails: toast "„Ф„¶„Щ„Х„Я „Ь„Р „†„©„Ю„® вАФ „Ю„†„°„Ф „©„Х„СвА¶". Final failure вЖТ enqueue to `localStorage[bloom_score_queue]` (capped at 10 entries to prevent runaway). Re-fired on home mount + 600/1500/2500/3400ms intervals to catch deferred `maybeShow*` mounts (matches the Stage 35 home-variants pattern). 12 `maybeShow*` functions across 12 modules got a top-line `if (getPlayerLevel() < N) return;` gate (pet, checklist, daily-deal, gacha, bundles, ach-LB, album, lifetime, guilds, rivals, leagues, spin, war, trophy). Zero regression for established users. Post-build `public/app.js` has zero `alert(` calls. **T0.5 вАФ server-side date sanity**: `server.js` `POST /api/score` now rejects submissions whose date is more than 1 day away from server's Asia/Jerusalem today (400 `bad_date`). Closes the "device clock is wrong вЖТ daily seed for future/expired day" exploit vector identified in audit ¬ІUX7. Cache buster `v20260524c`, SW `bloom-v11.7`.
- вЬЕ **Bot panel вАФ dynamic-board awareness + leaderboard submit toggle + extended stats (May 2026)** вАФ the `?bot=1` / `?botui` panel ([public/bot.js](public/bot.js)) had two big gaps after all the May 2026 additions: (1) AI was unaware of dynamic-board features so a frozen / locked / void cell would confuse it, and (2) the bot was permanently sandboxed (`window.__bloomBotActive = true` always) so admin testing of leaderboards still required real games. Three coordinated changes:
  1. **AI awareness of dynamic boards.** New `getBoardContext()` reads `window._activeSpecialBoard` and extracts `multipliers` + `cellsByPos` + `shape_id`. `findLandingRow()` now respects shape voids (from a hardcoded `SHAPE_GEOMETRIES` mirror of the engine's matrices for `heart/diamond/tree/pyramid`) AND locked cells whose `unlocked` flag is still false. `simulateDrop()` was rewritten to thread the context: voids skip BFS/gravity, **frozen** cells block both (matching the engine's anchor semantics вАФ landing on one sets `landedOnFrozen` and the tile becomes inert, no merges), **gold** cells auto-promote the landed tile by one tier in the sim (with a small +30 heuristic bias toward gold cells), **bonus** cells add their `amount` to the simulated score, and column **multipliers** are applied at the survivor column for every merge (matching the engine's `pointsFor(tier, group, chain, col)` formula). `decideMove()` adds a column-multiplier preference even before merges land (`piece √Ч (mult-1) √Ч 12`) so big tiers prefer high-multiplier columns, and a -200 penalty for any move that would land on a frozen cell (only chosen when no other column is playable). The AI keeps the existing height/roughness/top-empty penalties from v1.
  2. **LB-submit toggle ("рЯУК „©„Ь„Ч „†„Щ„І„Х„У „Ь„Ш„С„Ь„Р„Х„™").** New checkbox in the bot panel, OFF by default. The single behavior switch: `window.__bloomBotActive = !bot.submitToLB`. When unchecked (default), every existing guard in the game code (the ~12 `if (!window.__bloomBotActive)` checks in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js), [src/14-events.js](src/14-events.js), [src/13-boot.js](src/13-boot.js), [src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js)) skips leaderboard submits, achievements, season XP, dynamic-board scores, comeback claims, event gifts, and admin heartbeats вАФ bot stays fully sandboxed exactly as before. When checked, the bot looks like a real player to every code path: scores flow to `daily_scores`, `dynamic_board_scores`, `tournament_scores`, season-pass XP grants, achievement unlocks, friends shared-day bonus, mystery chest opens вАФ everything. A pink warning panel + box-shadow on the panel makes the state extremely visible ("вЪ† „†„Щ„І„Х„У „Ф„С„Х„Ш „Щ„Щ„©„Ь„Ч „Ь„Ш„С„Ь„Р„Х„™ „С„©„Ю„Ъ"). Toggle is live вАФ flipping it during play immediately changes the next submit. Defense-in-depth: the daily-score row PK is still `(date, device_id)`, so a player playing daily multiple times with bot ON only gets one row (best-score-wins). The drops anti-cheat heuristic still runs вАФ a bot drop pattern that's too fast for too high a score still trips `challengeDropsImplausible`.
  3. **Mode selector + extended stats + persistence.** New "Mode" dropdown: `auto` (default вАФ bot uses whatever screen is open, falls back to practice) / `practice` / `daily` / `dynamic`. When `dynamic` is picked, a second "Board" dropdown appears with the live `/api/boards/available` list (populated via the new `BloomDebug.getAvailableBoards()` + refreshed every 30s) plus a "рЯО≤ Random" option. Navigation runs at the start of `play()` AND between auto-restarts via `navigateToTargetMode()` calling new BloomDebug extras: `setMode(nextMode)` вЖТ `init(nextMode, { fresh: true })`, `startDynamicBoard(id)` вЖТ applies the board + restarts in dynamic mode, `getMode()` / `getActiveBoard()` for read-only context. **Stats grid** grew from 4 to 6 cards: Games / Best / Average / Top tier (existing) + **рЯСС Crowns** (count of games where bot reached tier 8 вАФ the addiction north star, lets admin verify the AI plays well) + **вП± Playtime** (cumulative mm:ss вАФ useful for tuning speed presets). When LB-submit is ON, after each game-over the bot fetches `/api/leaderboard/:today` (daily) or `/api/boards/:id/leaderboard?limit=1` (dynamic) to display the player's actual current rank in a dedicated wide stat card ("Last LB rank ¬Ј „Щ„Х„Ю„Щ ¬Ј #14 / 87"). All stats persist to `localStorage[bloom_bot_state_v2]`; settings (speed/mode/board/autorestart/submitToLB) persist to `bloom_bot_state_v2`-paired `bloom_bot_settings_v2` вАФ closing the tab and reopening the bot resumes exactly where it left off (handy for video recording sessions). Cache buster bumped, BloomDebug API extended.
- вЬЕ **Admin-managed skin catalog вАФ DB-backed shop with add/edit/disable (May 2026)** вАФ user-reported bug surfaced a much bigger gap: Aurora skin purchase returned `invalid_skin` because the server's hardcoded `SKIN_PRICES` map ([server.js:5523](server.js#L5523)) never got the new id when Aurora shipped. The security pattern from May 2026 phase 1 (server-authoritative skin prices) was load-bearing вАФ client supplies only the skin id, server picks the price вАФ but the source of truth was hardcoded, so any new skin needed a code change. Two-part fix: **Phase A** added `aurora: 300` to the hardcoded map (5-minute deploy so existing shoppers could complete the purchase). **Phase B** replaced the whole hardcoded approach with a DB-backed admin system mirroring the dynamic-boards architecture:
  1. **New table `skin_configurations`** in [schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js) (idempotent CREATE + `INSERT ... ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING` seed of the 7 historical skins so existing players' shop catalog doesn't change). Columns: `skin_id` (immutable string id), `name` (display label with emoji prefix), `price` (рЯТО cost), `is_enabled` (show in shop at all), `is_sellable` (existing owners keep but new buyers see "„Ь„Р „Ц„Ю„Щ„Я „Ы„®„Т„Ґ" вАФ useful for seasonal skins that come and go), `definition` (JSONB: `{tiers: [{bg, fg, svg_key, name, emoji}, ...]}` вАФ 8 entries one per tier), `special_class` (optional body class trigger like `aurora` вЖТ flips `.skin-aurora-active` for bespoke CSS animations), `sort_order`, timestamps.
  2. **Server endpoints**: `GET /api/skins/available` (public, 60s `_skinsCache` mirroring the existing `_boardCacheByMode` pattern, only enabled rows), admin CRUD under `/<ADMIN>/api/skins` (LEFT JOIN `player_skins` to show owner counts on every list row). New helpers `validateSkinDefinition(def)` (enforces 8 tiers, each with valid `#hex`/`linear-gradient(...)`/`radial-gradient(...)` bg, hex fg, SVG key in the allowlist `circle/leaf/flower/flame/bolt/star/diamond/crown`, name + emoji length caps) and `validateSkinId(raw)` (lowercase alpha-num + underscore, 2-40 chars, must start with letter вАФ CSS-class-friendly).
  3. **`POST /api/player/buy-skin` rewritten** to query `skin_configurations` first; rejects `skin_disabled` / `not_sellable` with explicit reasons that the client surfaces. Legacy `SKIN_PRICES` hardcoded map kept ONLY as a fallback for the case where the DB seed hasn't run yet (fresh dev env). `POST /api/player/skins/declare` extended to accept any DB-known skin id via a single `WHERE skin_id = ANY($1::text[])` lookup, not just the legacy 7.
  4. **Client integration** in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js): `SKIN_PACKS` switched from `const` to `let` + new `applyServerSkins(serverList)` rebuilds it from the API response on boot, mapping each tier's `svg_key` string back to the matching SVG via the existing `SVG` dict. `syncBodySkinClass()` is now generic вАФ reads `pack.specialClass` and toggles `.skin-{class}-active` instead of being hardcoded to `aurora`. When the active skin disappears (admin disabled/deleted it), client auto-reverts to `classic` and persists immediately so the next page load doesn't try to revive a dead skin. Shop UI in `showSkinShop()` shows "„Ь„Р „Ц„Ю„Щ„Я „Ы„®„Т„Ґ" (disabled grey button) when `s.isSellable === false`. The aurora gate in [src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) was replaced with a new `loadServerSkins()` fetch вАФ the legacy `aurora_skin_enabled` config key is now redundant (admin uses the per-skin `is_enabled` toggle instead, and it works for any future skin).
  5. **Admin UI** in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) under рЯОЃ „Ю„©„Ч„І tab: new "рЯО® „Ч„†„Х„™ „°„І„Щ„†„Щ„Э" section listing every skin with per-row status pills (вЬУ „§„Ґ„Щ„Ь / вЬЧ „Ю„Х„°„™„® / рЯТ∞ „Ь„Ю„Ы„Щ„®„Ф / рЯФТ „Ь„Р „†„Ю„Ы„® / вЬ® special_class), 4 action buttons (рЯЪЂ „Ф„©„С„™/„Ф„§„Ґ„Ь toggle / рЯФТ „Ф„°„®/„Ф„Ч„Ц„® „Ю„Ы„Щ„®„Ф toggle / вЬО „Ґ„®„Х„Ъ / рЯЧС „Ю„Ч„І), and a "+ „°„І„Щ„Я „Ч„У„©" composer. The editor modal is a full form: `skin_id` input (lowercase only, immutable on edit), display name (with emoji prefix), price input, sort_order, special_class (free text), is_enabled + is_sellable checkboxes, and the centerpiece вАФ 8 tier-editor rows each with `<input type="color">` for bg AND fg, free-text `name`, `emoji` input (4-char cap), and SVG-key dropdown. A "рЯУЛ „Ш„Ґ„Х„Я „™„С„†„Щ„™ „І„Ь„Р„°„Щ" button pre-fills the 8 rows from the classic palette so the admin doesn't start from a blank slate. Live 8-tile preview below the editor updates on every input change. Delete with owners present blocks at 409 (`{error: 'has_owners', owner_count}`); admin sees a confirm dialog prompting `?force=1` (destructive вАФ owners lose the skin вАФ but documented inline). All mutations write to `admin_actions` audit log + call `invalidateSkinsCache()`. **Limitation**: the per-tier color picker is hex-only; gradient backgrounds (used by Aurora) can be set via direct PATCH or by editing the seed JSON, but not via the picker UI. Documented inline in the modal ("рЯТ° „Ь„®„І„Ґ gradient: „Ґ„®„Щ„Ы„Ф „Щ„У„†„Щ„™ „©„Ь „Ф-JSON"). Future enhancement: add a text-input alternative on each row, or build a gradient composer. Cache buster `v20260523f`, SW `bloom-v9.0`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 5 Board Shapes (May 2026)** вАФ completes the original 6-phase BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md spec for shapes. The 4√Ч6 grid stays physically rectangular (no fitGrid changes, no layout breakage) вАФ instead, a `definition.shape_id` masks some cells as `inactive` (visual voids + engine walls). Allowlist: `['heart', 'diamond', 'tree', 'pyramid']`. Server validation in `validateBoardDefinition`. New `SHAPE_GEOMETRIES` registry in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) вАФ each shape is a 6√Ч4 matrix of 0/1, parallel to the engine's grid. `isShapeInactiveAt(r, c)` is the O(1) hot-path check used by `findGroup`, `applyGravity` (treats voids as anchors like locked/frozen), `drop`'s landing scan, and a rewritten `isGameOver` that walks per-column finding the topmost playable row. Render in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) short-circuits inactive cells: appends a `.cell.shape-void` div and skips all the tile/special-cell branches. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): `.cell.shape-void` is `background:transparent; opacity:0` by default (truly invisible) вАФ when a theme class is also on the body, void cells get a faint holiday-colored tint so the shape silhouette stands out without competing with active cells. Admin: new shape picker dropdown under the theme picker in the boards modal (visible for `type='themed'`), with the 4 shape options. Cell counts after masking: heart 15/24, diamond 16/24, tree 18/24, pyramid 20/24 вАФ natural "smaller, more strategic" game length. The 4 holiday themed presets in the guide modal were UPGRADED to bundle their shape too: рЯТХ Valentine вЖТ heart, рЯЗЃрЯЗ± Yom Ha'atzmaut вЖТ diamond, рЯХО Hanukkah вЖТ tree, рЯНЈ Passover вЖТ pyramid. Preset previews redrawn with emojis showing the actual masked shape. `applyPatternPreset` now also threads `shape_id`. Cache buster `v20260522v`, SW `bloom-v7.2`.
