- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 3F+3G Locked + Teleport (May 2026)** вАФ completes the 6-cell-type roster from the original BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md spec. `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES = ['gold','bonus','frozen','electric','locked','teleport']`. **рЯФТ Locked**: blocks both drops and gravity (treated as anchor) until `gameTotalMerges >= unlock_after` (admin-set 1-30), at which point the cell flips `unlocked = true` and renders as regular. Unlock fires `triggerUnlockBurst(r, c)` вАФ a 30px рЯФУ icon scales up with rotation, a yellow flash radiates outward, and a "„†„§„™„Ч!" pill floats upward. Per-cell `unlock_after` validated server-side. `isLockedAt(r, c)` returns true only for still-locked cells. drop()'s scan adds `if (isLockedAt(r, col)) continue;` before the empty check. applyGravity treats locked as anchor (writes cursor jumps to `row - 1`). Locked cells are excluded from `reshuffleAllSpecialCells` вАФ they're the contract between board and player, can't move. **рЯМА Teleport**: a tile that lands on a teleport cell is relocated to a random empty non-special non-locked cell. The teleport cell itself stays (the next tile lands there too). Logic in drop() between gold-upgrade and pendingEvent: detect via `isTeleportAt`, pick uniformly random target, `grid[old]=0` + render + 280ms wait + `grid[new]=tile` + render with appearing animation + 200ms wait. `triggerTeleportAnimation` paints a purple рЯМА spiral that scales 0.4вЖТ2.5 with 720¬∞ rotation at the source (telSpiralOut), then a matching mirror spiral that scales 2.2вЖТ0.6 with -720¬∞ rotation at the destination (telSpiralIn) 220ms later. CSS `.cell.special-locked` paints a 45¬∞ diagonal grey-stone stripe pattern + a center рЯФТ that shakes ¬±8¬∞ every 4s. `.cell.special-teleport` uses a conic-gradient purple swirl + рЯМА corner spinning at 1.8s/rev. Admin: 2 new paint mode buttons (рЯФТ „†„Ґ„Х„Ь / рЯМА „Ш„Ь„§„Х„®„Ш), a new "„†„Ґ„Щ„Ь„Ф „Ґ„У: [5] „Ю„Щ„Ц„Х„Т„Щ„Э" input (1-30) that applies to all locked cells on the board (paired with the existing bonus-amount input), counter splits 6-way ("вЬ® N ¬Ј рЯ™Щ N ¬Ј вЭДпЄП N ¬Ј вЪ° N ¬Ј рЯФТ N ¬Ј рЯМА N"). Admin guide modal extended from 4-card grid to 6-card grid + 2 new collapsible detail sections (locked + teleport) + 2 new pattern presets (locked-tier-progression with locked row above gold corners, teleport-roulette with bottom teleports feeding top bonus corners). Cache buster `v20260522r`, SW `bloom-v6.8`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,995 drops / 8,828 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 3E Special Cells: Electric (May 2026)** вАФ fourth special cell type. Extends the merge-group BFS: when the search visits a tile sitting on an electric cell, it queues 8 extra positions (radius-2 orthogonals + diagonals) so the group can absorb same-tier tiles that aren't directly adjacent. Cross-board mega-merges of 5-8 tiles in one drop. `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES = ['gold','bonus','frozen','electric']`. New `isElectricAt(r, c)` mirrors the frozen helper. In [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `findGroup`: after the standard 4-neighbor push, an extra `if (isElectricAt(r, c)) stack.push(...)` adds the 8 radius-2/diagonal neighbors. `visited` keeps the BFS bounded even with multiple electric cells. After each successful merge, the side-effects block scans the group for any electric-cell position; if found, `triggerElectricFlash(group)` fires: every cell in the group gets `.electric-flash` (yellow inset glow + brightness 1.7√Ч + saturate 1.3√Ч for 500ms), and from each electric cell, 8 вЪ° emojis burst outward in cardinal + diagonal directions, each with its own keyframe (`ebFlyN/NE/E/SE/S/SW/W/NW`) translating 280-380% in the corresponding direction over 720ms with scale 0.3вЖТ1.1 and a slight rotation per direction. Cell ring CSS: `.cell.special-electric` with bright yellow inset border (`#F5C400 вЖТ #FFE65A`), 1.4s pulse loop (faster than other types вАФ "electric" feels live), and a `::after` вЪ° corner that crackles ¬±10¬∞/+15% scale at 0.9s. Admin adds 4th paint mode "вЪ° „Ч„©„Ю„Ь„Щ" with `CELL_PAINT_STYLES.electric` (yellow gradient #FFF4B3вЖТ#F5C400) + `PAINT_BORDER.electric = '#7A6100'`. Counter splits 4-way (`вЬ® N ¬Ј рЯ™Щ N ¬Ј вЭДпЄП N ¬Ј вЪ° N`). Tooltip frames electric as "the most spectacular" cell type and recommends 1-2 cells max. Cache buster `v20260522p`, SW `bloom-v6.6`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,081 drops / 8,999 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 3D+++ Board-wide Reshuffle + Mesmerizing Animations (May 2026)** вАФ extends the per-frozen 'shatter' relocate to ALL special cells with two new admin modes. Now `relocate_mode` allowlist is `['static', 'shatter', 'on_chain', 'on_merge']`. New behaviors: `on_chain` reshuffles every EMPTY special cell (gold / bonus / frozen-without-tile) to random new positions when a chain (вЙ•2 merges) completes; `on_merge` does the same after every single merge (max chaos). Cells with tiles on them stay anchored (a frozen-with-tile is still a puzzle; a gold/bonus that JUST upgraded shouldn't yank away mid-action). The reshuffle pairs each shuffleable cell with a unique random target via FisherвАУYates, mutates `_specialCells` + `_specialCellsByPos` via `moveSpecialCellInPlace`, re-renders the board, then plays a STAGGERED 110ms-apart fly animation for each cell. Each flight: a 26px type-matching emoji (вЬ®/рЯ™Щ/вЭДпЄП) shoots from old вЖТ mid (lifted 40px above to make an arc) вЖТ new while spinning 720¬∞ and scale-pulsing 0.6вЖТ1.4вЖТ0.8. Lands with a 4-spark burst at the destination, color-coded per type (gold sparks for вЬ®, mint for рЯ™Щ, ice-blue for вЭДпЄП). New CSS keyframes `specialFly`, `spArriveSparkTL/TR/BL/BR` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css). Engine integration in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `drop()`: snapshots `gameTotalMerges` before/after `processChains` to compute `_thisDropMerges`, then triggers `reshuffleAllSpecialCells()` 120ms later if mode matches (the delay lets the chain's settle-render paint first). Admin dropdown expanded to 4 options with detailed Hebrew tooltip framing `on_chain` as "the recommended sweet spot вАФ rewards skill". The row appears whenever any special cell type exists (not just frozen вАФ phase 3D++ had a frozen-only gate). Cache buster `v20260522o`, SW `bloom-v6.5`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,962 drops / 8,938 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 3D++ Frozen relocate (May 2026)** вАФ added admin-controlled "frozen cells relocate after shatter" mode for variable / non-boring frozen behavior. New optional `definition.relocate_mode` field on `special_cells` boards: `'static'` (default вАФ current behavior) or `'shatter'` (frozen cell jumps to a random empty non-special position after each shatter). Server validation allows the two modes; future expansion to `'roaming'` is straightforward. Client adds `moveSpecialCellInPlace(fromR, fromC, toR, toC)` in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) вАФ surgical mutation of `_specialCells` + `_specialCellsByPos` without re-sanitizing the whole list. Engine in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js): after `thawFrozenTile` finishes its 550ms shatter burst, if the active board's `relocate_mode === 'shatter'`, `relocateFrozenCellRandomly(r, c)` picks a random empty non-special cell and moves the frozen ring there; if no candidate exists (rare full-board case) the cell silently disappears. Visual: a top-of-screen "вЭДпЄП „Ф„І„®„Ч „І„§„• „Ь„Ю„Щ„І„Х„Э „Ч„У„©!" toast slides in + a concentric blue pulse halo at the new position helps the eye relocate the threat. Admin: new dropdown `вЭДпЄП „Р„Ч„®„Щ „©„С„®: рЯІК „°„Ш„Ш„Щ / рЯО≤ „Ц„Ц „Р„Ч„®„Щ „©„С„®` inside the special-cells editor вАФ only visible when there's at least one frozen cell or the frozen brush is selected. Tooltip frames `shatter` as the "most addictive" mode and recommends pairing it with daily. Cache buster `v20260522n`, SW `bloom-v6.4`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,005 drops / 9,000 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 3D+ Frozen polish (May 2026)** вАФ second pass on frozen cells after user feedback that the "hole below frozen tile" looked like a bug + the only way to clear frozen was a random bomb event (passive, not addictive). Two fixes:
  1. **Shadow indicator** on empty cells below a frozen anchor in the same column. `render()` in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) now walks each column top-down, finds the topmost frozen-with-tile, and adds `.frozen-shadow` to every empty cell below it until a non-empty cell. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): diagonal stripe tint + faint вЭДпЄП in the middle with a slow drift вАФ communicates "intentionally blocked by ice above" instead of looking like a bug.
  2. **Adjacent-merge thaw mechanic** вАФ turns frozen from "stuck until bomb" into a strategic puzzle. New state `_frozenThawProgress = {}` (per-game, reset in init), `checkFrozenThawAdjacent(mergeRow, mergeCol)` runs after every successful merge in `processChains` and increments any frozen-with-tile cell that's orthogonally adjacent to the merge survivor. After `FROZEN_THAW_THRESHOLD = 3` adjacent merges, `thawFrozenTile(r, c)` shatters: clears the tile, awards `FROZEN_SHATTER_BONUS = 200` points, plays sound+haptic, and fires a `.frozen-shatter-burst` overlay with 4 вЭДпЄП ice flakes flying outward + a `+200` blue badge floating up. The cell remains frozen (ready to freeze the next tile that lands). Render shows crack progression as `.frozen-crack-1/2/3` classes on the frozen tile вАФ visible cracks paint via `::before` linear-gradients, crack-3 shimmers as a "about to shatter!" warning. Admin tooltip updated to explain the new thaw mechanic. Cache buster `v20260522m`, SW `bloom-v6.3`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,985 drops / 8,924 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 3D Special Cells: Frozen (May 2026)** вАФ first cell type to change the merge AND gravity invariants, not just add a modifier. A tile landing on a frozen cell becomes inert: cannot be part of any merge group, and acts as a gravity anchor (it doesn't fall, and tiles above stack on top of it normally). Below the anchor stays empty (the anchor blocks gravity downward). Only a bomb event (existing) can clear a frozen tile. New `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES = ['gold','bonus','frozen']`. `isFrozenAt(r, c)` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) is the hot-path lookup used by BOTH the BFS and gravity loops. `findGroup` got one new line: `if (isFrozenAt(r, c)) continue;` вАФ treats frozen tiles as wrong-tier, so they're skipped both as seed and as neighbor. `applyGravity` got a new branch: when it hits a frozen tile during the bottom-up walk, the write cursor snaps to `row - 1` (the next slot above the anchor) so subsequent falling tiles land on top instead of overwriting the anchor. Validated by 3 standalone simulation tests (vanilla / anchor + stack-above / anchor + empty-below-blocked) вАФ all passed bit-exact. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): `.cell.special-frozen` ice-blue ring `#6FB7E0 / #B5D4F4` + animated вЭДпЄП corner; when `.filled`, a `::before` pseudo-element paints a white-blue frost overlay and the SVG gets `filter: saturate(0.55) brightness(0.85)` so the tile color visibly "ices over". Admin: third paint mode "вЭДпЄП „І„§„Х„Р" added; counter splits 3-way (`вЬ® N ¬Ј рЯ™Щ N ¬Ј вЭДпЄП N`); tooltip warns 1-3 frozen cells max (more = unwinnable). Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,046 drops / 8,994 merges / 0 floating tiles). Cache buster `v20260522l`, SW `bloom-v6.2`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 3C Special Cells: Bonus (May 2026)** вАФ second special cell type after gold. A tile merge whose survivor lands on a bonus cell adds the cell's configured `amount` to the score (admin sets amount per board, 50-10000). The framework now has two coexisting cell types, validating the multi-type paint UI. Server: `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES` grew to `['gold', 'bonus']`; `validateBoardDefinition` enforces `amount` for bonus cells (Number 50..10000, missing/out-of-range rejected). Client constants: `setSpecialCells` in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) preserves the `amount` field when sanitizing вАФ bad bonus entries silently drop (defensive, never throws). Engine: [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `processChains` checks `getSpecialCellAt(kr, kc)` right after `score += points;` вАФ if the survivor cell is bonus, adds amount and fires a mint-green "рЯТО +N" floating badge at the merge spot. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): `.cell.special-bonus` mirrors the gold visual but in mint (`#4FBD8B` / `#9FE1CB`) so the two are distinguishable at a glance. Admin: paint-mode selector at the top of the cells editor вАФ two pill buttons (`вЬ® „Ц„Ф„С` / `рЯТО „С„Х„†„Х„°`), one active at a time, plus a shared `„°„Ы„Х„Э [500] рЯТО` input that applies to every bonus cell on the board. Click a cell вЖТ paints with selected brush. Click same brush again вЖТ clears. Different brush вЖТ replaces (one type per cell). The 4 quick presets (bottom-row / corners / cross / clear) now paint with the currently-selected brush, so making "corners bonus + bottom-row gold" is two preset clicks. The cell counter splits by type: "вЬ® 3 ¬Ј рЯТО 4", turns red past 8 (total). Cache buster `v20260522j`, SW `bloom-v6.0`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,828 drops / 8,766 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 3B Special Cells: Gold (May 2026)** вАФ first cell-level board behavior. Boards can now have a `'special_cells'` type with a `definition.cells = [{row, col, type}]` array. Phase 3B implements one type: `'gold'`. A tile landing on a gold cell upgrades by one tier (capped at MAX_TIER = crown). New constants in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js): `getSpecialCells()` returns the array, `getSpecialCellAt(r, c)` is the O(1) hot-path lookup used by `drop()` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js). The per-mode init logic was refactored: `applyBoardToSession(board)` is a single helper that knows how to apply either `multipliers` or `special_cells` (and future types) вАФ every per-mode branch (daily / practice / dynamic / duel snapshot) now funnels through it instead of duplicating the type switch. Server-side `validateBoardDefinition` extended with full `special_cells` validation (4√Ч6 bounds, dedup by position, allowlist of types вАФ currently just `'gold'`, expand `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES` to add more). Visual: `.cell.special-gold` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) renders a breathing gold ring with a вЬ® corner marker, visible even on empty squares so players know where to aim. Admin: the `рЯФЃ „™„Р„Щ„Э „Ю„Щ„Х„Ч„У„Щ„Э` option in the modal is now enabled вАФ clicking it reveals a 4√Ч6 grid editor where each cell is toggleable, plus 4 quick-presets (`bottom-row` / `corners` / `cross` / `clear`) and a live "N „™„Р„Щ „Ц„Ф„С" counter that turns red past 6 cells (UX nudge вАФ too many golds breaks the game). Future cell types (`frozen` / `electric` / `locked` / `teleport` / `bonus`) extend the same framework: add to `SPECIAL_CELL_TYPES` on the server, add a branch in the engine handler, add a CSS class. Cache buster `v20260522i`, SW `bloom-v5.9`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 14,053 drops / 9,031 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 3 per-mode targeting (May 2026)** вАФ extends phase 2 from pure opt-in to per-mode admin targeting. Admin can now mark each board as applying to one or more game modes: **рЯОѓ Dynamic** (opt-in picker, original behavior), **вЪ° Practice** (free play; score skipped from leaderboard for fairness), **вЪФпЄП Duel** (snapshotted onto the duel row at creation so both players see the same board even if admin changes the active one mid-duel), **рЯУЕ Daily** (every player playing today sees the board вАФ same for everyone, so the daily leaderboard stays fair). Contest + challenge are listed but not wired yet (next round). New `applies_to TEXT[] NOT NULL DEFAULT ARRAY['dynamic']::TEXT[]` column on [schema.sql](schema.sql) (idempotent ALTER вАФ existing rows get `['dynamic']` automatically). New server helper `getActiveBoardForMode(mode)` + `sanitizeAppliesTo(raw)` + new public endpoint `GET /api/active-board/:mode` with per-mode 60s cache (invalidated on any admin write). Duel creation in [server.js](server.js) `POST /api/duels` now snapshots `board_multipliers` + `board_name` onto the `duels` row at creation time вАФ pattern mirrors the existing `difficulty_*` snapshot. New admin UI section in the modal "рЯОѓ „Ч„Ь „Ґ„Ь „Ю„¶„С„Щ „Ю„©„Ч„І" with 4 checkboxes; the daily one is wrapped in a pink-tinted warning box and triggers an explicit `confirm()` on save (it's the only mode that touches a shared leaderboard, so the admin must opt-in twice). Client integration: top of `init()` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) clears any stale multiplier, then each mode branch resolves its board (`fetchBoardForMode('daily')` for daily, same for practice, snapshot read for duel, restoration from `window._activeDynamicBoard` for dynamic). [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) `startDuelGame` reads `board_multipliers` from the duel row and applies it before the first render. The fairness guard in 11-game.js leaderboard-submit branch was extended: `practiceFairForLeaderboard = (mode==='practice') && !sessionDifficulty && !window._duelMode && !window._activeSpecialBoard` вАФ so practice with an active board never pollutes the global default leaderboard. The pill bar in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) lost its `mode === 'dynamic'` gate вАФ now renders for any mode whenever a multiplier is active. New `showSpecialBoardToast()` in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) fires at every game start when `window._activeSpecialBoard` is set вАФ gradient pink-orange slide-in pill at the top of the viewport with the board name + multiplier preview, dedup'd per board id so a quick replay doesn't spam, auto-dismisses after 3.2s or on tap. CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css). The admin board list now shows per-mode badges (рЯОѓ „У„Щ„†„Ю„Щ / вЪ° „§„®„І„Ш„Щ„° / вЪФпЄП „У„Х-„І„®„С / рЯУЕ „У„Щ„Щ„Ь„Щ) on every row so the admin sees at a glance where each board kicks in. Cache buster `v20260522g`, SW `bloom-v5.7`. Engine self-test clean (200 games / 13,991 drops / 8,861 merges / 0 floating tiles).
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 2 redesigned to opt-in mode (May 2026)** вАФ initial phase-2 build (commit 825095c) auto-applied any admin-activated board to every player on boot, which polluted the daily / contest / duel / challenge / default-practice experience the user already knew. After user feedback ("„Ц„Ф „Ю„Ю„© „Ь„Р „Ш„Х„С вА¶ „Х„Ь„Р „Ь„§„Т„Х„Ґ „С„Ь„Х„Ч „©„Ф„Х„Р „Ы„С„® „Ю„Ы„Щ„®") the model was flipped to **opt-in**: the admin still creates and schedules boards (`board_configurations` table unchanged), but the **client never auto-applies anything**. Instead, the home screen ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js)) shows a dedicated "рЯОѓ „Ь„Х„Ч„Х„™ „У„Щ„†„Ю„Щ„Щ„Э" entry вАФ but only when at least one board is currently in its schedule window. Tapping it opens a picker modal in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) (new file) that lists every available board as a card with type icon + name + multiplier preview ("рЯОѓ „Ю„Ы„§„Щ„Ь„Щ „Ґ„Ю„Х„У„Х„™ ¬Ј √Ч6 ¬Ј √Ч4 ¬Ј √Ч2 ¬Ј √Ч1"). Selecting a board calls `setColumnMultipliers(board.definition.multipliers)` and `init('dynamic', {fresh: true})` вАФ a new game mode added in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) that is practice-like (random seed, unlimited replays) but **never submits to any leaderboard** (`daily_scores`, `difficulty_scores`, `contest_scores`) вАФ the existing fair-leaderboard guard already excludes anything that isn't `mode === 'daily'` or a default-difficulty practice. Going home, or starting any other mode, calls `clearDynamicBoardSession()` so the next vanilla game has no leftover multiplier. The pill bar (`.col-mult-bar` in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) + [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css)) is now gated by `mode === 'dynamic'` AND mounted as a sibling between `#tier-bar` and `#grid-wrap` (no longer inside `#grid-wrap`'s flex flow), with `style.width` set in JS to match `gridEl.style.width` so the pills line up exactly with the columns below. Server gets a new `GET /api/boards/available` endpoint returning the full list (the old `/api/active-board` single-row endpoint stays for back-compat). Admin copy updated to "„Ь„Х„Ч„Х„™ „Ц„Ю„Щ„†„Щ„Э „Ь„С„Ч„Щ„®„Ф" (available for selection) instead of the old "„§„Ґ„Щ„Ь „Ь„©„Ч„І„†„Щ„Э" (active for all players). Cache buster `v20260522d`, SW `bloom-v5.4`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 1: Column score multipliers (May 2026)** вАФ first foundation of the Dynamic Boards System (see [BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md](BLOOM_DYNAMIC_BOARDS.md)). Behind the existing `getBoardRows()`/`getBoardCols()` abstractions, new `getColumnMultipliers()` / `setColumnMultipliers(arr)` in [src/01-constants.js](src/01-constants.js) вАФ default `null` (no-op). `pointsFor(tier, group, chain, col)` in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) now takes the survivor column and multiplies the base by `mults[col]` when active; when null it returns the vanilla score with zero overhead (validated by `scripts/test_engine.mjs` вАФ 0 regressions across 200 games / 13,966 drops / 8,905 merges). Single caller in `processChains()` ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) passes `kc` (survivor column, not drop column вАФ chain reactions can move across columns, and rewarding the *survivor* keeps the strategic choice honest). UI: `.col-mult-bar` pills above the grid show `√Ч6`/`√Ч4`/`√Ч2`/`√Ч1` with tiered visuals вАФ gradient-pink + glow for √Ч6, gold pulse for √Ч4, mint for √Ч2, dimmed for √Ч1; built in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) using design tokens (`--color-warning`, `--color-success`, `--shadow-glow`). A floating "√ЧN „Ґ„Ю„Х„У„Ф!" badge fires next to the merge cell on вЙ•2√Ч landings вАФ gold-to-pink gradient pill, 1.1s lifetime. Activatable today via devtools console: `__bloomDebug.setColumnMultipliers([6,4,2,1]); __bloomDebug.restart();` вАФ admin UI lands in Phase 2. Cache buster `v20260522a`, SW `bloom-v5.2`.

- вЬЕ Daily challenge mode вАФ Asia/Jerusalem date seeds, one run per device per day

- вЬЕ Tier-ladder "next piece" indicator вАФ horizontal row of all 8 tier icons with mini merge-points beneath each. Active tier is scaled up with a colored glow ring and its score un-fades to the tile color. After each drop a silent left-to-right sweep cycles through tiers 1-4 (`revealNextTier`) and settles on the chosen piece, teaching the ladder order through repetition.
- вЬЕ **Live contest leaderboard** вАФ while a contest game is in progress, the active player's score updates onto every other contestant's leaderboard view as a pulsing green pill, 1√Ч/sec via `pushLiveScore`. The pill is shown *in addition to* the accumulated total so the rank ordering reflects the projected end-of-game score.
- вЬЕ **Live spectator mode** вАФ players can watch any other contestant who's currently mid-game. Two entry points: (a) post-game from the game-over modal, (b) **mid-game** from the contest leaderboard screen (`showContestLeaderboard`) вАФ every row with `liveScore !== null` is `spectatable` (role=button, data-spectate-target/data-spectate-name), wired via a delegated handler on `#clb-board`. A top-level "„¶„§„Ф „С„Ю„©„Ч„І „Ч„Щ (N)" button shows when at least one live row is rendered. Mid-game entry calls `saveContestGameState()` then `stopLivePush()`, and on exit (`init('contest')`) resumes from the saved state. Watched grid + score + next-piece refreshes every 1s via `GET /api/contests/:code/live-state/:targetDeviceId`. Watching is cost-aware: the active player only POSTs grid frames (`/live-state`) when the server confirmed they have at least one watcher (`hasWatchers` in `/live-score` response). The spectator's `/watch` heartbeat (every 5s) carries either `lastFinalScore` or вАФ when paused mid-game вАФ their *current* in-progress score, so the watched player sees an honest "this watcher reached X" value.
- вЬЕ **Audience awareness** вАФ the active player sees a floating "рЯСБ N" badge over the board with the watcher count. Tap to expand a list of each watcher's name + last-completed-game score. Watcher heartbeat is 5s; TTL on the server is 10s, so closing a tab disappears the watcher from the badge within вЙ§15s without any explicit teardown.
- вЬЕ **Admin dashboard** at `admin/index.html` вАФ gated behind `ADMIN_PATH` (URL slug) **and** `ADMIN_PASSWORD` (HTTP Basic Auth). Includes DAU/WAU/MAU/D1 KPIs vs 2026 hybrid-casual benchmarks (40/20/7), 30-day DAU sparkline, 7-day funnel (visited вЖТ played вЖТ completed вЖТ returned-next-day), weekly cohort retention table (D1/D7/D30 per cohort), time-of-day heatmap (7√Ч24, Asia/Jerusalem), top-scores with z-score outlier flagging (threshold > 3ѕГ), contest management (PATCH endsAt/status/name, DELETE), paginated player list with drill-down + cascading delete, "what's happening right now" live view (from `contest_live_state` + `contest_watchers` filtered to 30s), audit log (`admin_actions` table), CSV export with UTF-8 BOM for every table. Reuses existing `cleanContestName`, `isValidDate`, and the rate-limit helper from server.js.
- вЬЕ **Visit tracking** вАФ `/api/ping` upserts `device_visits` rows on each page boot. Lightweight (~1 row/device/day), enables bounce-rate and accurate retention denominators.
- вЬЕ **Demo seeder** (`scripts/seed_demo.js`) вАФ populates 30 players √Ч 30 days √Ч 5 contests for screenshots/load-testing. Scoped to `device_id LIKE 'demo-%'` and contest codes `DвА¶DEMO`. Refuses to run if >1000 non-demo `daily_scores` rows exist unless `--force`. npm scripts: `seed:demo`, `seed:reset`, `seed:clean`.
- вЬЕ **UX Polish + Addiction Maximizer вАФ stage 39 (May 2026)** вАФ comprehensive polish round after 38 stages. The home had 156 infinite animations on one page = visual chaos that diluted focus. Three coordinated fixes:
  1. **Priority Calmer** ([src/80-polish.js](src/80-polish.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE, loads after all other 30s before 99-close). `TILE_PRIORITIES` array ranks every home tile by addiction priority: streak-danger=100 / pet-crying=95 / trophy-milestone=90 / guild-war-reward=88 / league-reward=86 / BP-claim=84 / ach-claim=82 / album-claim=80 / prestige-ready=78 / spin-available=70 / daily-deal=65 / starter-pack=60 / bundle=55 / pet-sad=50 / checklist=40 / guild-war-active=38 / rival-active=35 / passive tiles=4-25. `applyPriorityCalmer()` runs after `applyHomeVariant()` (monkey-patched into the existing window function), finds all matching tiles, picks the highest-priority winner, applies `.polish-spotlight` to it (gold-pink animated halo via `::before` pseudo-element) and `.polish-calmed` to everything else (animation-play-state:paused, filter:saturate(0.75) brightness(0.94), opacity:0.88). Re-runs at 800ms / 2200ms / 3500ms / 5000ms to catch tiles that mount late.
  2. **First-visit Micro-tutorials** вАФ `TUTORIAL_TEXT` dict maps tile IDs to 1-sentence Hebrew explanations (e.g. spin вЖТ "рЯО° „Т„Ь„Т„Ь „Щ„Х„Ю„Щ „Ч„Щ„†„Э вАФ „°„Х„С„С „§„Ґ„Э „С„Щ„Х„Э „Х„Ц„Ы„Ф „С„§„®„° „Ю„©„™„†„Ф"). `showMicroTooltip()` mounts a gold gradient balloon next to the tile with auto-positioning (flips below if too close to top, clamps horizontally). Per-tile dedup via `localStorage[bloom_tile_seen_v1]`. **Only ONE tooltip at a time** to avoid overload. Auto-dismisses after 8s or on "„Ф„С„†„™„Щ вЬУ" click. Re-show via `window.__bloomPolish.resetTutorials()`.
  3. **Unified loading spinner** вАФ `MutationObserver` watches body for new DOM, finds any element with text "вП≥ „Ш„Х„Ґ„Я..." and replaces with `.polish-spinner` (36px gold-border spinning circle). Consistent loading state across all 14 modals built across stages.
  4. **Admin Engagement Overview** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)) вАФ new section at TOP of рЯУК „У„©„С„Х„®„У tab with `.engagement-grid` of cards. Each card shows: icon + system name + stat number + status badge (вЬУ „§„Ґ„Щ„Ь / вП∞ „¶„®„Щ„Ъ „Ш„Щ„§„Х„Ь / вПЄ „Р„Щ„Я „©„Ч„І„†„Щ„Э) + auto-jump-to-section on click (switches tab + scrolls). Currently 4 systems: Trophy Road / Spin Wheel / Guild Wars / Rivalries вАФ extensible. Fetches all 4 stats endpoints in parallel via `Promise.all`. Solves "where is X feature in admin?" pain after 38 stages spread the addiction stack across 6 tabs.
  Cache buster `v20260523ad`, SW `bloom-v11.4`.
- вЬЕ **Trophy Road вАФ stage 38 вАФ Clash Royale pattern (May 2026)** вАФ the #1 retention mechanism in mobile games. Unlike League/Battle Pass, **trophies can GO DOWN** if you play poorly вАФ the fear of losing is the strongest dopamine driver. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_trophies` (device_id PK, trophies, trophies_lifetime, highest_trophies, current_arena_id, claimed_milestones JSONB, total_games, total_wins, last_change, last_change_at), `trophy_history` (BIGSERIAL audit log). 11 master config keys + 10 milestone pairs (`trophies_milestone_N_at` + `_gems`). Defaults: win (вЙ•500 score) = +15рЯПЖ, lose (<100) = вИТ8рЯПЖ, crown bonus +40рЯПЖ, personal-best bonus +25рЯПЖ. New-player protection: under 50 trophies = no loss. Safe floor 0. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): 8 visual arenas hardcoded in `TROPHY_ARENAS` (рЯМ± sprout/0 вЖТ рЯМ≥ forest/50 вЖТ рЯПШ village/200 вЖТ рЯП∞ castle/600 вЖТ рЯМЛ volcano/1500 вЖТ вЭДпЄП ice/3000 вЖТ рЯММ galaxy/6000 вЖТ вЪ° legend/12000). `_calcTrophyChange(opts, cfg)` is the pure calc вАФ score+tier+isNewBest+currentTrophies вЖТ `{delta, breakdown}`. `_trophyGrantFromGame(deviceId, opts, cfg)` is the atomic transaction вАФ row-lock, calc, UPDATE state, INSERT history, set per-game dedup key `_trophy:<deviceId>:<gameId>`. 3 endpoints: `GET /api/trophies/state` (returns trophies + arena + nextArena + milestones with claimed/ready flags + stats), `POST /api/trophies/grant-from-game` (rate-limited 200/hr, called from client game-over with score+tier+isNewBest+gameId), `POST /api/trophies/claim-milestone` (atomic claim with row-lock + JSONB array append + balance credit). **Client** ([src/34-trophy-road.js](src/34-trophy-road.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **dark-blueвЖТgold gradient** showing current trophies + arena + next-arena hint, gold-pulsing when milestone unclaimed. **Game-over hook** wired into [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) right after Stage 27 guild-contribute вАФ `grantTrophiesForGame()` fires fire-and-forget with score+tier+isNewBest+gameId, skipped for bots/skin-trials. **Toasts**: green `+15рЯПЖ` fly-in (up arrow + count) for wins, red `вИТ8рЯПЖ` for losses, plays soft tones + scaled buzz. **Arena promotion**: 1.4s after trophy toast, full-screen radial overlay with arena emoji spinning + "„І„Х„У„Ю„™ „Ь„Р„®„†„Ф „Ч„У„©„Ф! ¬Ј „Р„®„†„™ [name]" + 5-pulse buzz + soundMilestone(7). Modal: big arena header with breathing emoji + trophy count + last-change pill (green/red), next-arena progress bar, 3-stat row (highest/games/winrate), 10-milestone list (locked = greyed with "рЯФТ NрЯПЖ needed", ready = gold-pulsing with "рЯОБ „І„С„Ь +NрЯТО" button, claimed = mint), full arena ladder visualization. Integrated into Stage 35 home variants: 3rd-priority hot card in Carousel + Hero candidate when milestone unclaimed. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `рЯПЖ Trophy Road` section in рЯТ∞ „Ы„Ь„Ы„Ь„Ф tab вАФ 4-stat overview (active players, max, avg, total games) + top-30 leaderboard with рЯ•ЗрЯ•ИрЯ•Й medals + win%. New `GET /admin/api/trophies/stats` endpoint. Cache buster `v20260523ac`, SW `bloom-v11.3`.
- вЬЕ **Guild Wars вАФ stage 37 вАФ clan-vs-clan competition (May 2026)** вАФ Clash Royale pattern that boosted Supercell's guild retention 3-5x at launch. Auto-matched weekly competition between two guilds. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `guild_wars` (BIGSERIAL + 2 FK to guilds + window + 2 scores + 2 game counts + status + winner_guild_id + finalized_at), `guild_war_contributions` (PK on war+device, per-member score + games count), `guild_war_claims` (PK on war+device, atomic dedup). 6 config keys: enabled / duration_days=7 / min_members_active=3 / winner_reward_per_member=500 / loser_reward_per_member=100 / min_games_to_claim=1. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_runGuildWarMatchmaker()` runs every 6h вАФ finds eligible guilds (3+ members, no active war), sorts by total_score_alltime, pairs adjacent (power-balanced), inserts war rows with NOW + 7 days. `_maybeContributeToWar(guildId, deviceId, score, client)` is called INSIDE the existing `/api/guilds/contribute` transaction (zero client wiring вАФ automatic for every guild member's game-over scan-for-crowns hook). Atomic UPDATE both `guild_wars.guild_X_score/games` + UPSERT into `guild_war_contributions`. `_finalizeGuildWar(warId)` is idempotent вАФ picks winner by score (tie вЖТ no winner), flips status, fires push notifications to all contributing members (best-effort `setImmediate`). `GET /api/guilds/war` returns active war + my contribution + top 10 contributors + unclaimed reward; also lazy-finalizes any expired wars for the player's guild on read. `POST /api/guilds/war/claim` atomic transaction: row-lock contribution вЖТ verify eligibility (min games + winner status) вЖТ INSERT-or-fail claim вЖТ balance credit. Admin: `GET /admin/api/guild-wars` lists 100 most recent (active first), `POST /admin/api/guild-wars/match-now` triggers immediate matchmaker, `POST /admin/api/guild-wars/:id/finalize` force-ends early with audit log. **Client** ([src/33-guild-wars.js](src/33-guild-wars.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **purple-gradient** (gold when unclaimed reward exists) вАФ only mounts when in-guild + has active war OR unclaimed reward. Tile shows status text dynamically ("рЯСС „Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь„Щ„Э „С-N „†„І„Х„У„Х„™" / "рЯФ• „Ю„Р„Ч„Х„® „С-N вАФ „І„У„Щ„Ю„Ф!" / "вЪФпЄП „Ф„Ю„Ь„Ч„Ю„Ф „Ф„Ч„Ь„Ф!" / "рЯПЖ „†„¶„Ч„Х„Я!" when claim ready). Modal: optional reward card at top (gold-gradient for winners, silver for losers, with claim button вЖТ atomic claim вЖТ full-screen celebration with 7-pulse buzz + soundMilestone(7) for wins). Active war card: countdown, VS row with both guild emojis + names + scores + game counts, dual-color progress bar (green vs red), my-contribution highlight, top-10 contributors with рЯ•ЗрЯ•ИрЯ•Й medals + names + scores. Tips footer explaining mechanic. Integrated into Stage 35 home variants: 2nd-priority card in Carousel (gold when unclaimed) + #2 hero candidate in Hero variant (after spin wheel). **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): рЯЫ°вЪФпЄП Guild Wars section in рЯТ∞ „Ы„Ь„Ы„Ь„Ф tab вАФ 6 config keys + "рЯФД Match Now" button + scrollable wars list with status badges (вЪФпЄП active / вЬУ finalized) + winner + per-guild scores + "рЯТ∞ Finalize Now" action per active war. 6 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with Clash-Royale-pattern rationale + economic-math. Cache buster `v20260523ab`, SW `bloom-v11.2`.
- вЬЕ **Daily Spin Wheel вАФ stage 36 вАФ Coin Master pattern (May 2026)** вАФ single most addictive daily-return mechanic in F2P puzzles ($1B/year industry). One spin per device per day. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `daily_spin_state` (device_id PK, last_spin_date, current_streak, longest_streak, total_spins, total_gems_won, last_reward JSONB). 4 master config keys + 12 segment definitions (each = 6 keys: label, emoji, type, amount, weight, color). Default 12 segments: 10рЯТО(w25) / 25рЯТО(w20) / 50рЯТО(w15) / 5BP(w12) / 100рЯТО(w8) / рЯЫ°freeze(w5) / 20BP(w6) / рЯОБchest(w4) / 200рЯТО(w3) / 500рЯТО(w1.5) / 1000рЯТО(w0.4) / рЯПЖJACKPOT 5000рЯТО(w0.1). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/spin/state` returns canSpin + streak + last reward + 12 segments + bonus config. `POST /api/spin/today` is the atomic transaction: row-lock state, server-rolls weighted segment, applies streak bonus to gem rewards (+10%/day cap +200%), grants per reward type (gems вЖТ balance UPDATE, bp_xp вЖТ player_season_progress UPSERT, freeze вЖТ client-counter, chest вЖТ gem-equivalent), updates state with new streak (yesterday вЖТ +1, else вЖТ 1). All inside BEGIN/COMMIT. **Client** ([src/32-daily-spin.js](src/32-daily-spin.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **purple-gold gradient** (Coin Master vibe) with `рЯО°` icon that auto-tilts every 4s, breathing pulse when canSpin. Click вЖТ modal with: streak card (when streak вЙ• 1) showing рЯФ• + bonus%, **SVG wheel** (12 colored segments + emoji + label per segment + pointer at top + spinning gold center), spin button. **Animation choreography**: click вЖТ `_spinning = true` вЖТ POST вЖТ on response, calculate target rotation = `-(idx + 0.5) √Ч 30¬∞ - 5 √Ч 360¬∞` (5 full turns + decel to target) вЖТ CSS transition with `cubic-bezier(0.17, 0.67, 0.21, 0.99)` over 4.2s вЖТ tick sounds at 300ms intervals during spin вЖТ reveal overlay with reward card. **4-tier reward card**: `small` (<100) / `big` (100-499) / `huge` (500-999) / `jackpot` (5000+). Jackpot card has continuous gold-glow animation + 32-particle confetti burst + 7-pulse buzz + soundMilestone(7). Each tier gets scaled confetti count + scaled buzz pattern. Streak bonus rendered as red-orange "рЯФ• +N%" pill. **Integrated into Stage 35 home variants**: top-priority card in Carousel + #1 candidate signal in Hero (when canSpin). **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): `рЯО° „Т„Ь„Т„Ь „Щ„Х„Ю„Щ / Spin Wheel` section in рЯТ∞ „Ы„Ь„Ы„Ь„Ф tab with 4-stat overview (total spins / 7-day active / total gems / longest streak). 12 segment definitions editable via the generic "„Ы„Ь „Ф„Ф„Т„У„®„Х„™" config table. New `GET /admin/api/spin/stats` endpoint. Cache buster `v20260523aa`, SW `bloom-v11.1`.
- вЬЕ **Home Variants A/B вАФ stage 35 вАФ 4 home layouts pickable from admin (May 2026)** вАФ solves the home-screen overload problem (the v2 home grew to 14+ tiles after stages 17-34, classic mobile cognitive-load territory). Admin picks ONE layout globally via `game_config.home_variant`. **Architecture**: pure decorator pattern in [src/31-home-variants.js](src/31-home-variants.js) (NEW FILE in own IIFE) вАФ `applyHomeVariant()` is called at the end of `showHomeV2()` after a 3.4s delay (waits for all `maybeShow*Tile` deferred mounts to settle), then re-arranges DOM based on variant. Every tile's own logic stays untouched вАФ variants only hide / move / wrap. **4 variants**: (1) рЯУЇ **standard** вАФ no-op, current v2 behavior; (2) рЯО† **carousel** вАФ adds a horizontally-scrolling "рЯФ• „Ч„Э „Ґ„Ы„©„Щ„Х" row at the top with 3-6 cards derived from active tiles (Battle Pass claim ready / league reward / pet crying / daily deal / etc.), each card clicks through to the underlying tile via a stable selector вЖТ `el.click()` map. `.hvar-carousel-card.hot` has a 2s pulse animation for time-critical cards; (3) рЯОѓ **hero** вАФ replaces the hero with a MASSIVE single-action card (60% viewport) showing the highest-emotion signal RIGHT NOW (priority: league reward вЖТ BP claim вЖТ sad pet вЖТ daily deal вЖТ bundle вЖТ boards вЖТ rival), with a giant black "рЯОБ „Ь„Р„°„Х„£" CTA that re-fires the underlying tile's click. All other secondary tiles collapse into a `рЯУВ „Ґ„Х„У N „§„Щ„¶„≥„®„Щ„Э` expander above the bottom links. Four hero theme classes: `hero-reward` (gold), `hero-urgent` (red, pulses), `hero-hot` (pink), `hero-neutral` (default orange); (4) рЯОУ **jit** вАФ Just-In-Time progressive disclosure. New players see only base CTA + pet. Tiles unlock in 5 waves based on `loadGamesPlayed()` against admin-configurable thresholds (`home_jit_unlock_games`, default `3,7,13,26`). When a tile is shown for the FIRST time, it gets a `рЯОЙ „Ч„У„©!` floating badge + `hvarJitUnlock` 1.4s scale-pop animation + `soundMilestone(4)` + buzz + scrollIntoView (staggered 1.4s apart). Per-tile first-show dedup via `localStorage[bloom_jit_seen_v1]`. Bottom-of-home teaser banner "„Ґ„Х„У **N „Ю„©„Ч„І„Щ„Э** „Ь„§„™„Щ„Ч„™..." with next-wave-content preview labels (e.g. wave 4 = "вЪФпЄП „Ь„Щ„Т„Ф / „Щ„®„Щ„С„Х„™ / „Ф„Щ„©„Т„Щ„Э") вАФ the prospective-FOMO punch. **Server** ([schema.sql](schema.sql)): 2 new config keys (`home_variant` default `'standard'`, `home_jit_unlock_games` default `'3,7,13,26'`). No new endpoints вАФ uses existing `/api/config` public endpoint (returns flat dict `{key: value}` so client reads `gameConfig.home_variant` directly). Admin PATCH `/api/config/home_variant` busts `_configCache` so changes propagate within seconds. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): new "рЯП† „Т„Щ„®„°„™ „Ю„°„Ъ „Ф„С„Щ„™" section at TOP of рЯОЃ „Ю„©„Ч„І tab (above existing config) with a 2x2 grid of variant buttons (active variant gets mint-green gradient + "вЬУ „§„Ґ„Щ„Ь" badge), plus a JIT-thresholds input with format validation (4 comma-separated numbers). Rich Hebrew tooltips on every variant explaining trade-offs + addiction rationale. **CSS** ([public/css/home-v2.css](public/css/home-v2.css)) appended ~150 lines covering all 3 non-standard variants with full dark-theme overrides. Body marker `data-home-variant="X"` lets CSS toggle base presentation per variant. Cache buster `v20260523z`, SW `bloom-v11.0`.

- вЬЕ **Guilds / Clans вАФ stage 27 вАФ peer-pressure retention (May 2026)** вАФ the biggest retention mechanic in modern mobile games. Industry data: +35% D30 retention, 3.4√Ч sessions/day vs solo players. **v1 scope** intentionally tight: create/join/leave + daily collective goal + per-member reward claim + leaderboard. **Skipped to v2**: real-time chat, clan-vs-clan wars, league tiers. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): 4 tables вАФ `guilds` (id, code 6-char UNIQUE, name, emoji, creator, member_count, total_score_alltime, max_members), `guild_members` (PK on guild+device, role, joined_at, score+crowns contrib counters), `guild_daily_progress` (PK on guild+date, goal_target/progress, is_complete flag), `guild_member_claims` (PK on guild+device+date for atomic dedup). 5 config keys: enabled / create_cost=500рЯТО / max_members=30 / daily_goal=30 crowns / reward_per_member=200рЯТО. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): 7 endpoints. `POST /guilds/create`: atomic gem-deduct + insert guild + insert creator as leader. `POST /guilds/join`: anti-cheat checks (already in guild, guild full) + atomic insert + member_count bump. `POST /guilds/leave`: deletes member; if last out вЖТ deletes guild; if leader left вЖТ promotes oldest member. `GET /guilds/mine`: returns guild + members (sorted by contribution) + today's progress + my claim status. `POST /guilds/contribute`: atomic вАФ bumps member counters + daily progress + checks if goal just completed (returns `justCompleted=true`). `POST /guilds/claim-daily`: server-side eligibility re-check + atomic UNIQUE-guarded claim + balance credit. `GET /guilds/leaderboard`: top-N by all-time total score. Admin: list + force-delete. **Client** ([src/28-guilds.js](src/28-guilds.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **royal blue + gold** (distinct from all other tiles). When not in a guild: "рЯЫ° „Ф„¶„Ш„®„£ „Ь„І„Ь„Р„Я ¬Ј „Ю„Ш„®„Ф „Ю„©„Х„™„§„™ + „§„®„°„Щ„Э „Щ„Х„Ю„Щ„Щ„Э" CTA. When in a guild: emoji + name + member count + progress bar + claim badge. Pulses gold when canClaim. **Join/Create modal**: two sections вАФ top input for join-by-code (auto-uppercases + monospace), bottom for create with name/emoji/description fields. **Guild modal** (when in guild): dark royal-blue header with emoji + name + share code + stats, goal card with progress bar + claim button, member list sorted by contribution with рЯ•ЗрЯ•ИрЯ•Й medals + role badges (рЯСС leader / в≠Р officer) + "(„Р„™„Ф)" highlight + contribution numbers, footer with рЯУ§ share code + рЯЪ™ leave. **Game-over hook** ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)): after pet XP grant, scans the final grid for tier-8 (crown) cells and calls `contributeToGuild(score, crowns)` вАФ server validates membership. **Toasts**: contribution shows "рЯЫ° +N „Ь„І„Ь„Р„Я ¬Ј 18/30", goal-complete shows huge celebratory gold "рЯОЙ „Ф„І„Ь„Р„Я „Ф„©„Ь„Щ„Э „Р„™ „Ф„Щ„Ґ„У „Ф„Щ„Х„Ю„Щ!". **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): `рЯЫ° „І„Ь„Р„†„Щ„Э / Guilds` section with 5 config keys + top-50 guilds list with medals + member counts + completion days + рЯЧС force-delete. 5 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with peer-pressure psychology rationale. Cache buster `v20260523w`, SW `bloom-v10.7`.

- вЬЕ **Smart Notifications вАФ stage 31 вАФ auto-personalized push scheduler (May 2026)** вАФ server-side scheduler that scans subscribed devices every 30 min, picks the highest-emotional signal per device, sends ONE personalized push. Differs from Stage 10 (admin broadcast): this is fully automatic + per-device. Both still work. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_push_state` (device_id PK, last_sent_at, last_send_reason, total_sent, last_scan_at). 6 config keys for cooldown/scan-interval/allowed-hours/batch-size. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_pickSmartPushFor(deviceId, cfg)` runs 8 parallel queries (each wrapped in catch to tolerate missing tables) and computes the highest-priority signal: **(1) Pet crying рЯШҐ** (>48h since visit вАФ guilt mechanic, highest emotion); **(2) Tournament ending рЯПЖ** (within 3h); **(3) Friend played today, you didn't рЯС•** (FOMO + social); **(4) Streak danger рЯФ•** (last play was yesterday); **(5) BP unclaimed рЯОЦ** (вЙ•5 rewards waiting); **(6) Comeback рЯСЛ** (3-30 days away); **(7) Daily Special рЯМЯ** (after 14:00 if not played today). All messages personalized with player name + specifics. `_runSmartPushScan()` is the scheduler loop вАФ runs every `smart_push_scan_minutes` (30 default) ONLY during 9:00-22:00 Asia/Jerusalem hours. Per-device cooldown 12h. Marks `last_scan_at` even when no push sent so we spread load. `_startSmartPushScheduler()` fires after 60s boot delay. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): new `рЯ§Ц „Ф„™„®„Р„Х„™ „Ч„Ы„Ю„Х„™ „Р„Х„Ш„Х„Ю„Ш„Щ„Х„™` section with 6 config keys + live stats (subscribers, sent in 24h/7d, total ever, reason breakdown by category) + "рЯФД „°„®„Х„І „Ґ„Ы„©„Щ„Х" manual trigger + recent-30-sends table with emoji-coded reasons. 6 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries. Public `GET /api/smart-push/preview` shows what would be sent for any device (debug). Cache buster `v20260523u`, SW `bloom-v10.5`.
- вЬЕ **Lifetime Progression вАФ stage 30 вАФ Call of Duty Prestige (May 2026)** вАФ the longest meta-arc in the game. NEVER resets between seasons. Up to 10 в≠Р stars on profile = permanent prestige badge. **Architecture insight**: XP is **computed server-side** from aggregate of existing player activity вАФ no new XP grants, no schema migrations of existing tables. Existing players are rewarded retroactively for accumulated history. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_lifetime_state` (device_id PK, cached_xp, prestige_count 0-10, last_prestige_at, cosmetic_unlocks JSONB, current_title). 4 config keys. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_computeLifetimeXp(deviceId)` aggregates from 8 sources via parallel queries (each wrapped in catch so missing tables don't break the calc): daily/difficulty/dynamic-board scores √Ч10, achievements √Ч75, total_earned√Ј2, album cells √Ч25, gacha pulls √Ч5, pet level √Ч50, season XP-derived tier √Ч100, friendships √Ч200. `GET /api/lifetime/state` returns `{level, prestigeCount, xpThisRun, xpToNext, title, canPrestige, prestigeReward}`. `_lifetimeTitleForLevel(level, prestige)` maps to Hebrew titles ("рЯМ± „Ю„™„Ч„Щ„Ь" вЖТ "рЯМЯ „Р„Т„У„Ф „Р„Щ„†„°„Х„§„Щ„™"). `POST /api/lifetime/prestige` is the atomic claim: re-verifies eligibility (levelвЙ•100), bumps prestige_count, credits 5000рЯТО reward. **Client** ([src/26-lifetime.js](src/26-lifetime.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home tile in **dark purple-gold** to stand apart from other tiles (royal/premium vibe). Shows в≠Рв≠Рв≠Р stars + level + title + progress bar. When can-prestige: tile pulses gold with shadow. Modal: 3-column header (stars / huge level number / title), big progress bar, **XP sources breakdown** ("how do I earn XP?") explaining all 8 sources, prestige card. Prestige action: confirm() вЖТ atomic POST вЖТ **full-screen celebration** with stars + sparkle (yellow-red gradient card, 7-pulse buzz). **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `в≠Р „§„®„Х„Т„®„° „Ч„Щ„Щ„Э / Prestige` section + 4 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries explaining the aggregate formula. Cache buster `v20260523t`, SW `bloom-v10.4`.
- вЬЕ **Tile Collection Album вАФ stage 29 вАФ Genshin-style completionism (May 2026)** вАФ visual album with 8 tiers √Ч N dynamic boards. Activates completionist drive at a different granularity than achievements (potentially hundreds of cells across many boards). **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_tile_collection` (`(device_id, board_id, tier)` PK with CHECK 1-8) for cell ownership. `player_collection_claims` (BIGSERIAL + UNIQUE on `(device_id, claim_type, target_id)`) for atomic dedup of completion rewards. 4 config keys. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `POST /api/album/record` accepts `(boardId, maxTier)` and bulk-inserts tiles 1..maxTier with ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING (collecting tier T also collects lower tiers). `GET /api/album/state` aggregates: active board list √Ч per-tier collection status + computed completion flags + claim status + reward amounts. Returns `unclaimedBoardCount + unclaimedTierCount` for the home badge. `POST /api/album/claim` is the atomic transaction with server-side eligibility re-verification + balance credit + UNIQUE-guarded claim insert. **Client** ([src/25-album.js](src/25-album.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): hooked into the dynamic-mode game-over branch in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) вАФ fires `recordAlbumProgress(boardId, highestTier)` after every game. Fires "рЯУФ +N „™„Р„Щ„Э „Ч„У„©„Щ„Э" toast for new collections. Home tile: indigo-teal with progress bar + "рЯОБ N" badge when there's something to claim (pulses orange when claimable). Album modal: header with 3 stats (collected/% complete/рЯОБ to claim), tier-complete rows at top with mini progress bars + claim buttons, then per-board list with name + claim button + 8-cell grid (indigo when collected, greyed when locked). All claim actions atomic with sound + buzz + balance update + cache invalidation. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `рЯУФ „Р„Ь„С„Х„Э „Р„®„Щ„Ч„Щ„Э` section with 4 config keys (enabled, show_on_home, reward_per_board, reward_per_tier) + 4 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries. Cache buster `v20260523s`, SW `bloom-v10.3`.
- вЬЕ **Achievement-driven Cross-Leaderboard вАФ stage 16 вАФ new competitive axis (May 2026)** вАФ global ranking by NUMBER of achievements unlocked (not score). Rewards completionists / breadth-players over single-board grinders. Until this stage, achievements lived only in `localStorage[bloom_dyn_achievements]` вАФ Stage 16 mirrors them server-side. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_achievements` table with `BIGSERIAL id`, `(device_id, achievement_key)` UNIQUE INDEX (handles dedup), recent-unlock and per-device indexes. Achievement keys are opaque strings вАФ client uses `cross:pioneer5`, `board:42:crown`, etc. 2 config keys: `ach_leaderboard_enabled` + `ach_leaderboard_show_on_home`. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `POST /api/achievements/unlock` (idempotent via ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING, validates key against `/^[a-z0-9_:-]+$/`). `POST /api/achievements/sync` for bulk-backfill from localStorage (capped at 500 keys per call, 10/hr rate limit). `GET /api/achievements/leaderboard?limit=50` returns top-N players with LEFT JOINs to `player_profiles` for name/country/player_code (fallback to most-recent `daily_scores` name). Includes "me" row + my-rank computation via `COUNT(*) WHERE count > my_count + 1`. `GET /api/achievements/me` for lightweight count + rank lookup. **Client** ([src/24-ach-leaderboard.js](src/24-ach-leaderboard.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): on boot, reads localStorage state and POSTs bulk sync (one-time per session). `grantPerBoard` + `grantCross` in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) now also fire `serverUnlockAchievement` (fire-and-forget) so new unlocks are mirrored immediately. **Home tile**: gold-yellow `.ach-lb-home-tile` mounts only for players with 3+ achievements вАФ shows "рЯПЕ „Ь„Х„Ч „Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь„Щ„Э вАФ „Ф„Щ„©„Т„Щ„Э #14 / „§„™„Ч„™ 17 „Ф„Щ„©„Т„Щ„Э". **Modal**: gold-themed with рЯПЕ icon, my-rank pill at top (when I'm outside top 50), full ranked list with podium colors (рЯ•З/рЯ•И/рЯ•Й), country flags, "you" highlight. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `рЯПЕ „Ь„Х„Ч „Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь„Щ„Э вАФ „Ф„Щ„©„Т„Щ„Э` section with toggles + top-20 player list (read-only) + refresh button. 2 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries. Cache buster `v20260523r`, SW `bloom-v10.2`.
- вЬЕ **Limited-time Bundles вАФ stage 25 вАФ themed event packs (May 2026)** вАФ themed multi-day premium bundles for holidays/events (Hanukkah, Valentine, Black Friday). Stronger FOMO than Daily Deals because the window is multi-day (3-30 days) and the design is theme-specific. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `limited_bundles` table (slug UNIQUE, name, description, emoji, theme_color, decoration_emoji, price_gems, original_value for strikethrough, contents JSONB, starts_at, ends_at, max_purchases_per_device, sort_order). `limited_bundle_purchases` (BIGSERIAL вАФ supports max>1 with counted dedup). 2 config keys + 3 seeded bundles (Hanukkah 8-day, Valentine 14-day, Black Friday 3-day starting in 60 days). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/bundles/active` returns enabled bundles in their start-end window + per-device purchase counts so client knows `canBuy`. `POST /api/bundles/buy` is the atomic transaction: re-verifies window (anti-cheat вАФ not trusting client's claim it's active), checks max_purchases_per_device limit, deducts price + grants gems/skin/BP-tiers atomically (reuses gacha/starter pack patterns). Admin: 4 CRUD endpoints INSIDE adminRouter block. **Client** ([src/23-bundles.js](src/23-bundles.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home banners (max 2 shown) themed per `--theme-color` CSS variable вАФ Hanukkah=deep blue, Valentine=pink, Black Friday=charcoal. Banner shows emoji + name + discount badge + price + strikethrough + live countdown ticker (60s refresh). **Modal**: per-bundle gradient with **floating decoration emojis** (8 scattered рЯХО/рЯМє/рЯТЄ with stagger animation) вАФ the "this is a special event" vibe. Live countdown (1s tick), explicit scarcity ribbon, content rows, big "рЯЫТ „І„†„Ф „Ґ„Ы„©„Щ„Х ¬Ј 600рЯТО" button. **Welcome overlay** on purchase: gold celebration card with contents recap. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `рЯОБ „Ч„С„Щ„Ь„Х„™ „Ч„Т` section + bundles list with status badges (рЯЯҐ active / вП≥ upcoming / вМЫ ended / вПЄ disabled) + theme-color left border per row + total purchases/revenue stats. **3 one-click presets**: рЯХО „Ч„†„Х„Ы„Ф / рЯТХ „Х„Ь„†„Ш„Щ„Щ„Я / рЯФ• Black Friday вАФ each pre-fills the editor with appropriate emoji/color/decoration/price/contents/dates. Full editor with datetime-local pickers for start/end. 2 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries. Cache buster `v20260523q`, SW `bloom-v10.1`.
- вЬЕ **Pet / Mascot вАФ stage 28 вАФ Tamagotchi emotional anchor (May 2026)** вАФ virtual flower pet that grows with the player. The pattern that built a $10B Tamagotchi industry by itself. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_pet` table (device_id PK, pet_name, level, xp, last_visited_at, last_fed_at, last_petted_at + dedup dates, feeds_today counter, total_pet_count, total_fed_count). 8 config keys: `pet_enabled` (default true), `pet_xp_per_game` (15), `pet_xp_per_level` (100), `pet_max_level` (20), `pet_feed_price_gems` (10), `pet_feed_xp_reward` (50), `pet_feeds_per_day_max` (3), `pet_daily_pet_reward_gems` (20). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_petComputeMood` returns one of happy/neutral/sad/crying by hours since last_visited_at (<24/<48/<72/>72). `_petComputeStage` returns one of 4 evolution stages (рЯМ± sprout 1-5 / рЯМњ sapling 6-10 / рЯМЄ bloom 11-15 / рЯМЇ king 16-20). 5 endpoints: `GET /pet/state` (lazy-creates row, returns full state including computed mood + stage + xpToNext + daily action eligibility), `POST /pet/name` (one-time name set, 5/hr rate limit), `POST /pet/pet` (atomic daily pet вАФ dedups on `last_petted_date=today`, grants gems), `POST /pet/feed` (atomic feed вАФ checks daily limit + deducts gems + adds XP + updates level), `POST /pet/grant-xp` (called from game-over flow with gameId dedup via game_config key). All transactions atomic. **Client** ([src/22-pet.js](src/22-pet.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home widget shows pet emoji + name + mood + level + action dots (рЯТЧ/рЯНљ if available). **Pulses RED with shake animation when pet is sad/crying** вАФ the guilt-trip emotional pressure. Tap вЖТ naming overlay (if no name yet) OR full modal. **Naming overlay**: gradient green card with bobbing рЯМ±, input field, "рЯТЧ „Ф„¶„С „©„Э" CTA. **Pet modal**: huge 100px bobbing pet emoji + name + stage + xp progress bar (gradient greenвЖТgold) + mood-themed message ("„Ф„§„®„Ч „©„Ь„Ъ „С„Х„Ы„Ф „Ю„Ю„Ъ!" for crying) + 2 action buttons (рЯТЧ daily pet pink-themed / рЯНљ feed gold-themed) + stats footer. Pet/feed actions trigger animated heart/sparkle burst from the emoji (6-8 particles flying in circle pattern with stagger). Level-up triggers a slide-down toast at top "рЯОЙ „Ф„§„®„Ч „©„Ь„Ъ „Ґ„Ь„Ф „У„®„Т„Ф!". **XP grant** wired into [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) universal post-game block (NOT mode-specific вАФ every game contributes, so the pet grows from daily/practice/contests/duels/challenges/dynamic equally). Server dedups by gameId so the same game can't grant twice. Pet name skip allowed вАФ naming is a soft prompt, not blocking. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `рЯМ± Pet / Mascot` section under рЯТ∞ „Ы„Ь„Ы„Ь„Ф with master toggle + level/XP config + daily actions config. 8 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with addiction-psychology rationale ("guilt mechanic returns players day after day"). Cache buster `v20260523p`, SW `bloom-v10.0`.
- вЬЕ **Live Ops Calendar + Daily Checklist вАФ stage 26 вАФ anticipation engine (May 2026)** вАФ two complementary surfaces that activate completionist drive + plan-ahead anchoring. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `calendar_events` table for admin custom events (date, title, description, emoji, category, sort_order, is_enabled). 3 config keys: `calendar_enabled`, `checklist_enabled`, `calendar_show_days` (default 30). 3 seeded sample events (weekend triple-XP day in 2 days, gacha banner in 7 days, season end in 14 days). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/calendar/upcoming` aggregates from FOUR sources in one fetch вАФ custom calendar_events, tournaments (live + upcoming), daily-specials computed via FNV-1a hash for each of next N days, and season_pass_ends_at. Returns events grouped by date. `GET /api/checklist/today` returns 5 to-do items: free gacha pull (if claimed today), play daily special (client overrides via localStorage), daily deal (if bought today), daily quest (via `_earn:` dedup keys), maintain streak (via daily_scores + difficulty_scores + dynamic_board_scores). 4 admin CRUD endpoints inside the adminRouter block. **Client** ([src/21-calendar.js](src/21-calendar.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): **Daily Checklist tile** mounts at top of home (after lives widget) вАФ cyan-teal theme, "рЯУЛ „Ю„©„Щ„Ю„Х„™ „Ф„Щ„Х„Э ¬Ј 2/5" header, gradient progress bar, 5 clickable items (cyan with circle icon when pending; mint with вЬУ when done). When all done: "рЯПЖ „Ы„Ь „Ф„Ю„©„Щ„Ю„Х„™ „Ф„Щ„Х„Ю„Щ„Х„™ „Ф„Х„©„Ь„Ю„Х!" green theme. Top-right "рЯУЕ „Ь„Х„Ч „©„†„Ф вЖТ" button opens the full calendar modal. **Calendar modal**: vertical scroll of N days, each day a card. Today's card has cyan border + "„Ф„Щ„Х„Э" label. Each day shows colored dots for event categories + per-event rows with emoji/title/time/description. Categories color-coded: рЯПЖ tournament=red, рЯМЯ daily_special=gold, рЯОЦ season_end=purple, рЯО® weekend=blue, вЬ® gacha=pink, рЯУЕ general=grey. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `рЯУЕ Live Ops Calendar` section under рЯТ∞ „Ы„Ь„Ы„Ь„Ф with master toggles + events list (date pill + emoji + title + вЬУ/вПЄ status + вЬПпЄП/рЯЧС) + full editor modal (date picker + emoji + title + description + category dropdown + sort_order + enabled toggle). 3 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with addiction-psychology rationale. - вЬЕ **Lives / Energy вАФ stage 19 вАФ scarcity-driven engagement (May 2026)** вАФ Candy Crush pattern, **DEFAULT-OFF** (admin opt-in via `lives_enabled='true'`). Limited lives that regen over time + refill via ad/рЯТО/wait. **Scope**: applies ONLY to dynamic boards. Daily/practice/contests/duels/challenges remain unlimited вАФ intentional to protect existing UX. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `player_lives_state` (current_lives, max_lives, last_regen_at + 3 stat counters). 6 config keys: `lives_enabled` (default 'false'), `lives_max` (5), `lives_regen_minutes` (30), `lives_refill_price_gems` (50), `lives_ad_refill_count` (1), `lives_per_game_dynamic` (1). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_computeLivesNow(deviceId, cfg)` is the lazy-regen calculator вАФ reads current state, applies floor((now - last_regen) / regen_minutes) regen ticks, advances last_regen_at by the consumed ticks, returns clean state with `msUntilNextRegen`. 4 public endpoints: `GET /lives/state`, `POST /lives/consume` (atomic decrement with current_lives >= n guard), `POST /lives/refill-gems` (atomic deduct + reset to max + last_regen_at=NOW), `POST /lives/refill-ad` (per-gameId dedup via game_config key, +N lives). All with rate-limiting. When `lives_enabled='false'`, all endpoints return `{enabled:false, currentLives:999}` so client gates are no-ops. **Client** ([src/20-lives.js](src/20-lives.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): `maybeShowLivesWidget()` mounts a pink-themed hearts widget at the top of home (red breathing if 0 lives). Widget shows: вЭ§пЄПвЭ§пЄПрЯ§НрЯ§НрЯ§Н hearts, count "2 / 5 „Ч„Щ„Щ„Э", regen countdown ticker "вП∞ 14„У 22„© „Ь„Ч„Щ„Щ„Э „Ф„С„Р„Щ„Э". Click вЖТ out-of-lives modal with **3 refill paths**: рЯУЇ ad (mint), рЯТО gems (gold), вП∞ wait (close). All disabled when full. `ensureLifeForDynamicGame()` is the gate вАФ called from `startDynamicBoard`. Resolves true if life consumed or system disabled, false if no lives вЖТ shows modal. Live ticker decrements client-side every 1s for smooth countdown, re-fetches authoritative state when timer hits 0. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `вЭ§пЄП „Ч„Щ„Щ„Э / Energy` section with **prominent вЪ† RISKY warning banner** at the top + red ribbon next to the section title. 6 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with explicit "A/B test if you enable" warnings. Cache buster `v20260523n`, SW `bloom-v9.8`.
- вЬЕ **Skin Gacha вАФ stage 18 вАФ variable-reward Skinner box (May 2026)** вАФ the Genshin/Apex pattern that drives $4B/year in F2P cosmetics. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): 3 tables вАФ `gacha_pool` (admin-editable pool of rewards: rarity, reward_type, amount, skin_id, weight, is_featured, is_enabled), `player_gacha_state` (per-device pity counter + total pulls + free pull tracking), `gacha_pulls_history` (full audit log). 15 config keys: master toggle, name, prices (single/ten), pity threshold (50), 5 rarity weights summing to 100, free-pull toggle, featured ID + boost %, dup-to-gems %. Seeded with **17 pool entries** covering all rarities and all reward types (gems/skin/bp_tier/chest/freeze). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_gachaResolveOnePull` rolls rarity weighted by config вЖТ then picks reward weighted within rarity (with featured-item boost applied). Pity logic forces legendary+ when counter hits threshold. `_gachaGrantReward` handles all 5 reward types: gems credit, skin insert (with **duplicate detection вЖТ auto-convert to gems at 50% of skin price**), BP tier XP boost (advances N tiers in Season Pass), chest/freeze converted to gem-equivalent for v1. `_doGachaPull(deviceId, multiplier, isFree)` is the atomic transaction: deduct price вЖТ check free-pull dedup вЖТ resolve N pulls вЖТ grant N rewards вЖТ log history вЖТ update state. All in one BEGIN/COMMIT. 3 public endpoints (state, pull, history) + 4 admin CRUD endpoints (placed correctly inside the `if (ADMIN_PATH && ADMIN_PASSWORD)` block вАФ fixed the bug from stage 21). **Client** ([src/19-skin-gacha.js](src/19-skin-gacha.js) вАФ NEW FILE in own IIFE): home banner purple-cosmic gradient distinct from gold (BP/Starter) and red (Daily Deals). Modal shows: spinning рЯО∞ icon, pity card with progress bar + "рЯФ• „Ґ„Х„У 7 „Ь„Р„Т„У„Щ „Ю„Х„С„Ш„Ч!" hint, 5-rarity rate breakdown grid color-coded per rarity, featured-banner if any, 3 pull buttons (free/single/10x with "„Ч„°„Ы„™ 10%" badge), history link. **Animated reveal sequence**: click вЖТ dark cosmic overlay with spinning glowing orb (1.4s build-up with rolling text) вЖТ card pop-in animation per result (scale 0.3 вЖТ 1.08 вЖТ 1 with rotation easeOutBack), rarity-themed border + glow + emoji + name + pity/featured/dup badges, sound + buzz scaled to rarity (mythic = 7-pulse buzz). 10-pull = 10 cards revealed in sequence with counter + skip-to-summary button. Summary aggregates: per-rarity counts + total gems/skins/BP-tiers won + "„©„Х„С!" button that reopens the modal for chain pulling. History modal shows last 50 pulls with rarity-coded left-border + emoji + name + badges + timestamp. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `рЯО∞ Skin Gacha` section under рЯТ∞ „Ы„Ь„Ы„Ь„Ф with 4 logical groups (master toggles, prices, rarity weights, featured), full pool list with status pills + content summary + total-pulled-count, edit-modal with rarity/reward_type dropdowns + emoji/name/weight/enabled fields, вЬПпЄП „Ґ„®„Х„Ъ + рЯЧС delete buttons. 15 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with rich economic-math + addiction-psychology explanations. Cache buster `v20260523m`, SW `bloom-v9.7`.
- вЬЕ **Daily Deals вАФ stage 21 вАФ rotating daily offer (May 2026)** вАФ one deal rotates daily (Asia/Jerusalem) from an admin-managed pool. Anchoring psychology ("„Ч„°„Ы„™ 60%!") + 24h countdown + one-purchase-per-day-per-deal. **Daily-return hook** вАФ players open the app each morning to see "what's on sale today". **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): `daily_deals` table (id, slug, name, description, emoji, price_gems, original_value for strikethrough, contents JSONB, category, is_enabled, sort_order) seeded with **7 starter deals** вАФ `gem_starter` (50рЯТОвЖТ200рЯТО), `gem_bundle` (500рЯТОвЖТ1200рЯТО), `skin_deal` (200рЯТОвЖТfire skin), `bp_boost` (300рЯТОвЖТ1 BP tier), `chest_x3` (150рЯТОвЖТ3 chests), `freeze_x3` (300рЯТОвЖТ3 streak freezes), `mega_bundle` (800рЯТОвЖТ1000рЯТО+space skin+1 BP tier). `daily_deal_purchases` table with PK `(device_id, deal_id, purchase_date)` for per-day-per-deal dedup. 4 master config keys. **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `_dailyDealHash` FNV-1a hash of today's date вЖТ index into enabled deals. `_pickTodaysDeal()` returns the chosen deal + date, honoring `daily_deals_override_id` admin override. `_msUntilNextIsraelMidnight()` for accurate countdown. `GET /api/daily-deals/today?deviceId` returns `{ ok, enabled, date, expiresAt, msLeft, deal: {...with discountPct calculated}, purchased }`. `POST /api/daily-deals/buy` is the atomic transaction: re-verifies dealId IS today's deal (anti-cheat вАФ can't buy yesterday's/tomorrow's), checks not-already-purchased, deducts price with balance guard, grants gems/skin/BP-tiers/etc atomically, inserts purchase record. Returns `{ok, granted: {...}, newBalance}`. 4 admin CRUD endpoints for managing the pool. **Client** ([src/18-daily-deals.js](src/18-daily-deals.js) вАФ NEW FILE in its own IIFE): `maybeShowDailyDealBanner()` fetched on home mount, mounts a red-orange `.daily-deal-home-banner` AFTER the starter-pack banner (so starter takes priority). Banner shows emoji + name + discount-% badge + price + original-price strikethrough + LIVE countdown ticker (updates every 1s). Click вЖТ `showDailyDealModal` opens big card with: red `-N%` ribbon, animated icon, content rows per item type (gems/skin/bp/chest/freezes), price-row (big red current + grey strikethrough), buy button. Live countdown in modal too вАФ auto-disables buy button when expired. On buy success: local balance + skin cache + BP status update, `soundMilestone(5)` + buzz, full-screen welcome celebration overlay. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `рЯФ• Daily Deals` section under рЯТ∞ „Ы„Ь„Ы„Ь„Ф with master toggles + deals list (status pill + name + emoji + price + content summary + today/total purchase count + вЬПпЄП „Ґ„®„Х„Ъ + рЯЧС delete buttons). Click вЬПпЄП opens a full modal editor with all fields: slug (locked on edit), emoji, name, description, prices, contents grid (5 input fields for gems/skin_id/bp_tiers/chest_count/streak_freezes), category, sort_order, is_enabled toggle. Cache buster `v20260523l`, SW `bloom-v9.6`.
- вЬЕ **Starter Pack вАФ stage 20 вАФ first-purchase funnel (May 2026)** вАФ the single highest-conversion offer in F2P puzzle games (50-90% buy-through in industry data). Fires ONCE after a player crosses a score threshold (default 5K). 7-day countdown + one-time-only = strong loss-aversion. Pays out 500рЯТО вЖТ 1500рЯТО + a skin + 3 Battle Pass tier boost (~5√Ч ROI). **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js)): new `starter_pack_state` table вАФ PK on `device_id`, tracks `eligible_at` + `expires_at` + `purchased_at` + `dismissed_count` + `pack_contents` snapshot at purchase. 9 admin config keys (`enabled`, `name`, `price_gems`, `price_usd`, `trigger_score`, `expires_hours`, `reward_gems`, `reward_skin_id`, `reward_bp_tiers`). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/player/starter-pack/status?deviceId&score` вАФ first checks if the row exists (creates on first call), if `eligible_at` is null AND `score >= trigger_score` stamps `eligible_at = NOW()` + `expires_at = NOW() + N hours`. Returns `{available, expiresAt, priceGems, rewardGems, rewardBpTiers, rewardSkinId, name, dismissedCount}`. Short-circuits `{purchased: true}` if already bought. `POST /api/player/starter-pack/buy` is the atomic transaction вАФ server re-verifies eligibility (not trusting client), deducts price from balance with balance-guarded UPDATE, credits reward_gems, INSERTs the skin (idempotent), computes XP boost to push the player up `reward_bp_tiers` tiers in Battle Pass (reads tier thresholds, calculates the gap to `current_tier + N`, upserts the boost), stamps `purchased_at` + snapshots `pack_contents`. All in one transaction вАФ any failure rolls back. Returns `{ok, newBalance, ...rewards}`. `POST /dismiss` increments a counter for telemetry (player keeps closing the banner вАФ admin can see dismiss rate). Rate-limited: status no limit, buy 5/hr, dismiss 30/hr. **Client** ([src/17-starter-pack.js](src/17-starter-pack.js) вАФ NEW FILE in its own IIFE): `maybeOfferStarterPack(scoreOverride)` is the public entry вАФ throttled 1/min internally, fetches status with the player's best score, and if `available=true` mounts a `.starter-pack-home-banner` at the TOP of `#home-screen-v2`. Banner: рЯОБ swinging icon + name + perks line (`1500рЯТО + „°„І„Щ„Я + 3 „У„®„Т„Х„™ BP`) + live countdown pill (`вП∞ 6„Щ 22„©`) + gold "„§„™„Ч вЖТ" CTA + √Ч close. Click banner OR CTA вЖТ `showStarterPackModal(data)` вАФ full-screen overlay with: red "„Ч„У-„§„Ґ„Ю„Щ„™ ¬Ј вП∞ 6„Щ 22„©" ribbon (loss-aversion stamp), giant рЯОБ icon, contents list (3 items: gems / skin / BP tiers), value calculation card showing `~2400рЯТО` total vs `500рЯТО` price = `„Ч„°„Ы„™ 79%` (anchoring psychology), giant gold "вЬ® „І„†„Ф „Ґ„Ы„©„Щ„Х ¬Ј 500рЯТО" button. Disabled state when balance insufficient: shows `рЯТО „Ч„°„® NрЯТО` instead. Buy вЖТ `confirm` вЖТ POST вЖТ on success: local balance + skin cache update, `soundMilestone(6)` + buzz, full-screen `showStarterPackWelcomeOverlay` (spinning рЯОБ, "„™„Х„У„Ф!", contents recap). **Trigger** ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)): game-over branch fires `maybeOfferStarterPack(score)` BEFORE the over-screen renders so the server can stamp eligibility with this game's score. Skipped for bot/skin-trial games. **Home mount** ([src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js)): also fires `maybeOfferStarterPack()` 800ms after mount вАФ so a returning player who closed the banner sees it again next session (within the 7-day window). **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): dedicated `рЯОБ Starter Pack` section under рЯТ∞ „Ы„Ь„Ы„Ь„Ф tab with 4 logical groups (master + naming, pricing, trigger conditions, pack contents) + 9 new TIPS_PER_KEY entries with detailed economic-math examples. Cache buster `v20260523k`, SW `bloom-v9.5`.
- вЬЕ **Premium Battle Pass вАФ stage 17 вАФ the #1 monetization driver (May 2026)** вАФ dual-track Battle Pass with paid premium tier вАФ the highest-revenue feature in modern F2P (Fortnite, Apex, Genshin all use this exact pattern). **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql) + [db.js](db.js) migrations array): 3 new columns on `player_season_progress` (`is_premium BOOLEAN` / `premium_purchased_at TIMESTAMPTZ` / `claimed_premium_tiers JSONB`); 3 master config keys (`season_pass_premium_enabled` default `'true'` / `_price_gems` default `'1500'` / `_price_usd` default `'4.99'`); 20 premium reward keys `season_tier_<N>_premium_reward` seeded at exactly √Ч2 the free reward (sum ~32,000рЯТО/season premium vs ~16,000рЯТО free). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): `buildSeasonTiers` now emits `premiumReward` per tier (falls back to `reward √Ч 2` when key missing). `/api/player/season/status` returns `isPremium` + `claimedPremiumTiers` + `premiumEnabled` + `premiumPriceGems` + `premiumPriceUsd`; `unclaimedCount` double-counts when premium owned (so a player who crossed tier 5 with premium and claimed nothing sees `10 рЯОБ`). `/api/player/season/claim-tier` accepts new `track` field (`'free'` | `'premium'`) вАФ gates premium claims on `is_premium=true`, dedups per-track via `claimed_premium_tiers`, returns both arrays so the client can update state. **New endpoint** `POST /api/player/season/buy-premium`: atomic balance deduct + flip `is_premium` in a single transaction (no orphan debits possible). Returns `{ok, price, newBalance}` on success or `{ok:false, reason:'insufficient_funds', price, balance}` for UI hint. Rate-limited 10/hr. Already-premium returns idempotent `{ok:false, reason:'already_premium'}`. **Client** ([src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): rewrote `renderSeasonModalBody` to dual-track layout вАФ each tier now shows TWO buttons side-by-side (mint free + gold premium). When premium NOT owned: premium buttons render as a `.dyn-season-track-tease` (dashed gold border, "рЯФТ +NрЯТО") for tiers the player has already earned вАФ **pure loss-aversion punch**. New big `.dyn-season-buy-banner` at TOP of modal with: вЬ® pulsing star, title "„©„У„®„Т „Ь-Premium Battle Pass", subtitle showing total premium gems available, **"рЯОБ NрЯТО „С-M „У„®„Т„Х„™ „©„Ы„С„® „Ч„¶„Щ„™ вАФ „Ю„Ч„Ы„Щ„Э „Ь„Ъ!" hint** showing exactly how much value the player is leaving on the table, and a big gold "рЯФУ „©„У„®„Т „Ґ„Ы„©„Щ„Х ¬Ј 1500рЯТО" CTA button. New `claimSeasonTier(tierN, track, btnEl)` signature passes track to server. New `confirmAndBuyPremium(btnEl)` вЖТ JS confirm() showing price + balance + total expected gems вЖТ POST вЖТ on success: `showPremiumWelcomeOverlay()` (full-screen golden celebration card with вЬ® spinning star, "Premium „§„Ґ„Щ„Ь!", auto-dismiss 8s). **Surfaces**: (1) Modal "вЬ® Premium" pill in header sub when owned. (2) Modal big buy banner when not owned. (3) Each tier card shows both rewards (gold one greyed/teased without premium). (4) Home tile: `<span class="home-v2-sp-prem">вЬ® Premium</span>` badge next to "„У„®„Т„Ф N" when owned. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): premium master controls section above XP rates (3 keys: enabled / price_gems / price_usd) with detailed Hebrew tooltip explaining monetization rationale + ROI math; 20-tier table got a 4th column "вЬ® рЯТО Premium" with gold-tinted input cells, auto-saves on blur/Enter; 3 new `TIPS_PER_KEY` entries with economic-math examples ("default 1500рЯТО вЖТ returns 32,000рЯТО = 20√Ч ROI"). The premium track is fully toggleable вАФ admin can disable via `season_pass_premium_enabled='false'` and the entire premium UI disappears (existing premium-owners keep their claimed rewards intact). Cache buster `v20260523j`, SW `bloom-v9.4`. **Stripe IAP wiring is stage 17b** вАФ currently the USD price is display-only.
