- вЬЕ **Daily Special Board вАФ stage 15 вАФ daily mini-event boards (May 2026)** вАФ the #1 daily-return hook in F2P puzzle games, ported to BLOOM. Every day at Asia/Jerusalem midnight ONE dynamic board is anointed as "рЯМЯ „Ф„Ь„Х„Ч „©„Ь „Ф„Щ„Х„Э" with **√Ч3 Season XP + √Ч2 quest rewards**. Deterministic pick вАФ all players see the SAME board today, but it rotates. Players who play it daily get massive Season Pass acceleration; players who skip a day feel the loss. **Schema** ([schema.sql](schema.sql)): 4 new `game_config` keys вАФ `daily_special_enabled` (master, default `'true'`) + `daily_special_xp_mult` (default `'3'`) + `daily_special_reward_mult` (default `'2'`) + `daily_special_override_id` (default `''`, lets admin force a specific board for today, e.g. Valentine on 14/2). **Server** ([server.js](server.js)): new `_dailySpecialHash(dateStr)` FNV-1a hash вЖТ deterministic index into the active dynamic-boards list. `pickDailySpecial(boardRows)` is the picker, `getDailySpecialForToday()` re-queries for the XP/reward branches. `GET /api/boards/available` now returns `{ ok, boards, dailySpecial: {enabled, id, xpMult, rewardMult, date, isOverride} }` at the top level вАФ single-fetch, no extra round trip. `POST /api/player/season/grant-xp` reads `meta.boardId` and when it matches today's special multiplies `xpGain` by `xpMult` (capped at `season_xp_max_per_game √Ч Math.ceil(xpMult)` so the daily can earn ~300 XP/game on default). `POST /api/player/earn` `dyn_quest` branch reads `meta.boardId` and multiplies the quest reward by `rewardMult` when the boardId matches today's special. Both are server-authoritative вАФ client never names the multipliers. **Client** ([src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) + [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): `window._dailySpecial` populated from the same `/api/boards/available` response that already runs every 90s. New `hasPlayedDailySpecialToday(date, boardId)` + `markDailySpecialPlayed(date, boardId)` localStorage helpers keyed on the date so it auto-resets at midnight. **Surfaces**: (1) **Picker header banner** вАФ at the ABSOLUTE TOP of the picker (above tournaments + season pass + quests): gold-pink pulsing gradient `.dyn-daily-special-banner` with рЯМЯ icon (rotating + scaling), board name in strong, 3 inline pills (`3√Ч XP` mint, `2√Ч „§„®„°„Щ„Э` mint, `„©„Ч„І „Ґ„Ы„©„Щ„Х вЖР` gold CTA). Tap = closes picker + immediately starts the special board. (2) **Picker card glow** вАФ the special board's card gets a `.daily-special` class with breathing gold border + box-shadow (`dailySpecialCardGlow` 2.6s keyframes), plus a unique gold-pink chip at the top of its chip row: `рЯМЯ „Ф„Ь„Х„Ч „©„Ь „Ф„Щ„Х„Э ¬Ј 3√Ч XP ¬Ј 2√Ч „§„®„°„Щ„Э`. (3) **Home button label** вАФ new `.fomo-daily-special` class with gold-pink gradient. Inserted into the existing priority ladder: `questClaimable > streakDanger > dailySpecial-unplayed > FOMO-countdown > streak-calm > default`. When the player hasn't played today's special yet: `рЯМЯ „Ф„Ь„Х„Ч „©„Ь „Ф„Щ„Х„Э: „Х„Ь„†„Ш„Щ„Щ„Я ¬Ј 3√Ч XP „Ю„Ч„Ы„Щ„Э!`. Auto-disappears after `markDailySpecialPlayed` fires on game-over. (4) **Game-over banner** ([src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js)) вАФ gold-pink `.over-daily-special-banner` immediately after the rank pill (above streak/ach/quest banners) with the celebration message "рЯМЯ „©„Щ„Ч„І„™ „Р„™ „Ф„Ь„Х„Ч „©„Ь „Ф„Щ„Х„Э! ¬Ј „І„Щ„С„Ь„™ **3√Ч XP** + **2√Ч „§„®„°„Щ„Э** „Ґ„Ь „Ф„Ю„©„Ч„І „Ф„Ц„Ф". CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css) with full dark-theme overrides. **Admin** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): 4 new `TIPS_PER_KEY` entries with economic-math examples + 2 new `PRESETS_PER_KEY` chip lists (`daily_special_xp_mult: [1.5, 2, 3, 4, 5]` / `daily_special_reward_mult: [1.5, 2, 2.5, 3]`). The `daily_special_override_id` field stays free-text since it's a numeric board id. Cache buster `v20260523g`, SW `bloom-v9.1`.
- вЬЕ **Daily Login Multiplier Stack вАФ stage 14 вАФ prospective FOMO via breakdown rows (May 2026)** вАФ the existing daily-login bonus already had streak tiers (15вЖТ200рЯТО for 1вЖТ30 day streaks), but it was a black box: the player saw `+50рЯТО` and didn't understand why. Now the overlay shows a **breakdown table** with one row per multiplier source, **active rows in mint** (вЬУ unlocked) and **locked rows in dashed grey** (рЯФТ with a "do X to unlock" hint). 4 new admin config keys: `daily_login_mult_dyn_streak_pct` (default +25%) + `_min` (default 3 dyn-streak days) + `_friend_shared_pct` (default +20%) + `_max_pct` (default 300% cap). **Server** in [server.js](server.js) `/api/player/earn` `daily_login` branch now reads `meta.dynStreak` + `meta.friendSharedYesterday` and stacks the multipliers on top of the tier base, capped at `_max_pct`. Returns a `breakdown: { base, baseTier, totalPct, cappedAtPct, breakdown: [{label, factor, contribution}], finalReward }` object so the client can paint the math transparently. **Client** in [src/08-contest-helpers.js](src/08-contest-helpers.js): `earnCredits('daily_login', ...)` now passes `dynStreak` (from `getDynamicStreak()`) + `friendSharedYesterday` (true if any cached friend has `playedToday`).
