The pink CTA row is the prospective-FOMO punch вАФ a player with NO friends sees what they're leaving on the table. CSS in [public/css/viral.css](public/css/viral.css): `.dr-breakdown`, `.dr-mult-row-active/-locked/-cta` with full dark-theme overrides. Admin tooltips for the 4 new keys with economic math examples ("streak√Ч4 + dyn 25% + friend 20% = 145% вЖТ capped at 300% = 4√Ч base"). Cache buster `v20260523e`, SW `bloom-v8.9`.
- вЬЕ **Friends Invite + Shared Streak вАФ stage 13 вАФ the viral loop (May 2026)** вАФ every player has a `BLOOM-XXXX` code already (from `player_profiles.player_code`); now sharing it is the K-factor lever. **Schema**: `friendships` table with symmetric storage (PK `(device_a, device_b)` where `device_a < device_b` lex, plus `initiator` + `bonus_paid` flag) вАФ eliminates the "duplicate-friendship" footgun. `friendship_shared_days` for per-day shared-play bonus dedup (PK `(a, b, date)`). `player_daily_dyn_activity` tracker for "did this device play a dynamic game today?". 4 admin config keys (`friends_enabled`, `friends_signup_bonus` default 200, `friends_shared_day_bonus` default 100, `friends_max_per_device` default 50). **Server** in [server.js](server.js): `POST /api/friends/invite` resolves `friendCode` вЖТ `device_id` via `player_profiles`, validates anti-self + max-cap, atomic insert + dual-credit transaction + push notification to the invitee ("рЯС• „У„†„Щ„Р„Ь „Ф„Х„°„Щ„£ „Р„Х„™„Ъ вАФ „©„†„Щ„Ы„Э „І„Щ„С„Ь„™„Э 200рЯТО"); `GET /api/friends/list?deviceId=` returns each friend's name + code + `playedToday` flag + my own `iPlayedToday`. **Recurring shared bonus**: hooked into the existing `POST /api/boards/:id/score` flow вАФ `recordDynActivityAndPayShared(deviceId)` runs after every dynamic-board score is recorded. It upserts `player_daily_dyn_activity` for today + scans the player's friends for any who also have an activity row today AND no `friendship_shared_days` row yet вЖТ atomic transaction credits both + marks the day claimed. Fire-and-forget (doesn't block score submission). **Client** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): `fetchFriends(force)` with 60s cache, `sendFriendInvite(code)`, `buildInviteUrl()` produces `<origin>/?ref=BLOOM-XXXX`, `shareInviteViaWhatsApp()` opens `wa.me/?text=...`, `shareInviteViaNative()` uses `navigator.share` with clipboard fallback. **URL `?ref=` autohandler** runs 1.5s after boot: parses ref, dedups via `localStorage[bloom_ref_seen:<code>]`, skips self-invites (compares to own code), then pops the gold-pink gradient overlay "рЯС• „Ч„С„® „Ф„Ц„Ю„Щ„Я „Р„Х„™„Ъ! ¬Ј „І„Х„У „Ф„Ч„С„®: BLOOM-XYZW ¬Ј +200рЯТО ¬Ј „Ь„©„†„Щ„Ы„Э ¬Ј „Щ„Ч„У „Ю„І„С„Ь„Щ„Э +100рЯТО „С„Ы„Ь „Щ„Х„Э „©„©„†„Щ„Ы„Э „™„©„Ч„І„Х". Tap-to-accept вЖТ `sendFriendInvite` вЖТ milestone sound + buzz + close. **Friends Modal** accessible from new pink-gradient headline pill in picker header ("рЯС• „Ф„Ц„Ю„Я „Ч„С„® вЖТ +200рЯТО „Ь„©„†„Щ„Ы„Э" if empty; "рЯС• 2 „Ю-5 „Ч„С„®„Щ„Э „©„Щ„Ч„І„Х „Ф„Щ„Х„Э" otherwise). Modal has 3 sections: (1) **My code** with 3 share buttons (рЯТђ WhatsApp green / рЯУ§ Native share / рЯУЛ Copy link); (2) **Add by code** input with `BLOOM-XXXX` placeholder + monospace 14-char input + error states (`friend_not_found` / `cant_self_friend` / `max_friends_reached`); (3) **Friends list** with avatar circles + name + code + per-row "вЬУ „©„Щ„Ч„І „Ф„Щ„Х„Э" mint pill OR "вП∞ „Ґ„У„Щ„Щ„Я „Ь„Р „Ф„Щ„Х„Э" grey pill вАФ the social FOMO surface ("„У„†„Щ„Р„Ь „©„Щ„Ч„І „Ф„Щ„Х„Э, „Р„†„Щ „Ь„Р вАФ „Ф„Х„Р „Ю„І„С„Ь „Р„™ „Ф-100рЯТО „С„Ь„Ґ„У„Щ„Щ"). Cache buster `v20260523d`, SW `bloom-v8.8`.
- вЬЕ **Live Tournaments вАФ stage 12 вАФ scheduled prime-time community moments (May 2026)** вАФ admin schedules a tournament with `[starts_at, ends_at)` window + a top-N prize pool. Any dynamic-board game played within the window auto-submits the player's BEST score (best-score-wins upsert mirroring daily_scores). After ends_at, the **next** fetch of `/api/tournaments` lazy-finalizes: top-N players have their prize credited to balance in a single transaction + receive a push notification ("рЯПЖ „Ц„Ы„Щ„™ „С„Ш„Х„®„†„Щ„®! „Ю„І„Х„Э 1 ¬Ј 5,000рЯТО „†„Ы„†„°„Х"). No cron needed вАФ pull-based finalize keeps infra simple. **Schema**: new `tournaments` table (id, name, description, starts_at, ends_at, `prize_pool JSONB` = array of `{rank, reward}`, status, finalized_at) + `tournament_scores` table (PK `(tournament_id, device_id)`, best-score-wins upsert + per-player games_played counter + `prize_claimed` int). `idx_tournament_scores_lb` for fast top-N queries. **Server** (4 public + 5 admin endpoints): `GET /api/tournaments` lists live/upcoming/recent-ended in one call with lazy-finalize trigger; `GET /api/tournaments/:id/leaderboard` returns top 50 + my rank + prize pool; `POST /api/tournaments/:id/score` enforces the window + drops anti-cheat + best-score upsert; admin CRUD: list/create/patch/delete + manual finalize. `maybeFinalizeTournament(id)` is the shared helper вАФ atomic transaction: claim_prize + balance credit + status flip + push notification per winner. **Client** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): `fetchTournaments(force)` with 60s cache, `getLiveTournament()` / `getUpcomingTournament()` selectors, `submitTournamentScoreFromGame(score, tier, drops)` wired into the dynamic-mode game-over branch (auto-submits silently вАФ best score wins). `renderTournamentBannerHtml()` renders a red-pink-gold pulsing banner at the TOP of the picker header when a tournament is live (or a blue "вП∞ „С„І„®„Х„С" banner when one starts within 24h). `showTournamentModal(id)` opens a full leaderboard with рЯ•ЗрЯ•ИрЯ•Й podium, country flags, you-row highlight, prize-pool display, and "рЯПЖ „©„Ч„І „С„Ш„Х„®„†„Щ„®" CTA that opens the picker. **Admin UI** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html) вЖТ рЯПЖ „™„Ч„®„Х„Щ„Х„™ tab) new "„Ш„Х„®„†„Щ„®„Щ„Э „Ч„Щ„Щ„Э" section with table of all tournaments + status badges (рЯФі LIVE / вП≥ „Ґ„™„Щ„У„Щ / вП∞ „Ю„Ю„™„Щ„Я „Ь„°„Щ„Х„Э / вЬУ „Ф„°„™„Щ„Щ„Э) + "+ „Ш„Х„®„†„Щ„® „Ч„У„©" composer modal with: name + description + starts_at/ends_at datetime pickers + prize_pool freeform input (format `#1:5000, #2:2000`) + **3 quick-presets** (в≠Р Prime Time = today 20:00-21:00, рЯОЙ Weekend = next Friday 14:00-16:00, вЪ° Quick = +5 min for 1h) + manual "рЯТ∞ „°„Щ„Х„Э" button for early finalize + cascade delete. Cache buster `v20260523c`, SW `bloom-v8.7`.
- вЬЕ **Season Pass вАФ stage 11 вАФ the #1 F2P retention engine (May 2026)** вАФ 20-tier reward track that turns every action into progress toward a visible goal. Inspired by Fortnite/Genshin/Apex Battle Pass вАФ the single most addictive feature in modern F2P. **Schema**: new `player_season_progress` table with `(device_id, season_id)` PK + `xp INT` + `claimed_tiers JSONB[]` + `recent_game_ids JSONB[]` (per-game dedup buffer, trimmed to last 50). 4 master config keys (`season_pass_enabled` / `season_id` / `name` / `ends_at`) + 6 XP-source rates + 40 tier keys (`season_tier_<N>_xp` + `season_tier_<N>_reward` for N=1..20). Tier curve: 40 XP вЖТ 5,950 XP across 20 tiers, rewards 25рЯТО вЖТ 3,000рЯТО (sum ~16,000рЯТО per season). Easy early game ("first 5 tiers in day 1") + harder late game ("tier 20 needs 3-4 weeks consistent play"). **Server** (3 endpoints in [server.js](server.js)): `GET /api/player/season/status` returns `{xp, currentTier, claimedTiers, unclaimedCount, tiers, seasonName, endsAt}`; `POST /api/player/season/grant-xp` validates `source` against allowlist (`dyn_game_finish` / `quest_done` / `achievement`), recomputes XP server-side from meta (anti-cheat вАФ client can't claim arbitrary XP), dedups per `gameId` via the in-row buffer, caps at `season_xp_max_per_game`; `POST /api/player/season/claim-tier` atomic credit+claim in a transaction (claimed_tiers append + balance increment) so a player can never get one without the other. **Client** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): `fetchSeasonStatus(force)` with 60s cache, `grantSeasonXpForGame(gameId, score, tier)` called from the dynamic-mode game-over branch, `showSeasonPassModal()` renders the full 20-tier roadmap with claim buttons, `showSeasonLevelUpToast(tier)` fires 4.5s after game-over (after chest reveal lands) when player crosses a tier вАФ `soundMilestone(5)` + buzz `[60,50,90]`. **Surfaces**: (1) **Picker header headline** вАФ gold gradient pill at the TOP of the picker (highest priority) with current tier number + thin progress bar + "рЯОБ N „Ь„І„С„Ь" unclaimed badge that pulses when present. Tap вЖТ opens Season Pass modal. (2) **Modal**: gold gradient header with season name, top progress bar (XP toward next tier), scrollable 20-tier list. Each tier card: numbered circle (gold for unlocked, mint for claimed, grey for locked) + XP threshold + reward amount + status pill (locked / claim button / "вЬУ „†„Р„°„£"). (3) **Game-over level-up toast** lands AFTER the chest reveal вАФ choreography: rank pill (200ms) вЖТ personal best banner вЖТ chest animation (4.5s) вЖТ season level-up toast (4.5s) вЖТ fade. No surface overlap. Cache buster `v20260523b`, SW `bloom-v8.6`.
- рЯРЫ **Critical bug-fix: missing `updated_at` column + reward-clamp bypass + shop expansion (May 2026)** вАФ user-reported triple bug: (1) quest/achievement rewards announced NрЯТО but balance only went up by вЙ§10рЯТО, (2) `/api/player/streak-freeze/buy` and similar endpoints returning 500, (3) skin/powerup purchases failing intermittently. **Root cause A**: the chest, comeback-claim, and streak-freeze/buy endpoints I added in stages 8-9 all do `UPDATE player_profiles SET balance = balance ¬± $1, updated_at = NOW()` вАФ but `player_profiles` schema has no `updated_at` column (only `created_at`). Postgres throws "column does not exist" вЖТ 500. Fix: added `ALTER TABLE player_profiles ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()` to both [schema.sql](schema.sql) and [db.js](db.js) `initDb()` migrations array for belt-and-suspenders. **Root cause B**: quest/achievement/streak-milestone rewards all went through `earnCredits('event_gift', {amount})`, and the server's event_gift handler CLAMPS to `[event_gift_credits_min, event_gift_credits_max]` (production values: 2-10рЯТО). So a quest promising +100рЯТО paid 10рЯТО. An achievement promising +300рЯТО paid 10рЯТО. A 60-day streak milestone promising +1000рЯТО paid 10рЯТО. This was the "credits don't appear" bug вАФ they did appear, just clamped. Fix: 3 new server actions in [server.js](server.js) `/api/player/earn`: `dyn_quest` / `dyn_ach` / `dyn_streak_milestone` вАФ each reads the actual reward amount from the existing `dyn_*_reward_*` config keys, with per-action allowlists for the `meta.quest_id` / `meta.ach_id` / `meta.milestone` (anti-cheat вАФ cheater can't invent unknown ids to mint payouts). Extended `META_DEDUP_ACTIONS` to include the three so dedup works correctly per-quest/ach/milestone. Client updated in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) (`claimQuestReward` + `checkAndGrantAchievements`) and [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) (streak milestone fire path). **Shop expansion**: added "„Ь„Х„Ч„Х„™ „У„Щ„†„Ю„Щ„Щ„Э" section to the in-game shop ([src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js)) with two new items вАФ рЯЫ° **Streak Freeze** (price from `dyn_streak_freeze_price`, default 200рЯТО, integrates with existing freeze count display) and рЯОБ **Bonus Mystery Chest** (100рЯТО to open an extra chest bypassing the daily cap вАФ pure Skinner-box gambling, sold transparently). Both gated by their respective master toggles so an admin who disabled the system never sees the items. Bonus chest path: `/api/player/spend` for the 100рЯТО deduction вЖТ instant `openMysteryChest()` call which rolls server-side and animates the reveal. Cache buster `v20260523a`, SW `bloom-v8.5`.
- вЬЕ **Push Notifications вАФ admin broadcast + smart prompts вАФ stage 10 (May 2026)** вАФ closes the retention loop with the channel that reaches players when the app is closed. **Most of the infrastructure was already in place** from an earlier round: server-side `web-push` integration ([server.js](server.js) lines 7-68 with VAPID setup + `sendPushToDevice` helper used by duels, gifts, challenges), `push_subscriptions` table in [schema.sql](schema.sql) line 410, `/api/push/vapid-public` + `/api/push/subscribe` + `/api/push/unsubscribe` endpoints, full client-side flow in [src/16-push.js](src/16-push.js) (`subscribeToPush`, soft pre-prompt overlay, `maybeAskForPushPermission` exposed as `window.__bloomMaybeAskPush`), and SW handlers in [public/sw.js](public/sw.js) for `push` / `notificationclick` / `pushsubscriptionchange`. **What this commit adds**: (1) Three admin endpoints in [server.js](server.js): `GET /<ADMIN>/api/push/status` (returns `configured` / `enabled` / `subscriberCount` / `vapidPublic`), `POST /<ADMIN>/api/push/test` (send to one device for QA), `POST /<ADMIN>/api/push/broadcast` (send to ALL subscribers in batches of 200 with parallel pushes per batch, soft-fails on individual stale endpoints via the existing 410-Gone cleanup, writes audit log to `admin_actions`). Master toggle `push_enabled` in `game_config` defaults `'true'`. (2) Admin push composer UI in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) under рЯФІ „†„Щ„Ш„Х„® tab вАФ status badge with subscriber count, title + body + URL + tag + requireInteraction inputs, 4 quick templates (l„Х„Ч „Ч„Т / „®„¶„£ „С„°„Ы„†„Ф / „§„®„° „Ю„Ю„™„Щ„Я / „Р„Щ„®„Х„Ґ „§„®„°„Щ„Э), test + broadcast buttons, result panel showing succeeded/failed counts. (3) **Smart prompt triggers** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) вАФ `__bloomMaybeAskPush(reason)` now fires at 3 high-intent dopamine moments: **first 3-day streak milestone** ("„†„©„Ю„Х„® „Ґ„Ь „Ф„®„¶„£ „©„Ь„Ъ"), **first achievement unlock** (вЙ§2 earned total, "„Ф„Щ„©„Т „®„Р„©„Х„Я!"), and **comeback claim** ("„С„®„Х„Ъ „©„Х„С„Ъ! „Ь„Р „™„§„°„§„° „©„Х„С"). The existing 3-day pre-prompt cooldown in [src/16-push.js](src/16-push.js) prevents over-asking. (4) Added `web-push@3.6.7` to `package.json` (first new dep approved by user). Pre-launch checklist for production: set `VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY` + `VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY` + `VAPID_SUBJECT` env vars on Railway (`npx web-push generate-vapid-keys`). Cache buster `v20260522zh`, SW `bloom-v8.4`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Streak Freeze + Comeback Bonus вАФ stage 9 (May 2026)** вАФ two retention safety nets layered on top of the existing streak system. **Streak Freeze** (Duolingo's `рЯЫ°` mechanic): player buys "freezes" with рЯТО (default 200/each via `dyn_streak_freeze_price`). When `recordDynamicStreakDay()` detects exactly a 1-day miss (`gap === 2`) AND `getStreakFreezes() > 0`, it consumes one freeze and treats the streak as continuous. Server enforces the purchase via the existing balance-guarded `UPDATE` pattern in `POST /api/player/streak-freeze/buy` (10/hr rate-limit). Freeze count is client-side `localStorage[bloom_dyn_freezes]` вАФ a determined cheater could fake the count but freezes have no trade value (protect only their own streak). New freeze pill in the picker header (blue gradient `.dyn-freeze-row`) with current count + buy button. On a successful purchase the picker re-renders to show the new count. When a freeze auto-applies on game-over, a separate `.over-streak-banner-freeze` (blue gradient + `dynFreezePulse` 3-cycle animation) tells the player "рЯЫ° „Ф„І„§„Р„™ „®„¶„£ „Ф„¶„Щ„Ь„Ф „Р„Х„™„Ъ! „Р„Щ„С„У„™ „Щ„Х„Э „Р„С„Ь „Ф„®„¶„£ „Ю„Ю„©„Щ„Ъ" so they FEEL the value of their 200рЯТО investment. **Comeback Bonus** (re-engagement for lapsed players): when `recordDynamicStreakDay()` resets a streak вЙ•3, it saves `lostStreak` + `lostStreakDate` into the streak object. `getComebackContext()` checks if the player is now eligible вАФ streak was вЙ•`dyn_comeback_min_streak` (3) AND `daysAway вЙ• dyn_comeback_min_days` (3). On picker open, fires `showComebackOverlay()` 350ms after the shell renders вАФ a full-screen rainbow-gradient celebration card with рЯСЛ waving icon, "„С„®„Х„Ъ „©„Х„С„Ъ!" title, the lost-streak count, the reward amount (+150рЯТО default), and a freeze-gift bonus (+1 free freeze via `dyn_comeback_freeze_gift`). Tap "рЯОБ „І„С„Ь „Р„™ „Ф„С„Х„†„Х„°" вЖТ `POST /api/player/comeback-claim` (server-side dedup: one claim per device per rolling 7-day window via `_comeback:<deviceId>:<week>` game_config key). Server-side validation: server re-checks `dyn_comeback_min_days/min_streak` against the client-claimed values, refuses if too low. Marks `st.comebackClaimedFor = lostStreakDate` so the overlay never re-fires for the same lost streak. **8 new admin config keys** with tooltips + presets: `dyn_streak_freeze_enabled/price/max_per_streak`, `dyn_comeback_enabled/min_days/min_streak/reward/freeze_gift`. The freeze pill, comeback overlay, and freeze-used banner all respect their master toggles. Cache buster `v20260522zg`, SW `bloom-v8.3`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Mystery Chest (Skinner box) вАФ stage 8 (May 2026)** вАФ the variable-ratio reinforcement layer that makes slot machines addictive, applied to every dynamic-board game-over. **5 rarity tiers** with admin-tuneable weights + amounts (`common/uncommon/rare/legendary/mythic` вАФ defaults `60/25/12/2/1` percent, payouts `3-10 / 15-30 / 50-100 / 200-400 / 800-1500` рЯТО). **Server-rolled** via `POST /api/boards/chest/open` in [server.js](server.js) ([requireDeviceAuth], 30/hr rate limit) вАФ client never picks the tier (anti-cheat). Atomic credit + per-day counter via a single `game_config` dedup key `_chest:<deviceId>:<date>`. **"Boosted pity"** вАФ first N chests/day (default 3) skip the common tier entirely so a new player's first 3 chests never feel cheap. **Daily cap** (default 20) prevents farming. **Client reveal animation** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) `openMysteryChest()` вЖТ 5-stage choreography over ~4.5s: (1) chest рЯУ¶ appears + shakes 900ms with knock tone, (2) lid pops + light burst (radial gradient `dynChestBurst` keyframe), (3) **slot-machine reel** spins through tier emojis (рЯУ¶вЖТрЯОБвЖТрЯТ†вЖТрЯМЯвЖТрЯФЃ) with ease-out deceleration + click tone per tick, (4) lands on the real tier вАФ pitch-graded landing sound (320/440/560/700/880 Hz for the 5 tiers), buzz `[60,40,80]`, card adds `.dyn-chest-card-landed` for breathing-glow + rim-pulse infinite, (5) gem amount counts up from 0 over 700ms. **Confetti** spawns for rare+ tiers (18-particle radial burst with per-tier color palettes). **Tier-specific corner sparkles вЬ®** decorate legendary + mythic via `::before/::after` pseudo-elements. **17 new `game_config` keys** in [schema.sql](schema.sql): `dyn_chest_enabled` (master), 5 `_weight_*`, 10 `_*_min/max`, `_daily_cap`, `_boosted_count`. **Admin tooltips + preset chip lists** for all 17 in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) вАФ explains economic math (e.g. "1 mythic per 100 chests = „©„Ч„І„Я „Щ„Ц„Ы„Х„® „Ь„Щ„Ю„Щ„Э"). **Wired into** the dynamic-mode game-over branch in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) вАФ fires 900ms after `render({over:true})` so the player reads the headline before the chest takes over. Also polished 4 weak user-facing strings (picker subtitle, pioneer chip, empty-state copy, streak pioneer banner) for stronger psychological pull. Cache buster `v20260522zf`, SW `bloom-v8.2`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Full admin control over retention systems (May 2026)** вАФ user feedback: "did you make sure the admin controls everything?" вЖТ no, the FOMO/PB/global-LB/streak/achievements/quests rewards were all hardcoded. Closing the gap with **34 new `game_config` keys** that let the admin tune the entire retention stack without a redeploy. **6 master toggles** (`dyn_quests_enabled` / `dyn_achievements_enabled` / `dyn_streak_enabled` / `dyn_personal_best_enabled` / `dyn_global_lb_enabled` / `dyn_fomo_enabled` вАФ all default `'true'`, admin opts OUT not in). Setting any to `'false'` hides every chip/banner/modal/in-game-pill associated with that system вАФ the localStorage is preserved so re-enabling restores everything intact. **28 per-reward keys**: 11 quest rewards (`dyn_quest_reward_play2/play3/score10k/score30k/score75k/tier7/tier8/theme/shape/beatself/beatleader`), 5 per-board ach rewards (`played/crown/score10/score50/score100`), 6 cross-board ach rewards (`pioneer5/pioneer10/crown5/all_themes/all_shapes/leaderboard1`), 6 streak milestone rewards (`dyn_streak_reward_3/7/14/30/60/100`). Defaults seeded in [schema.sql](schema.sql) match the original hardcoded values. **Client wiring** ([src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js)): new `dynConfig(key, default)` / `dynConfigInt` / `dynConfigBool` readers from the `gameConfig` module-scope variable (loaded by `/api/config` at boot) + `dynFeatureEnabled(name)` for the 6 master toggles. Reward helpers `dynStreakReward(milestone)` / `dynAchReward(id)` / `dynQuestReward(id)` resolve at runtime. `window.DYN_STREAK_REWARDS` is now a `Proxy` that auto-resolves to `dynStreakReward(N)` so any code reading `DYN_STREAK_REWARDS[7]` picks up the admin's override. Quest rewards are also re-resolved on every `getDailyQuests()` read so an admin's mid-day reward bump applies to already-completed-but-not-claimed quests. **Admin tooltips** ([admin/index.html](admin/index.html)): 34 new `TIPS_PER_KEY` entries with rich Hebrew copy explaining each key вАФ recommended value ranges, retention rationale, dependency notes (e.g. "dyn_ach_reward_leaderboard1: requires the /leaderboard fetch to confirm rank=1"). 28 new `PRESETS_PER_KEY` chip lists for one-click typical values (e.g. crown reward presets `[75, 150, 250, 300]`). All keys appear in the existing "„Ы„Ь „Ф„Ф„Т„У„®„Х„™" config table with auto-detected toggle/preset/free-input UI вАФ `*_enabled` keys get the green вЬУ „§„Ґ„Щ„Ь / red вЬЧ „Ы„С„Х„Щ toggle buttons, numeric reward keys get input + preset chips. Cache buster `v20260522ze`, SW `bloom-v8.1`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Daily Quests (May 2026)** вАФ the F2P checklist mechanic. 3 fresh quests every Asia/Jerusalem day, deterministic per date via `mulberry32(hashSeed(date + ':dyn-quests-v1'))` so all players see the same pool draw (community talking point) but the menu varies day-to-day. Pool of 11 quests in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) `DYN_QUEST_POOL`: 2/3 different boards (50/100рЯТО), scoreвЙ•10K/30K/75K (50/100/250рЯТО), tierвЙ•7/8 (75/200рЯТО), play themed/shape (60/60рЯТО), beat your own best (120рЯТО), beat the global leader (300рЯТО). Storage `localStorage[bloom_dyn_quests_<YYYY-MM-DD>]` keeps yesterday's row cleaned up via deferred `setTimeout(0)` removal. **Manual claim pattern** (Clash Royale / Duolingo, NOT auto-claim): completed quest shows a gold-pink pulsing `рЯОБ „І„С„Ь +NрЯТО` button. Tap = call `claimQuestReward(id)` вЖТ `earnCredits` fires + button replaces itself with `вЬУ „†„Р„°„£` + `soundMilestone(3)` + `buzz([30,30,60])`. The "I have rewards waiting" hook drives return visits even when the player doesn't want to play. **Quest pipeline** in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) dynamic-mode game-over branch: synchronous `applyQuestProgressOnGameOver()` returns just-completed quests + asynchronous re-check after the /leaderboard fetch resolves (for the beat_leader quest that needs the global rank). Fires `renderQuestCompletedToast(q)` for late completions. **Surfaces**: (1) **Home button label** вАФ `рЯОБ N „§„®„°„Щ„Э „©„Ь „Ю„©„Щ„Ю„Ф „Ю„Ю„™„Щ„†„Щ„Э „Ь„Ъ вАФ „Ь„Ч„•!` (mint-green breathing background `.fomo-quest-claim`) takes PRIORITY over streak-danger and FOMO вАФ a sitting unclaimed gem reward is louder than any other signal. (2) **Picker header pill** вАФ `рЯОѓ „Ю„©„Щ„Ю„Х„™ „Щ„Х„Ю„Щ„Х„™: 1/3 ¬Ј 1 рЯОБ „Ь„І„С„Ь` (green gradient, gold-pink pulsing king variant when claimable). (3) **Game-over banner** вАФ green-emerald pulsing card per quest completed this game (`over-quest-banner`). (4) **Quests modal** вАФ full catalog with per-quest progress bar (locked: dimmed `+50рЯТО` pill; completed: gold-pink claim button; claimed: muted `вЬУ „†„Р„°„£`). Each row's bar fills 0вЖТ100% as progress updates; completed rows recolor to gold-pink gradient. Cache buster `v20260522zd`, SW `bloom-v8.0`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Achievements / Badges (May 2026)** вАФ the completionist engine. 5 per-board + 6 cross-board achievements, each unlock fires `earnCredits` for 25-1000рЯТО. Storage in `localStorage[bloom_dyn_achievements]` (renamed from `ACH_KEY` to `DYN_ACH_KEY` to avoid collision with the existing achievements system in [src/04-ui-utils.js](src/04-ui-utils.js)). Shape: `{ perBoard: { <boardId>: { played: ts, crown: ts, score10: ts, ... } }, cross: { pioneer5: ts, all_themes: ts, ... } }`. **Per-board achievements** (5√ЧN boards): рЯМ± played (25рЯТО), рЯСС reached crown (150рЯТО), рЯТО scoreвЙ•10K (50рЯТО), рЯПЖ scoreвЙ•50K (150рЯТО), рЯТѓ scoreвЙ•100K (300рЯТО). **Cross-board achievements** (6 total): рЯЧЇпЄП 5 different boards (200рЯТО), рЯІ≠ 10 different boards (500рЯТО), рЯСС 5 crowns (500рЯТО), рЯОД all 4 themes (800рЯТО), рЯЯ¶ all 4 shapes (800рЯТО), рЯ•З #1 on any board (1000рЯТО). **Surfaces**: (1) **Picker card chip** вАФ `рЯПЕ рЯМ± рЯСС рЯТО` icon stack of earned per-board achievements next to the existing chips, gives instant "I have 3 / 5 here, can I get the rest?" psychology. (2) **Picker header button** вАФ `рЯПЕ „Ф„Щ„©„Т„Щ„Э: 7 / 34` gold pill, opens the full modal. (3) **Game-over banner** вАФ `over-ach-banner` (gold-pink pulsing) for each achievement unlocked this game, stacks vertically when multiple fire on one big game-over. (4) **Floating top-of-viewport toast** for late unlocks (the leaderboard rank-1 achievement only confirms after the /leaderboard fetch вАФ fires `renderAchievementUnlockToast(u)` 200-400ms after the over screen renders). (5) **Achievements modal** вАФ full catalog with earned items glowing gold + locked items dimmed with reward visible, grouped into "рЯПЖ „Ы„Ь„Ь„Щ„Щ„Э" (cross with `x / y` progress lines) + "рЯОѓ „§„® „Ь„Х„Ч" (per-board accordion with 5-icon badge grid per board). Rank-1 detection uses a two-phase grant: initial pass grants everything score/tier-based, post-fetch pass grants the `leaderboard1` cross achievement once the /api/boards/:id/leaderboard response confirms `rank === 1`. Cache buster `v20260522zc`, SW `bloom-v7.9`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Cross-board streak (May 2026)** вАФ the multi-day retention layer. Duolingo-style "play any dynamic board for N consecutive days" вАФ losing the streak is on the player (no auto-freeze in v1), regaining it is satisfying. **Storage**: `localStorage[bloom_dyn_streak]` = `{count, last (YYYY-MM-DD Asia/Jerusalem), milestonesClaimed: []}`. The variable was originally named `STREAK_KEY` but conflicted with the existing daily-streak system in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) вАФ renamed to `DYN_STREAK_KEY` etc. so the two streaks coexist. **Logic**: `recordDynamicStreakDay()` (called from the dynamic-mode game-over branch in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) compares today's date with `last`: if same day вЖТ no-op; if exactly 1 day later вЖТ increment; otherwise вЖТ reset to 1 + clear `milestonesClaimed`. Milestones: 3/7/14/30/60/100 days; rewards: 50/150/300/600/1000/2000 рЯТО, granted via `earnCredits('event_gift', {amount, streak_milestone: N})`. **Three visible surfaces**: **(1) Home button subtitle** вАФ `isStreakInDanger()` (streak вЙ•3 AND not played today) takes priority: "рЯФ• „Ф„®„¶„£ „©„Ь„Ъ „С„°„Ы„†„Ф! N „Щ„Ю„Щ„Э вАФ „©„Ч„І „Ф„Щ„Х„Э" + `.fomo-streak-danger` class adds a red-pink breathing background. Otherwise FOMO countdown / streak headline (`рЯФ• „®„¶„£ N „Щ„Ю„Щ„Э ¬Ј M „Ь„Х„Ч„Х„™ „Ц„Ю„Щ„†„Щ„Э`) per priority. **(2) Picker modal header banner** вАФ three states: `dyn-streak-banner-pioneer` (рЯМ± onboarding copy with full milestone schedule, no streak yet), `dyn-streak-banner-safe` (calm warm gradient + "„©„Ю„®„™ „Р„Х„™„Х „Ф„Щ„Х„Э вЬУ"), `dyn-streak-banner-danger` (red breathing gradient + "„©„Ч„І „Ы„Ь „Ь„Х„Ч „У„Щ„†„Ю„Щ „Ґ„У „Ч„¶„Х„™"). All three show the next-milestone progress line ("„Ґ„Х„У N „Щ„Ю„Щ„Э „Ь„С„Р„У„Т„≥ M (+RрЯТО)"). **(3) Game-over banner** in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) вАФ `over-streak-banner-milestone` (gold-pink pulsing celebration on milestone hits with the reward amount) OR `over-streak-banner` (warm calm version with progress to next milestone) вАФ passed via new `opts.streakResult` from the dynamic game-over branch. New CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css). Cache buster `v20260522zb`, SW `bloom-v7.8`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Per-board top-50 leaderboard modal (May 2026)** вАФ completes the addiction loop. Each picker card now sports a gold trophy button next to it (`.dyn-boards-trophy-btn`) that opens a per-board top-50 leaderboard modal вАФ totally separate from the play action, so the player can browse standings without committing to a game. The modal in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): gold gradient header with board name + theme/shape meta; live `fetch('/api/boards/:id/leaderboard?limit=50&deviceId=вА¶')` with 30s setInterval refresh; rows show `рЯ•ЗрЯ•ИрЯ•Й` for top 3 / `#N` rank for the rest, country flag (regional-indicator codepoint math, no asset work), name, score. "You" row is highlighted with a gold-pink gradient border + box-shadow; off-list players (>50) get a separate sticky "„Р„™„Ф #87" pill at the bottom. **The most addictive piece** is the persistent `рЯОѓ next-target` banner above the list: when the player has a score, it computes `aboveScore - myScore` and renders "вЪФпЄП „Ґ„Х„У 1,234 „†„І„Х„У„Х„™ „Ы„У„Щ „Ь„Ґ„І„Х„£ „Р„™ „У„†„Щ„Р„Ь" in a pulsing gold-orange pill вАФ same psychological lever as the contest "overtake watch". When the player IS the leader: "рЯСС „Р„™„Ф „Ф„Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь! ¬Ј „Ф„Ю„І„Х„Э „Ф„©„†„Щ: 89K" in the full pulsing pink-gold king variant. Modal lifecycle: `_boardLbRefreshHandle` cleared on close + ESC + backdrop click; `_boardLbCurrentBoard` guards paint() against stale fetches if the player switches boards rapidly. Footer has "вЖР „Ч„Ц„Х„®" (back to picker) + "вЦґ „©„Ч„І „Ґ„Ы„©„Щ„Х" primary CTA (closes modal + immediately starts the board) вАФ so the leaderboard is a no-friction stepping stone, not a dead-end. New CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): full light/dark theme palette, `.dyn-boards-trophy-btn` (46px gold pill on each card), `.board-lb-overlay/.modal/.head/.body/.foot`, `.board-lb-row` with top-1/2/3/you variants, `.board-lb-next-target` + `-king` with `nextTargetPulse` + `nextTargetPulseKing` keyframes. Cache buster `v20260522za`, SW `bloom-v7.7`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Per-board GLOBAL leaderboards (May 2026)** вАФ the social half of the addiction loop, stacked on top of the personal-best layer from the previous commit. Turns "рЯПЖ „©„Щ„Р 47K" (me vs me) into "рЯПЖ 47K ¬Ј #14 „Ю„™„Х„Ъ 87 ¬Ј рЯСС „У„†„Щ„Р„Ь: 89K" (me vs everyone). **Schema**: new `dynamic_board_scores` table in [schema.sql](schema.sql) вАФ PK `(board_id, device_id)`, FK to `board_configurations(id)` with ON DELETE CASCADE so deleting an admin board cleans up its scores. Best-score-wins upsert mirroring `daily_scores`. `idx_dynamic_board_scores_board_score` for fast top-N queries. **Server**: 3 new endpoints in [server.js](server.js): `POST /api/boards/:id/score` (requireDeviceAuth, 60/hr rate limit, drops-required + challengeDropsImplausible anti-cheat, returns `{rank, total, score}` for the over-screen rank pill); `GET /api/boards/:id/leaderboard` (top 50 + my rank); `/api/boards/available` enriched with one JOIN to return `leader_name`, `leader_score`, `leader_tier`, `players` per board. **Client picker chips** in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): `рЯСС „У„†„Щ„Р„Ь: 89K` (pink-gradient leader chip) OR `рЯСС „Р„™„Ф „Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь!` (gold-pink pulsing king chip when the player's local best вЙ• leader_score) PLUS `рЯС• 47 „©„Щ„Ч„І„Х` social-proof chip. **In-game leader chip** in the mode-bar subtitle ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) renders side-by-side with the personal-best chip. `bumpScore()` swaps the leader chip to a pulsing gold-pink `рЯСС „Ч„¶„Щ„™ „Р„™ „Ф„Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь! +2,408` when score crosses the global leader's number вАФ fires `soundMilestone(6)` + `buzz([60,60,60,60,100])` ONCE (dedup'd via `dataset.celebrated`). **Game-over rank pill** ([src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css)): renders an instant `вП≥ „Ю„Ч„©„С „У„Щ„®„Х„Т „С„Ь„Х„ЧвА¶` placeholder, then the POST response patches the `#over-board-rank-host` with the real label: `рЯСС „Ю„І„Х„Э „®„Р„©„Х„Я „С„Ь„Х„Ч X!` (king variant: pulsing gradient) / `рЯПЖ #2 „Ю„™„Х„Ъ 87 ¬Ј „Ґ„С„®„™ 99% „Ю„Ф„©„Ч„І„†„Щ„Э` / `в≠Р #5 „Ю„™„Х„Ъ 87 ¬Ј „Ґ„С„®„™ 95%` / `рЯОѓ #18 „Ю„™„Х„Ъ 87` (tiered emoji by rank). Submit is fire-and-forget вАФ the personal-best feedback paints instantly, the global-rank pill slots in 200-400ms later with no UI jank. Cache buster `v20260522z`, SW `bloom-v7.6`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Per-board personal best loop (May 2026)** вАФ the strongest single addiction engine in the dynamic-boards system. Each board now has its own localStorage best record so the player chases their own score per-board, not just the global daily best. Three visible surfaces: **(1) Picker card chip** вАФ `рЯПЖ „©„Щ„Р 47K` (gold gradient) when the player has a record, `рЯМ± „Ч„У„© „Ь„Ъ` (mint gradient) when this board is unplayed. Drives "be the first / beat your last" psychology side-by-side. **(2) In-game target chip** in the mode-bar subtitle вАФ `рЯПЖ „Ь„Ґ„С„Х„®: 47,392` in soft gold. The chip is live: when `score > target` mid-game, `bumpScore()` swaps it to a pink-orange pulsing `рЯСС „Ґ„С„®„™ „Р„™ „Ґ„¶„Ю„Ъ! +2,408` + plays `soundMilestone(4)` + `buzz([40,40,80])` for immediate gameplay-time feedback (not just on game-over). The +N overage updates live as score grows. **(3) Game-over banner** вАФ three variants in [src/12-tour-info.js](src/12-tour-info.js) `render({over:true})`: gold-pink pulsing "рЯПЖ „©„Щ„Р „Ч„У„© „С[„©„Э] +N „Ю„Ґ„Ь [prev]" when beating own record, red-pink "рЯШ± „Ы„Ю„Ґ„Ш „Ґ„С„®„™ „Р„™ „Ґ„¶„Ю„Ъ! „Ч„°„® N" when within 85% of best, soft gold "рЯОѓ „Ф„©„Щ„Р „©„Ь„Ъ „С[„©„Э]: N ¬Ј „†„°„Ф „©„Х„С!" otherwise. Storage: `localStorage[bloom_board_best_<boardId>]` = `{score, tier, ts}` keyed by stable server-issued board id. `setBoardBest()` is monotonic вАФ never overwrites with a lower score. Wired into the dynamic-mode branch of game-over in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js): captures `prevBoardBest` BEFORE writing the new value, passes both to `render()` so the over screen can show the delta. New helpers in [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js): `getBoardBest(id)` / `setBoardBest(id, score, tier)` / `formatBoardScore(n)` (compact "K"/"M" notation for chip space). CSS: `.dyn-boards-chip-best/-pioneer` + `.dyn-target-chip-passed` keyframes + `.over-board-best-up/-near/-target` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css) + [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css). Cache buster `v20260522y`, SW `bloom-v7.5`.
- вЬЕ **Dynamic Boards вАФ Phase 6 LiveOps FOMO layer (May 2026)** вАФ closes the 6-phase roadmap. Boards already had `starts_at` / `ends_at` columns + a server-side schedule filter, but neither the home button nor the picker surfaced the urgency, so a player browsing the home screen had no signal that today's special board was hours from disappearing. Three-part fix: (1) [server.js](server.js) `/api/boards/available` now SELECTs `starts_at, ends_at` alongside the existing fields (60s cache is invalidated on any admin write so newly-scheduled boards appear quickly). (2) [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) introduces `boardUrgency(board)` returning `'critical'` (<4h to ends_at) / `'new'` (<24h since starts_at) / `'soon'` (<24h to ends_at) / `'normal'` / `'expired'`; `pickFocusBoard(boards)` ranks critical > new > soon. `updateDynamicBoardsButton()` rewrites the home button label every time it runs: `рЯФ• „Х„Ь„†„Ш„Щ„Щ„Я „Ю„°„™„Щ„Щ„Э „С„Ґ„Х„У 4„© 12„У` (critical), `рЯЖХ „Ч„†„Х„Ы„Ф вАФ „Ч„У„© „Ф„Щ„Х„Э` (new), `вП∞ „§„°„Ч вАФ „†„©„Р„® 6„© 22„У` (soon), else the vanilla count. A 60s `setInterval` (`startFomoTick` / `stopFomoTick`) re-runs the update + re-renders any open picker вАФ torn down in `hideHomeV2()` via `window.stopDynamicBoardsTick` so detached DOM doesn't keep ticking. (3) Picker cards: each card gets a per-board FOMO badge via `renderFomoBadge(board)` вАФ `рЯФ• „Ю„°„™„Щ„Щ„Э „С„Ґ„Х„У 3„© 22„У` (pulsing red gradient w/ box-shadow), `рЯЖХ „Ч„У„© „Ф„Щ„Х„Э ¬Ј „Ґ„У 25/5` (mint pulse), `вП∞ „†„©„Р„® 18„© 04„У` (warm orange static), `рЯУЕ „Ґ„У 25/5` (subtle calendar pill for non-urgent boards with an end date). `refreshPickerTimers()` updates only the badge hosts on each tick вАФ keeps scroll/focus intact. New CSS in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css): `.dyn-fomo-pill-{critical,new,soon,cal}` + `@keyframes dynFomoPulseCritical/New` + `.dyn-boards-card.fomo-critical` with `dynBoardCardCritical` border breathing + `.home-v2-boards.fomo-{critical,new,soon}` gradient backgrounds matching urgency. Cache buster `v20260522x`, SW `bloom-v7.4`. Dynamic Boards roadmap is now complete on all 6 phases.
- вЬЕ **Themed-board UX fix вАФ preview + auto-default + empty-board guard (May 2026)** вАФ user-reported: clicked a board name in the home picker, saw no visual change. Diagnosis via `curl /api/boards/available`: board #3 named "„С„Х„†„Х„°" had `{type:"themed", definition:{cells:[]}}` вАФ a fully empty themed board with no theme_id, no shape_id, no cells. The admin had selected type='themed' but didn't pick a theme from the dropdown, so saving produced a no-op definition that `applyBoardToSession` correctly applied nothing for. Four-part fix: (1) [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) `onBoardTypeChange()` now auto-sets `board-theme-id` to `'valentine'` when type changes to 'themed' and the picker is empty вАФ instant visible feedback, no silent empty saves. (2) New `refreshThemedPreview()` + `<div id="board-themed-preview">` host renders a live 4√Ч6 mini-grid in the admin editor with the actual theme palette + shape voids + cell emoji as the admin edits вАФ admin sees EXACTLY what the player will see before clicking save. Wired into `onchange` of theme/shape selects, `oninput` of board-name, click of cells-grid, plus on editor open. (3) `saveBoard()` validation: refuses to save when `type === 'themed'` AND `!theme_id` AND `!shape_id` AND `!cells.length` with an explicit Hebrew error "вЪ† „Ь„Х„Ч „Ч„Т „®„Щ„І вАФ „С„Ч„® „Ь„§„Ч„Х„™ „Ґ„®„Ы„Ф / „¶„Х„®„Ф / „™„Р„Щ„Э „Ю„Щ„Х„Ч„У„Щ„Э" вАФ root-causes the original bug. (4) [src/05c-dynamic-boards.js](src/05c-dynamic-boards.js) picker overhaul: per-card theme tint background (matches `body.theme-X-active` hue from boards.css), plus a chip row showing `рЯТХ „Х„Ь„†„Ш„Щ„Щ„Я` / `вЭ§пЄП „Ь„С` / `вЬ®√Ч2` etc. so the player can tell themed boards apart before clicking. New CSS `.dyn-boards-chip` + variants `-theme/-shape/-cell` in [public/css/boards.css](public/css/boards.css). Cache buster `v20260522w`, SW `bloom-v7.3`.
- вЬЕ **Contest leave actually leaves (May 2026)** вАФ user-reported: "„†„™„І „Ю„Ю„Ы„©„Щ„® „Ц„Ф" (the leave button on a contest's leaderboard) only cleared `localStorage` and called `clearContestGameState` / `clearContestDisplayName` / `invalidateMyContestsCache`. The `contest_scores` DB row was untouched, so the next page refresh hit `/api/contests/mine`, the row came back, and the contest reappeared in the "my contests" list вАФ making the leave button look broken. Fixes: (a) [schema.sql](schema.sql) adds `ALTER TABLE contest_scores ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS left_at TIMESTAMPTZ` (idempotent); (b) new `POST /api/contests/:code/leave` endpoint in [server.js](server.js) sets `left_at = NOW()` for the device's row (soft-leave preserves the score on the contest's own leaderboard вАФ matching the existing confirm copy "„Ф„¶„Щ„Х„Я „†„©„Ю„® „С„Ь„Х„Ч") + cleans up `contest_live_state` and `contest_watchers` rows so the player doesn't linger as a live spectator-target after leaving, with a 30/hour rate-limit; (c) `/api/contests/mine` now filters `WHERE cs.left_at IS NULL`; (d) `/api/contests/:code/join` clears `left_at` in its UPSERT's DO UPDATE clause so re-joining via the code resumes the existing row with the score intact; (e) [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) `clb-leave` handler awaits `apiPost('/api/contests/<code>/leave', {})` BEFORE the local cleanup so the row is flagged before the next `/mine` fetch. Cache buster `v20260521l`, SW `bloom-v5.1`.
- вЬЕ **Bonus-tile leak + reward number trust fix (May 2026)** вАФ two user-reported bugs in one batch. **(1) Event overlay leaking onto home.** The "force first event" `setTimeout(spawnRandomEvent, 3000)` in `startEventSystem` was untracked and survived `stopEventSystem`. When a player entered the game and bounced back to home within 3s, the timeout fired, `spawnRandomEvent` found `grid` still populated, and `renderEventOnCell` built a `position:fixed` overlay at the cell's viewport coords вАФ which on a desktop browser sits OUTSIDE the centered 380px `.app` column and visibly floated next to the home card with its `2.0s` countdown. Fixes in [src/14-events.js](src/14-events.js): (a) `eventInitTimer` is now tracked + cleared by `stopEventSystem`; (b) a new `eventSystemRunning` flag gates every async callback (interval + init timeout) so a tick that fires between stop and clear early-returns; (c) new `isGameSurfaceVisible()` (false when `#home-screen` / `#contest-screen` / `#challenge-screen` / `#spectator-screen` is mounted) guards `trySpawnEvent`, `spawnRandomEvent`, AND `renderEventOnCell`; (d) `renderEventOnCell` additionally refuses to mount if the cell center sits OUTSIDE the `.app` bounding rect вАФ belt-and-suspenders for any future menu that forgets to call stop; (e) new `purgeEventOverlays()` nukes `#event-drop-overlay` + `.fx-overlay` elements, invoked from both `showHome` and `showHomeV2` after `stopEventSystem`; (f) window resize / orientationchange now repositions the overlay (or purges if no surface). **(2) Daily login reward mismatch.** The reward overlay teased a streak-tiered amount (25 вЖТ 50 вЖТ 100 вЖТ 200 by streak day) via `getDailyRewardAmount`, but `earnCredits('daily_login')` paid a flat `daily_login_reward` config вАФ currently `15` in prod after the 2026-05-17 economy migration (schema.sql line 609). So a returning player saw "+25 рЯТО" in the overlay and a "+15 рЯТО" toast pop up. Fixes: (a) [schema.sql](schema.sql) adds tiered keys `daily_login_reward_streak_3` (50), `_streak_7` (100), `_streak_30` (200) вАФ all `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`; (b) [server.js](server.js) `/api/player/earn` now picks the tier when `action === 'daily_login'`, reading `meta.streak` (clamped 1..400) вАФ dedup is still one claim/device/day so the worst-case forged-streak payout is bounded by the 200рЯТО ceiling; (c) [src/08-contest-helpers.js](src/08-contest-helpers.js) `showDailyLoginReward` resolves the tier from boot-cached `gameConfig`, picks `Math.max(displayReward, srvVal)` as `resolvedReward`, runs the slot reel on that value, and passes `meta: { streak: displayStreak }` to `earnCredits` so the wallet matches; (d) [src/07-identity.js](src/07-identity.js) `showCreditToast` gains `daily_login: 'рЯОБ „С„Х„†„Х„° „Щ„Х„Ю„Щ'` + `comeback: 'рЯСЛ „С„®„Х„Ъ „©„Х„С„Ъ!'` labels. **(3) Score-milestone tier credibility (audit catch).** Same family of bug: milestone banners showed 2/3/5/10/20/50 but the call routed through `event_gift` which is server-clamped to `[event_gift_credits_min, event_gift_credits_max]` AND rate-limited to 30s вАФ so back-to-back milestones during a chain reaction silently dropped, and the displayed number lied. Fixes: (a) client switched from `earnCredits('event_gift', {amount, milestone})` вЖТ `earnCredits('score_milestone', {milestone})` вАФ uses per-milestone dedup, no rate-limit; (b) 200K renamed to 250K to match the server's `ALLOWED_MILESTONES` allowlist and a new 1M tier added; (c) server [server.js](server.js) reads `score_milestone_reward_<at>` per-tier with the flat `score_milestone_reward` as fallback; (d) [schema.sql](schema.sql) seeds the 7 tier keys mirroring `SCORE_MILESTONES` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) вАФ 2/3/5/10/25/50/100. Cache buster `v20260521k`, SW `bloom-v5.0`.
- вЬЕ **Contest scoring overhaul + clarity pass (May 2026)** вАФ multi-part work driven by user feedback that the contest UX was confusing and not addictive enough.
  1. **HUD redesign вАФ absolute scores everywhere.** The previous HUD displayed deltas in the target/chaser score positions ("„Ф„У„° 4,194" = my lead over her). As I scored, that number grew, which read as "Hadas is gaining points!" instead of "my lead is growing". Bad. New layout in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) `paintContestHud`: every side shows the **player's actual total** in the big number; a small delta line below with `вЖС N „Ь„Ґ„І„Х„£` (target) or `вЖУ N „Ь„§„†„Щ„Ъ` (chaser) provides the contextual gap with explicit labels. Three rows in each side: name вЖТ absolute score вЖТ delta. Zero ambiguity.
  2. **Score mode toggle вАФ cumulative vs best-of.** New `score_mode` column on `contests` ('cumulative' default, 'best' alternative). [Server.js](server.js) `POST /api/contests` accepts `scoreMode` body param; `POST /api/contests/:code/score` branches the upsert reducer between `contest_scores.score + EXCLUDED.score` (cumulative) and `GREATEST(contest_scores.score, EXCLUDED.score)` (best). `GET /api/contests/:code` returns `score_mode` with a 'cumulative' fallback for any pre-migration row. Client: new pill picker in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) `showCreateContestForm` (рЯІЃ „Ю„¶„Ш„С„® / рЯПЖ „Ф„Ы„Щ „Т„С„Х„Ф) with a hint line that updates per choice. HUD's projection logic respects mode вАФ best-of uses `Math.max(p.score, myLiveScore)` instead of summing вАФ so the displayed rank reflects "if I lock in this game" under either rule. Leaderboard scoring-note badge swaps between the two modes ("рЯПЖ „Ф„Ы„Щ „Т„С„Х„Ф вАФ „®„І „Ф„Ю„©„Ч„І „Ф„Ш„Х„С „С„Щ„Х„™„® „†„°„§„®" vs "рЯІЃ „†„Щ„І„Х„У „Ю„¶„Ш„С„® вАФ „Ы„Ь „Ю„©„Ч„І „Ю„¶„Ш„®„£ „Ь„°„Ъ „Ф„Ы„Ь"). HUD's mode-label line under my score becomes "„Р„™„Ф ¬Ј рЯПЖ „Ф„Ы„Щ „Т„С„Х„Ф" when active so the rule is always glanceable.
  3. **Home resume-game card.** Mid-game contest state was already saved on `beforeunload`/`visibilitychange`/per-drop, but after a refresh the user landed on home with no surfaced indication that a paused game existed вАФ they had to navigate back to the contest manually to find the "„©„Ч„І „Ґ„Ы„©„Щ„Х" button (which silently restored the game). [src/05a-home-v2.js](src/05a-home-v2.js) `renderHeroBannerV2` now checks `findPausedContestGame()` FIRST (highest-priority hero) and renders a clickable card: "вПЄ „Ф„Ю„©„Ъ „Ю„©„Ч„І „С„™„Ч„®„Х„™ [name] ¬Ј „†„Щ„І„Х„У: N ¬Ј „†„©„Ю„® „Ь„§„†„Щ 4 „У„І„≥". Tap вЖТ `setActiveContest` + `init('contest')` restores grid/score/nextPiece. Stale runs (>12h old) get a softer "вП± „Щ„© „Ю„©„Ч„І „Щ„©„Я „Ю„Х„©„Ф„Ф" treatment but still resume on tap. New helper `findPausedContestGame()` in [src/08-contest-helpers.js](src/08-contest-helpers.js) iterates every `bloom_contest_state_*` key, returns the freshest valid one, and opportunistically GCs entries past the TTL.
  Cache buster `v20260521j`, SW `bloom-v4.9`.
- вЬЕ **Spectator render fix + HUD teardown (May 2026)** вАФ user-reported: clicking a live row to spectate showed the spectator header + control buttons but a blank space where the live board should be. Root cause in [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css): `.spectator-grid > .grid` inherited the game's `.grid { display:grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(4, 1fr); grid-template-rows: repeat(6, 1fr) }` rules, which the in-game grid sizes at runtime via `fitGrid()` вАФ the spectator grid never gets that treatment, so `1fr` resolved to 0 and the 24 cells collapsed to 0√Ч0 (invisible). Fix: explicit `width: min(280px, 80vw); aspect-ratio: 4/6; margin: 0 auto` on the spectator grid + smaller SVG (`60%`) inside the cells to match the reduced cell size. Same issue had been silently broken for any contest entered via the contest-screen entry point (not just the new HUD's expand button). Also in [src/10-spectator.js](src/10-spectator.js) `startSpectator()`: tear down the in-game contest HUD on spectate (it shows MY rank + targets, which is irrelevant + visually distracting while I'm watching someone else); `stopSpectator()`'s mid-game-resume branch already calls `init('contest')` which remounts the HUD cleanly. Cache buster `v20260521i`, SW `bloom-v4.8`.
- вЬЕ **Contest HUD bugfix pass (May 2026)** вАФ two user-reported issues with the brand-new in-game contest HUD:
  1. **"„Ф„Ю„°„§„®„Щ„Э „Ь„Р „Р„Ю„Щ„™„Щ„Щ„Э"** вАФ the displayed score, rank, and target/chaser gaps came from two different totals. The 400ms tick wrote just the current game's `score` into the score element, while the 5s paint computed rank + gaps against `accumulated + score`. So the HUD's "10,546" was visually inconsistent with the "вИТ90,412 to overtake X" derived from a totally different number. Fix in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js): the tick now caches the most recent `players` list in `_contestHudCachedPlayers` and re-runs the full `paintContestHud` on every 400ms beat вАФ one render path, one source of truth for all three numbers. The displayed score is now the **projected total** (accumulated + current game), matching what the rank and gap calculations use. Also removed the confusing `вИТ` prefix on the gap (the absolute number reads as "this many points to close"; the prefix made the intent ambiguous).
  2. **"„©„Ь„Х„Ч„¶„Щ„Э „©„Х„С „Ц„Ф „Ь„Р „Ю„Ч„Ц„Щ„® „Ь„Ю„©„Ч„І"** вАФ tapping в§Ґ on the HUD opened the leaderboard but the back arrow routed to home or contest-menu, leaving the in-progress game inaccessible without re-entering the contest from the home screen. Fix: new cross-call flag `_contestHudJustOpenedLb` set by the HUD's в§Ґ handler and consumed by the next `showContestLeaderboard` mount. When set: (a) shell subtitle becomes "вПЄ „Ф„Ю„©„Ч„І „©„Ь„Ъ „Ю„Х„©„Ф„Ф" (so the player knows the game is paused not abandoned), (b) the back arrow calls `init('contest')` which restores from the state saved by the HUD's `saveContestGameState()` call, (c) a prominent green "вЖ© „Ч„Ц„Х„® „Ь„Ю„©„Ч„І „©„Ь„Ъ" primary CTA renders at the top of the form area, (d) the existing "„©„Ч„І „Ґ„Ы„©„Щ„Х" button gets relabeled "„Ф„™„Ч„Ь „Ю„©„Ч„І „Ч„У„©" and styled as secondary, and crucially calls `init('contest', { fresh: true })` so it wipes the saved state instead of resuming it. Cache buster `v20260521h`, SW `bloom-v4.7`.
- вЬЕ **Contest live HUD вАФ in-game opponent widget (May 2026)** вАФ until now contest gameplay had no ambient signal showing where you stood: scores updated silently on a separate leaderboard screen, and the only mid-game feedback was the transient `showContestAlert` toast (fires only on threshold events). Mirroring the duel-HUD pattern, new `startContestHud(code)` / `stopContestHud()` / `paintContestHud(players)` in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js) mount a `.contest-hud` pill at the top of the viewport whenever `init('contest')` runs. Three-column layout: **„Ь„Ґ„І„Х„£ вЪФпЄП** (player above me, with `вИТ1,234` gap in pink) ¬Ј **„Р„™„Ф** (large gold score + `#3 / 47` rank pulse) ¬Ј **„®„Х„У„£ рЯСА** (player below me, with `+800` lead in mint). Tap `в§Ґ` вЖТ saves contest state via `saveContestGameState()` + `stopLivePush()` then opens the full leaderboard via `showContestLeaderboard` (same pause/resume pattern as the existing exit-game flow). Data refresh: 5s `fetchContest` poll + 400ms local `score` tick вАФ opponent scores reflect their actual heartbeat between my drops, my own number updates instantly between merges. **Live-rank projection**: paint logic recomputes ranking locally by substituting my live `score` for what the server has on `cs.score+ls.live_score` (server hasn't seen my in-flight game yet). So the rank shown isn't "where I am now" вАФ it's "where I'd be if I locked in this score this second", which is the projection that turns "where do I stand?" into "if I keep this up I overtake „У„†„Щ„Р„Ь". Rank-up = gold pulse + scale-up keyframe, rank-down = pink pulse + scale-down. Lifecycle: mounts via `init('contest')` block (alongside `startOvertakeWatch`), tears down on game-over (both branches in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)), on mode switch (init's else branch), and on `hideContestScreens()` (so navigating to leaderboard via the HUD itself doesn't leave a stale floating widget). Cache buster `v20260521g`, SW `bloom-v4.6`.
- вЬЕ **Smart contest leaderboard (May 2026)** вАФ the contest board ([src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js)) used to render every participant in a flat scroll-wall; with 50+ players that meant "where do I stand?" was lost in noise and the most-addictive comparisons (just above/below me) were invisible without scrolling. New layout, gated by player count:
  - **вЙ§ 12 players** вАФ flat list, unchanged (no value from sectioning small contests).
  - **> 12 players (compact view, default)** вАФ `рЯПЖ „Ф„Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь„Щ„Э` section with top 5, then if I'm rank вЙ•6 a `рЯУН „Ф„Ю„Щ„І„Х„Э „©„Ь„Ъ ¬Ј #N „Ю„™„Х„Ъ M` section with me + 2 neighbors above and 2 below, separated by a `¬Ј ¬Ј ¬Ј` divider. Bottom CTA: `„Ф„¶„Т „Р„™ „Ы„Ь N „Ф„©„Ч„І„†„Щ„Э` (gold-on-black gradient pill).
  - **Expanded view** вАФ every row shown flat. If `> 20` players a search input also appears (`„Ч„Щ„§„Х„© „Ь„§„Щ „©„ЭвА¶`, 140ms debounced; focus + caret preserved across the 20s silent refresh so typing isn't eaten). Top-of-list `вМГ „Ч„Ц„®„Ф „Ь„™„¶„Х„Т„Ф „І„Х„Ю„§„І„Ш„Щ„™` to fold back. Expand scrolls MY row to viewport center.
  - **Top-3 podium** вАФ `рЯ•З рЯ•И рЯ•Й` medal glyphs in the rank circle (instead of digits), plus subtle silver/bronze background tints on rows 2/3 to match the existing gold on row 1.
  - **Persistent "next target" pill** вАФ under MY row, a pulsing gold pill: `вЪФпЄП „Ґ„Х„У 1,234 „Ы„У„Щ „Ь„Ґ„І„Х„£ „Р„™ [name]`. The most-addictive moment in any leaderboard is "I can take them in one game" вАФ this is now ambient rather than waiting for the periodic `refreshOvertake` poll to fire a transient banner.
  - **Search smart-ranking** вАФ filtered rows keep their real contest rank (mapped via `players.indexOf`) so a search for "„У„†„Щ" doesn't collapse the matches to "1, 2, 3" and lose context.
  Architecture: `renderContestSmartBoard(players)` is the single entry point now used by both `showContestLeaderboard` (mount) and `refreshContestBoardSilently` (every 20s tick). Row-level `renderContestBoardRows(players, allPlayers, startIdx)` got a new signature: `allPlayers` keeps leader-relative deltas correct on slices, and `startIdx` keeps rank numbers truthful. Module-level state (`contestBoardExpanded`, `contestBoardSearchTerm`) resets on each mount so a stale search from a previous contest visit can't filter the new list to "no results". New CSS in [public/css/screens.css](public/css/screens.css) + dark-mode overrides in [public/css/dark.css](public/css/dark.css). Cache buster `v20260521f`, SW `bloom-v4.5`.
- вЬЕ **One-tap duel rematch (May 2026)** вАФ every terminal-state row in the "„Ф„У„Х-„І„®„С„Х„™ „©„Ь„Щ" list inside the duel modal now carries a gold `вЪФпЄП „©„Х„С` button that re-opens the duel modal pre-filled with the opponent's 4-char BLOOM suffix. Closes the loop: a finished duel вЖТ 1 tap вЖТ ready to send a fresh challenge with the difficulty/wager re-chosen. Implemented in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) `loadMyDuels` (gates on `status вИИ {settled, tie, declined, expired}` so in-progress rows still show their existing accept/play/decline buttons) + new `window.rematchDuel(suffix)` global that closes the current duel modal and calls `showDuelModal({prefillSuffix})`. The flex row layout was tightened (`display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;flex-wrap:wrap`) so the rematch pill doesn't push other actions off the right edge on narrow phones. Retention rationale: the duels list is effectively your personal opponent leaderboard вАФ surfacing a one-tap rematch turns it into the closest thing BLOOM has to a "play again with the same person" loop, which is the most addictive social pattern in multiplayer casual games. Cache buster `v20260521e`, SW `bloom-v4.4`.
- вЬЕ **Duel score visibility fix (May 2026)** вАФ user-reported bug: when finishing a duel as the SECOND player (so the duel settled immediately on the server), the result overlay rendered "vs ..." instead of the opponent's actual score. Root cause: `POST /api/duels/:id/score` settle path returned only `{ok, result, winner, prize}` вАФ `opponentScore` was missing, so the client's `(d && d.opponentScore) ? ... : '...'` fell through. The polling path (`pollDuelUntilSettled` вАФ only used when *I* finished first) already passed `opponentScore`, which is why this only repro'd as a second-player. Fix in [server.js](server.js) `POST /api/duels/:id/score`: settled + tie responses now also include `yourScore: s, opponentScore: isChallenger ? u.opponent_score : u.challenger_score`. Same-batch hardening in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js): (a) overlay's `oppScore` guard switched from truthy `?:` to `!= null` so a legitimate opponent score of 0 still renders; (b) the duel notification banner (cross-session "you won/lost" surfacing in `showDuelNotificationBanner`) now appends `¬Ј 77,445 vs 60,000` to the sub-line; (c) "my duels" list rows (`loadMyDuels`) now render the full score-vs-score on every settled/tie row, not just "„†„Щ„¶„Ч„™!/„Ф„§„°„У„™". Cache buster `v20260521d`, SW `bloom-v4.3`.
- вЬЕ **Duel/event UX fixes (May 2026)** вАФ four user-reported bugs addressed in one batch:
  1. **Explosion FX invisible/delayed**: `triggerBomb` / `triggerFreeze` used to set `cell.style.background` for a 400ms flash, but `render()` ran immediately after with `gridEl.innerHTML = ''` вАФ wiping the inline style before paint. New approach: `fxAtCell()` spawns a `position:fixed` overlay in `<body>` (`.fx-overlay.fx-explode`, `.fx-overlay.fx-freeze`) that lives independently of the grid DOM. Bomb explosions stagger outward from the center (distance √Ч 55ms delay) to read as a real blast. **Plus**: `triggerEvent()` now fires BEFORE `processChains()` in `drop()` вАФ previously a long chain pushed the explosion 1-2s late.
  2. **No notifications for incoming duels**: New `checkIncomingDuels()` in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) polls `/api/duels/mine` on boot + every 60s + on `visibilitychange`. Shows a top-of-screen banner (`showDuelNotificationBanner`) for: (a) pending duels where I'm the opponent, (b) settled duels with results I haven't seen. De-duped per session via `sessionStorage[bloom_seen_duel_notifications]`. Tap вЖТ opens duel modal.
  3. **Challenger had to refresh to play**: `POST /api/duels` now returns the full duel row, and the client auto-calls `startDuelGame()` 600ms after creation (no more waiting for the opponent). Server-side, `POST /api/duels/:id/score` now accepts submissions while status is `'pending'` OR `'accepted'` вАФ settlement triggers as soon as both scores exist regardless of accept order.
  4. **Opponent score never shown on game-over**: `submitDuelScore` checks for `result === 'waiting'` and starts `pollDuelUntilSettled()` (5s interval, 5 min cap). On settle/tie, `replaceDuelResultOverlay()` swaps the in-flight overlay (tagged `data-duel-result-overlay`) for the final result with the opponent's real score. New `GET /api/duels/:id` endpoint backs this polling.
- вЬЕ **Player-chosen difficulty per game mode** вАФ five presets (`default`/`easy`/`medium`/`hard`/`insane`) selectable by:
  - **Friends contest**: host picks at creation. Stored on `contests` row (`difficulty_label` / `difficulty_weights` / `difficulty_speed_pct`), inherited by everyone who joins. Form pill in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js).
  - **1v1 duel**: challenger picks. Stored on `duels` row (same 3 columns). Both players get the same setting. Pill picker in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js).
  - **Practice**: player picks for themselves. Stored in `localStorage[bloom_practice_difficulty]`. Inline chip in the mode-bar subtitle (`practice-diff-chip`) opens a modal.
  - **Daily**: NOT player-selectable вАФ admin-only (fairness). Practice scores ALSO STOP submitting to the daily leaderboard when difficulty != default (or when running a duel). Check: `practiceFairForLeaderboard = (mode === 'practice') && !sessionDifficulty && !window._duelMode` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js).
  - Server-side single source of truth: `DIFFICULTY_PRESETS` + `resolveDifficulty(label)` in [server.js](server.js). Frontend mirror in [src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) (for label/emoji/name display only). The presets are snapshotted onto each contest/duel row at creation, so changing the preset table later never re-balances live contests.
  - Engine integration: `sessionDifficulty` is reset on every `init()` and populated based on mode (practice from localStorage, contest from `activeContestData.*`, duel from the duel row passed into `startDuelGame`). `getDropWeights()` and `gameSpeedScale()` check `sessionDifficulty` BEFORE the admin global `gameConfig`. Daily stays uniform because its `init()` branch never touches `sessionDifficulty`.
- вЬЕ **Admin difficulty / speed / slot machine controls** вАФ three new tunables in `game_config`. **Drop pool**: `drop_weights` is a comma-separated list of 8 weights (tiers 1..8). The frontend `WEIGHTS` constant is fallback-only; `getDropWeights()` reads from `gameConfig.drop_weights`. All-zero falls back to default. Admin section ships with 5 presets (default 55/28/12/5/0/0/0/0, easy, medium, hard, insane) + 8 sliders with live `%` calculation. **Game speed**: `game_speed_pct` (50-200) multiplies every gameplay sleep via `gsleep(ms)` wrapping `sleep()` in `src/11-game.js`. **Slot machine**: `slot_enabled` / `slot_duration_ms` (200-2000) / `slot_intensity` (1-8) replace the old 4-tier sweep in `revealNextTier`. Default: 3 passes through tiers 1..8 over 650ms with ease-in-quad deceleration + 380ms bounce-up landing animation (`.tier-cell.slot-landed` keyframes in [public/css/base.css](public/css/base.css)). Cost-aware via `revealToken` bail-out for fast tappers.
- вЬЕ **Layout regression fix + engine self-test (May 2026)** вАФ practice-mode subtitle ("„С„®„Щ„®„™ „Ю„Ч„У„Ь вМД ¬Ј „™„™„Ч„®„Ф „Ґ„Ь „Ь„Х„Ч „Ф„Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь„Щ„Э рЯПЖ") was wrapping to two lines on narrow phones, inflating the mode-bar height by ~14px. `fitGrid()` in [src/06-contests.js](src/06-contests.js#L1059) is height-bound on tall-narrow viewports, so every lost pixel translates to ~1px off each cell √Ч all 6 rows вАФ users saw smaller board cells AND smaller tier-bar tiles (the tier-bar shares fitGrid's width budget). Two fixes: (1) compacted the subtitle to a single line by replacing the long "„™„™„Ч„®„Ф „Ґ„Ь „Ь„Х„Ч „Ф„Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь„Щ„Э рЯПЖ" sentence with a small рЯПЖ (or вКШ when difficulty != default) icon next to the chip вАФ tooltip on hover keeps the full meaning accessible; (2) added `white-space: nowrap; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis;` to `.mode-title` and `.mode-sub` in [public/css/home.css](public/css/home.css) so future copy can't silently re-trigger the bug. Added engine diagnostics: `?debug=1` URL param turns on `[drop]`/`[merge]`/`[gravity]` console logs with compact `serializeGrid()` snapshots; `__bloomDumpGrid()` and `__bloomLayoutLog` are exposed for one-off devtools queries; `[fitGrid]` is logged on every render (cell px, width/height-bound, mode-bar height, viewport). Built [scripts/test_engine.mjs](scripts/test_engine.mjs) вАФ runs 500 games √Ч 100 drops asserting the gravity invariant after every step. Found a backwards invariant in v1; corrected v2 passes 41,242 drops / 26,557 merges / 16 crown tiles / 0 floating-tile bugs. Cache buster bumped to `v20260517q`.
- вЬЕ **Bot mode expansion + admin leaderboard surgery (May 2026)** вАФ three coordinated changes:
  1. **Bots now play every mode**: [bot-engine.js](bot-engine.js) accepts `mode: 'duel'` and `mode: 'challenge'` in addition to the existing practice/daily/contest. Duel mode pairs finishing bots into real rows in the `duels` table (challenger/opponent both bots, status 'settled' or 'tie', synthetic `opponent_code` like `BOT-XXXX`). Challenge mode resolves the admin-provided slug вЖТ `challenges.id`, then INSERTs a `completed` row into `challenge_entries` with a score-derived `drops_count` so the cheat heuristic doesn't auto-flag. The pre-existing `daily_scores` INSERT was broken (used non-existent `display_name`/`highest_tier`/`games_played`/`drops_count` columns) вАФ fixed to use the real schema `(date, device_id, name, score, tier)`. Every bot already heartbeats every 5s with `grid_json` so they're spectatable via `/?watch=DEVICE_ID` and visible in admin live view.
  2. **Per-row leaderboard deletion**: new admin endpoints `DELETE /api/score/:date/:deviceId` (daily_scores вЖТ cascades through day/week/month leaderboard windows) and `DELETE /api/contest-score/:code/:deviceId` (contest_scores + contest_live_state). Wired with рЯЧС buttons in the "„†„Щ„І„Х„У„Щ„Э „Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь„Щ„Э" table and a new "рЯСБ „Ф„¶„Т „Ч„С„®„Щ„Э" expander on every contest row that shows full member list with per-entry deletes. Helper endpoint `GET /api/contest/:code/scores` returns up to 200 contest members. Every delete writes to `admin_actions` audit log.
  3. **Version visibility + live bot panel**: new admin endpoint `GET /api/version` reads the cache-buster from `public/index.html`, plus `RAILWAY_GIT_COMMIT_SHA`, node version, and uptime. Surfaced in the header as a monospace `build vXXXX ¬Ј gitsha ¬Ј вЖСuptime` pill. The bot status panel now shows ALL active bots (not just 8) in a scrollable list with name/tier/games/score, auto-refreshing every 3s, with a toggleable auto-refresh checkbox. Cache buster bumped to `v20260517p`.
- вЬЕ **Duel live spectator (May 2026)** вАФ when a player finishes a duel before their opponent, the "„Ю„Ю„™„Щ„Я „Ь„Щ„®„Щ„С" overlay used to show a static spinner with no insight into the opponent. Now `submitDuelScore()` in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js), upon a `result: 'waiting'` response, calls `attachDuelLiveSpectator(duelId, myScore, oppName)` which: (1) GETs `/api/duels/:id` to learn the opponent's device ID, (2) injects a mini live-board widget (`[data-duel-spec-widget]`) into the waiting overlay showing the opponent's name, real-time score, and actual grid using `getActiveTiers()` SVGs, (3) polls `/api/live-state/:opponentDeviceId` (universal endpoint backed by 5s `/api/heartbeat` snapshots) every 1.5s. Self-terminates when the widget DOM is removed (player dismissed overlay) or the duel poller resolves to settled/tie. Settle-poll cadence also tightened from 5sвЖТ2s (still 5-min total cap) so the final result lands faster. Cache buster bumped to `v20260517o`. Not a mirror вАФ the opponent's *actual* live game state.
- вЬЕ **Audio recovery fix (May 2026)** вАФ players who had ever tapped the legacy unified mute button (`bloom_muted=1`) on a pre-volume-slider version were stuck silent forever: `readVolumeKey` in [src/03-audio.js](src/03-audio.js) treated the legacy flag as authoritative and migrated *both* channels to volume=0. New behavior: only the per-channel legacy keys (`bloom_muted_music`/`bloom_muted_sfx`) are honored on migration; the unified `bloom_muted` is intentionally ignored. After read, the resolved volumes are immediately persisted to the new keys and all legacy keys are cleared so migration runs exactly once. Also fixed: `ensureAudio()` now re-arms `currentTrack` inside the `resume().then(...)` callback (Safari leaves pre-gesture BufferSources scheduled but silent), and a one-shot `pointerdown`/`touchstart`/`keydown` capture-phase listener calls `ensureAudio()` unconditionally on the very first user gesture as a belt-and-suspenders unlock. Cache buster bumped to `v20260517n`.
- вЬЕ **Admin bonus simulator** вАФ new section in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) "рЯОБ „°„Щ„Ю„Х„Ь„Ш„Х„® „С„Х„†„Х„°„Щ„Э" that visually previews every in-game event (рЯТ£ bomb, в≠Р star, рЯОБ gift, рЯФ• fever, вЭДпЄП freeze, рЯОѓ target). Admin clicks a bonus вЖТ it animates on a 4√Ч6 mock board with the same `fx-explode`/`fx-freeze` overlays, banners, confetti, fever bar, and target-glow used in the real game. Self-contained client-side IIFE (no server calls, no DB writes). Mirrors the default values from [src/14-events.js](src/14-events.js) (bomb +2000/tile, star +500, gift 5-50рЯТО / 5% jackpot 500рЯТО, fever √Ч3, freeze +1000, target √Ч5). A persistent gold "„Ш„Щ„§ „Ь„©„Щ„Ю„Х„©" card above the list explains the section's purpose, and the tip pane below the board updates per-bonus with the relevant config keys (`event_bomb_radius`, `event_fever_weight`, etc.) so admins know what to tune in "„Ф„Т„У„®„Х„™ „Ю„©„Ч„І". Uses `TIPS.bonus_sim` for the `?` tooltip.
- вЬЕ **Scope √Ч time leaderboard (v2, May 2026)** вАФ the day/week/month tabs are now the *secondary* axis. Primary axis is scope: **рЯМН „Ґ„Х„Ь„Ю„Щ / рЯЗЃрЯЗ± „Ю„У„Щ„†„™„Щ / рЯОЪпЄП „І„Х„©„Щ**. Admin controls which scopes appear via `game_config.leaderboard_tabs_enabled` (CSV preserving order; default `"world,country,difficulty"`), plus `leaderboard_default_tab` and `leaderboard_default_difficulty`. Players pick a flag once via a 4-column country-picker modal (`promptForCountry` in [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js)) that chains after `promptForName` on first home view, with a "„Ф„Ч„Ь„£ „У„Т„Ь" affordance inside the leaderboard modal for returning users. Country list is a hardcoded Hebrew-labeled set in [src/07-identity.js](src/07-identity.js) `COUNTRY_LIST` (~55 ISO-3166 alpha-2 codes) вАФ `flagEmoji(cc)` derives the flag glyph from regional-indicator codepoints, so adding a country needs no asset work. Stored in `localStorage[bloom_country]` + `player_profiles.country` (new column) + mirrored onto every `daily_scores`/`difficulty_scores` row at submission time. Difficulty board reads from a new `difficulty_scores` table (PK `date+device_id+difficulty_label`, same "best score wins" upsert + day/week/month windowing as `daily_scores`); practice + duel modes write here via [src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `submitPracticeOrDuelScore()` вАФ called from both the chain-continuation and the regular game-over branches. Daily mode is **explicitly excluded** from the difficulty board (admin-controlled fairness вАФ daily seed is uniform). New endpoints: `GET /api/leaderboard/v2?scope=world|country|difficulty&period=day|week|month&difficulty=...&endDate=...&deviceId=...&country=...` (returns `{ list, total, rank, from, to, period, scope, country, difficulty, needsCountry }`), `POST /api/profile/country` (idempotent), `POST /api/score/practice` (with anti-cheat drops-implausibility check matching `/api/score`). Old `/api/leaderboard/range/:period` stays in place for back-compat. New CSS section in [public/css/home.css](public/css/home.css) for `.country-grid` + compact `.lb-period-tabs`/`.lb-diff-tabs` pills + `.lb-flag` inline glyph. Admin section "рЯПЖ „Ш„С„Ь„Р„Х„™ „Ю„Х„С„Щ„Ь„Щ„Э" in [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) вАФ checkbox-per-tab with вЖСвЖУ reorder, default-tab + default-difficulty dropdowns. Cache buster bumped to `v20260518b`.
- вЬЕ **Identity + invite UX (May 2026)** вАФ addressed two long-standing pain points around player identity:
  1. **Admin dedup fix**: there were **two duplicate `adminRouter.get('/api/players', ...)` definitions** in [server.js](server.js). Express only ever served the first, which `SELECT`ed from `daily_scores` and had no `player_code` column вАФ so admins saw two "„У„†„Щ„Р„Ь" rows with no way to tell them apart. Deleted the dead second route; rewrote the active one to LEFT JOIN `player_profiles` and return `player_code`, profile `display_name`, and `country`. Admin search `?q=` now matches on `player_code` too. [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) `loadPlayers()` table now leads with a monospace `BLOOM-XXXX` column + country flag next to the name. Local `flagEmoji(cc)` helper added in admin (regional-indicator codepoint math, no asset work).
  2. **Easier 1v1 invite**: duel modal in [src/02-shop.js](src/02-shop.js) used to require typing the full `BLOOM-XXXX`. Now the input is split вАФ fixed `BLOOM-` prefix pill (dark, gold text, matches difficulty pills) + 4-char suffix input restricted to the same `A-HJ-NP-Z2-9` alphabet as `generatePlayerCode`. Paste is normalized: `BLOOM-WXYZ` / `bloom-wxyz` / `WXYZ` all become `WXYZ` automatically. A new "„Ф„І„Х„У „©„Ь„Щ: BLOOM-XXXX рЯУЛ" pill at the top of the modal lets a player copy their own code and send it to a friend who will challenge them back.
  3. **Challenge from leaderboard**: in the v2 leaderboard modal ([src/11-game.js](src/11-game.js) `renderLbModalBody`), every row whose player has a known BLOOM code now renders a small `вЪФпЄП` button and becomes clickable. Tapping closes the modal and reopens the duel modal with the suffix pre-filled (`showDuelModal({ prefillSuffix })`). The codes ride along on each row via a new `LEFT JOIN player_profiles pp ON pp.device_id = best.device_id` inside `/api/leaderboard/v2`.
  4. **Name editing from home**: the home pid pill now shows the player's display name next to their BLOOM code with a `вЬПпЄП` button. Clicking opens `promptForName(cb, { edit: true })` вАФ a new mode that pre-fills the current name, swaps the title/copy to "„Ґ„®„Щ„Ы„™ „©„Э", and skips the country-picker chain. Save persists to `localStorage[NAME_KEY]` AND fires `POST /api/profile/name` (new endpoint, 10/hr rate-limit) so the change shows up in admin / leaderboards / duels instantly.
  5. **Auto-sync `display_name` on daily submit**: `POST /api/score` now runs `UPDATE player_profiles SET display_name = $1 WHERE device_id = $2 AND (display_name IS NULL OR display_name <> $1)` right after the `daily_scores` upsert. Guarantees the canonical profile name stays aligned with whatever the player picked on the leaderboard, with no extra round-trip from the client. Cache buster bumped to `v20260518e`, SW `CACHE_NAME` to `bloom-v3.6`.
- вЬЕ **BLOOM Challenges** вАФ public single-shot prize contests. Four types (`race`, `top_n`, `beat`, `first_to_tier`), admin picks at creation. PK on `(challenge_id, device_id)` enforces "single attempt" at the DB layer. Score-only-grows guard on `/score` heartbeat. Winner slots assigned eagerly under `SELECT FOR UPDATE` for race/first-to-tier (race-safe), on `/complete` for `beat`, on admin `/finalize` for `top_n`. Cheat-flag heuristics: z-score > 3ѕГ AND drops-vs-score sanity table. Frontend mode `'challenge'` (4th mode tab "„Р„™„Т„®„Щ„Э"): no save/load, no reset button, `beforeunload` warning, prize chip floats over the grid, custom result screen with in-line winner contact form. Admin section "„Р„™„Т„®„Щ„Э" вАФ full CRUD with lock-down once entries exist + starts_at passed (only safe fields editable). Helpers added: `cleanSlug`, `challengeDropsImplausible`, `challengeZScore`, `maybeGrabWinnerSlot`. New rate-limit buckets: `challenge:enter` (5/hr), `challenge:score` (600/hr), `challenge:claim` (5/hr).
- вЬЕ **Admin dashboard вАФ tabbed UX + per-field tooltips (May 2026)** вАФ [admin/index.html](admin/index.html) previously ran 20 sections as one ~3,135-line scroll. Refactored into a sticky **6-tab navigation** at the top: `рЯУК „У„©„С„Х„®„У` (KPIs + DAU + funnel + retention + heatmap), `рЯОЃ „Ю„©„Ч„І` (config / difficulty / LB tabs / bonus simulator), `рЯТ∞ „Ы„Ь„Ы„Ь„Ф` (AdSense / Stripe / diamonds / wager / jackpot), `рЯС• „©„Ч„І„†„Щ„Э` (gift, bots, top scores, players list), `рЯПЖ „™„Ч„®„Х„Щ„Х„™` (contests + challenges), `рЯФІ „†„Щ„Ш„Х„®` (admin guide + live + audit + CSV). DOM order is preserved вАФ each `<section>` is wrapped in `<div class="admin-tab-panel" data-tab="X">` and toggled with `display`. `switchAdminTab()` persists the choice in `localStorage[bloom_admin_active_tab]` and closes any open tooltip. **Per-control tooltips**: the existing `showTip()` system was extended with a new `data-tip-text="HTML"` attribute (in addition to the existing `data-tip="KEY"` lookup) вАФ every save button, slider, toggle, and form field gets its own inline `?` with a focused Hebrew explanation (50 occurrences total). The 42-key game-config table gained a tooltip column backed by a new `TIPS_PER_KEY` dictionary covering every event/shake/wager/referral/diamond/pricing key. `wireTips()` is re-invoked after the config table renders so the new buttons get wired. No backend changes вАФ all existing PATCH `/config/:key` and other endpoints work unchanged; `display:none` keeps hidden panels in the DOM so `getElementById` and `refreshAll()` continue to operate on every section regardless of which tab is active.

---

## 6. What was rolled back (do not assume these exist)

In commit `4fb5972` (Roll back to initial daily-challenge game, layered with sound system), the following were **removed** from the current build:

- вЭМ Welcome splash / persistent home screen with logo + slogan
- вЭМ 6-step interactive tutorial (board intro, first drop, first merge, multi-merge demo, chain, full path to Crown)
- вЭМ Background MP3 music (`bloom-music.mp3`) вАФ the file is no longer referenced and the music loop is gone; only synth SFX remain
- вЭМ Pre-reset confirmation prompts

`ROADMAP_1.md` still describes these as "shipped" вАФ that doc is **stale**. Trust the code, not the roadmap.
